# Legacy Deck History & Variant Index

> **See also**: [Legacy Basics](legacy-basics.md) | [Meta Analysis](legacy-analysis.md) | [Deckbuilding Guide](deckbuilding-guide.md) | [Archetype Guide](archetype-guide.md) | [MTG Slang](mtg-slang.md)

## Metadata

- **Format:** Legacy
- **Last Updated:** 2026-04-06
- **Data Sources:** mtggoldfish.com, mtgtop8.com, mtgdecks.net
- **Sample Size (Decks):** 1,564
- **Sample Size (Matches):** 35,000
- **Total Entries:** 6,433
- **Distinct Archetypes:** 54
- **Post-Ban:** [Entomb](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Entomb%22) (November 2025)
- **Notes:** Format considered healthy per March 2026 B&R announcement. No changes. Energy cards from Modern Horizons 3 have created viable non-blue aggro strategies. Dimir Tempo is the clear best deck but not oppressively so.

---

## Dimir Tempo

**Also known as:** UB Tempo, Dimir Shadow, UB Scam

**Archetype:** tempo
**Colors:** U, B
**Tier:** tier 1
**Meta Share:** 14.6%
**Win Rate Estimate:** 52-53%
**Cost Estimate:** $3,800 (driven by [Underground Sea](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Underground+Sea%22), [Force of Will](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Force+of+Will%22), [Wasteland](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Wasteland%22), [Polluted Delta](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Polluted+Delta%22))
**First Appeared:** 2023
**Peak Meta Share:** 2025-2026
**Deck Count in Sample:** 228

The format's premier tempo deck, leveraging the power of [Orcish Bowmasters](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Orcish+Bowmasters%22), efficient black disruption, and blue card selection. Combines [Brainstorm](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Brainstorm%22)/[Ponder](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Ponder%22) with [Thoughtseize](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Thoughtseize%22) and cheap threats like [Tamiyo, Inquisitive Student](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Tamiyo%2C+Inquisitive+Student%22) and [Murktide Regent](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Murktide+Regent%22) to apply pressure while denying the opponent resources. The most played deck in Legacy by a wide margin.

### Decklist

**Main Deck:**

- 4 [Brainstorm](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Brainstorm%22)
- 4 [Ponder](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Ponder%22)
- 4 [Force of Will](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Force+of+Will%22)
- 4 [Daze](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Daze%22)
- 3 [Thoughtseize](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Thoughtseize%22)
- 3 [Fatal Push](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Fatal+Push%22)
- 2 [Spell Pierce](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Spell+Pierce%22)
- 1 [Snuff Out](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Snuff+Out%22)
- 4 [Tamiyo, Inquisitive Student](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Tamiyo%2C+Inquisitive+Student%22)
- 4 [Orcish Bowmasters](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Orcish+Bowmasters%22)
- 3 [Murktide Regent](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Murktide+Regent%22)
- 4 [Barrowgoyf](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Barrowgoyf%22)
- 4 [Polluted Delta](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Polluted+Delta%22)
- 3 [Misty Rainforest](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Misty+Rainforest%22)
- 2 [Scalding Tarn](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Scalding+Tarn%22)
- 4 [Underground Sea](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Underground+Sea%22)
- 1 [Watery Grave](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Watery+Grave%22)
- 4 [Wasteland](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Wasteland%22)
- 1 [Island](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Island%22)
- 1 [Swamp](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Swamp%22)

**Sideboard:**

- 2 [Surgical Extraction](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Surgical+Extraction%22)
- 2 [Hydroblast](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Hydroblast%22)
- 1 [Force of Negation](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Force+of+Negation%22)
- 1 [Dismember](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Dismember%22)
- 1 [Sheoldred's Edict](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Sheoldred%27s+Edict%22)
- 2 [Plague Engineer](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Plague+Engineer%22)
- 1 [Subtlety](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Subtlety%22)
- 1 [Stern Scolding](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Stern+Scolding%22)
- 1 [Nihil Spellbomb](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Nihil+Spellbomb%22)
- 2 [Flusterstorm](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Flusterstorm%22)
- 1 [Massacre](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Massacre%22)

### Key Matchups

- **Favorable:** Sneak and Show, Beanstalk Control, Jeskai Control, [Doomsday](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Doomsday%22)
- **Unfavorable:** [Ocelot Pride](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Ocelot+Pride%22) Midrange, Lands, Eldrazi
- **Even:** Izzet Delver, Painter, The EPIC Storm

**Similar Decks:** Izzet Delver, Sultai Tempo, [Death's Shadow](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Death%27s+Shadow%22)
Shares the [Brainstorm](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Brainstorm%22)/[Ponder](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Ponder%22)/[Force of Will](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Force+of+Will%22)/[Daze](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Daze%22) shell with Izzet Delver but trades red removal for black disruption. Sultai Tempo adds green for Uro. [Death's Shadow](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Death%27s+Shadow%22) is a more aggressive variant of the same UB core.

### Key Cards Explained

<img src="https://api.scryfall.com/cards/named?exact=Orcish+Bowmasters&format=image&version=normal&set=ltr" alt="Orcish Bowmasters" width="217"> <img src="https://api.scryfall.com/cards/named?exact=Tamiyo%2C+Inquisitive+Student&format=image&version=normal&set=dsk" alt="Tamiyo, Inquisitive Student" width="217"> <img src="https://api.scryfall.com/cards/named?exact=Murktide+Regent&format=image&version=normal&set=mh2" alt="Murktide Regent" width="217">

- **Orcish Bowmasters:** Premier creature in the format. Punishes [Brainstorm](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Brainstorm%22), provides removal, and creates a growing threat. Core to why black is the best color in Legacy.
- **Tamiyo, Inquisitive Student:** Efficient one-drop that flips into a planeswalker generating card advantage. Replaced [Delver of Secrets](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Delver+of+Secrets%22) in many UB lists.
- **Murktide Regent:** Large delve threat that comes down for UU and dominates combat. Fueled by the many instants and sorceries in the deck.
- **Barrowgoyf:** MH3 [Tarmogoyf](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Tarmogoyf%22) variant that is even more efficient in a format full of diverse card types in graveyards.
- **Daze:** Free countermagic that punishes opponents for tapping out early, enabling the tempo gameplan.

### Historical Timeline

**2023** (tier 2, ~5%)
Deck emerges after [Orcish Bowmasters](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Orcish+Bowmasters%22) printed in Lord of the Rings (June). Black overtakes red as the partner color for blue tempo shells. Early UB Scam lists use [Grief](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Grief%22) for free disruption.
- [Orcish Bowmasters](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Orcish+Bowmasters%22) as core creature
- [Grief](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Grief%22) + [Reanimate](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Reanimate%22) package
- [Thoughtseize](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Thoughtseize%22) main over [Lightning Bolt](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Lightning+Bolt%22)

**2024** (tier 1, ~10%)
MH3 adds [Tamiyo, Inquisitive Student](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Tamiyo%2C+Inquisitive+Student%22) and [Barrowgoyf](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Barrowgoyf%22), cementing UB as the best Delver/tempo shell. Tamiyo replaces [Delver of Secrets](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Delver+of+Secrets%22). Deck overtakes Izzet Delver in metagame share.
- [Tamiyo, Inquisitive Student](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Tamiyo%2C+Inquisitive+Student%22) replaces [Delver of Secrets](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Delver+of+Secrets%22)
- [Barrowgoyf](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Barrowgoyf%22) added as efficient threat
- [Grief](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Grief%22) potentially banned mid-year

**2025** (tier 1, ~13%)
[Entomb](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Entomb%22) ban removes Reanimator from tier 1, and Dimir Tempo benefits from less combo in the meta. Becomes the most-played deck in Legacy by a wide margin.
- Refined sideboard for post-[Entomb](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Entomb%22)-ban meta
- [Murktide Regent](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Murktide+Regent%22) as top-end finisher solidified

**2026** (tier 1, ~14.6%)
Continues as the format's best deck at 14.6% meta share. No changes in March B&R. Lists are highly optimized with small flex slot variations week to week.
- Stable core
- Flex between [Fatal Push](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Fatal+Push%22), [Snuff Out](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Snuff+Out%22), [Spell Pierce](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Spell+Pierce%22) counts

### Bans Impact

- **Expressive Iteration** (2023-03): Removed the Izzet version's best card advantage engine, helping push players toward Dimir for Bowmasters.

**Frequency of Change:** medium
**Change Notes:** Card choices flex between [Fatal Push](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Fatal+Push%22), [Snuff Out](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Snuff+Out%22), and [Dismember](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Dismember%22) based on metagame. Sideboard heavily tuned week to week. [Barrowgoyf](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Barrowgoyf%22) from MH3 was a major addition in 2024.

---

## Ocelot Pride Midrange

**Also known as:** Energy Midrange, Naya Energy, Cat Midrange

**Archetype:** midrange
**Colors:** W, G, R
**Tier:** tier 1
**Meta Share:** 8.5%
**Win Rate Estimate:** 51-53%
**Cost Estimate:** $2,200 (driven by [Savannah](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Savannah%22), [Plateau](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Plateau%22), [Wasteland](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Wasteland%22), [Urza's Saga](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Urza%27s+Saga%22))
**First Appeared:** 2024
**Peak Meta Share:** 2025-2026
**Deck Count in Sample:** 133

An energy-based midrange deck built around [Ocelot Pride](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Ocelot+Pride%22), [Guide of Souls](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Guide+of+Souls%22), and [Amped Raptor](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Amped+Raptor%22). Represents the most successful non-blue aggressive strategy in Legacy, using efficient energy creatures and [Swords to Plowshares](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Swords+to+Plowshares%22) for interaction. The deck pressures blue combo and control while going over the top of other creature decks with token generation.

### Decklist

**Main Deck:**

- 4 [Ocelot Pride](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Ocelot+Pride%22)
- 4 [Guide of Souls](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Guide+of+Souls%22)
- 4 [Amped Raptor](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Amped+Raptor%22)
- 3 [Ajani, Nacatl Pariah](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Ajani%2C+Nacatl+Pariah%22)
- 2 [Phlage, Titan of Fire's Fury](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Phlage%2C+Titan+of+Fire%27s+Fury%22)
- 4 [Galvanic Discharge](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Galvanic+Discharge%22)
- 4 [Swords to Plowshares](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Swords+to+Plowshares%22)
- 3 [Green Sun's Zenith](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Green+Sun%27s+Zenith%22)
- 1 [Dryad Arbor](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Dryad+Arbor%22)
- 2 [Sylvan Library](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Sylvan+Library%22)
- 3 [Urza's Saga](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Urza%27s+Saga%22)
- 4 [Windswept Heath](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Windswept+Heath%22)
- 4 [Wooded Foothills](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Wooded+Foothills%22)
- 2 [Arid Mesa](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Arid+Mesa%22)
- 3 [Savannah](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Savannah%22)
- 2 [Plateau](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Plateau%22)
- 1 [Taiga](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Taiga%22)
- 1 [Forest](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Forest%22)
- 1 [Plains](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Plains%22)
- 3 [Wasteland](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Wasteland%22)
- 1 [Boseiju, Who Endures](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Boseiju%2C+Who+Endures%22)
- 3 [Endurance](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Endurance%22)
- 1 [Collector Ouphe](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Collector+Ouphe%22)

**Sideboard:**

- 2 [Mindbreak Trap](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Mindbreak+Trap%22)
- 2 [Torpor Orb](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Torpor+Orb%22)
- 2 [Chalice of the Void](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Chalice+of+the+Void%22)
- 2 [Red Elemental Blast](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Red+Elemental+Blast%22)
- 2 [Force of Vigor](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Force+of+Vigor%22)
- 1 [Choke](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Choke%22)
- 2 [Containment Priest](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Containment+Priest%22)
- 1 [Haywire Mite](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Haywire+Mite%22)
- 1 [Pithing Needle](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Pithing+Needle%22)

### Key Matchups

- **Favorable:** Dimir Tempo, Izzet Delver, Jeskai Control
- **Unfavorable:** Sneak and Show, Oops! All Spells, [Doomsday](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Doomsday%22)
- **Even:** Lands, Painter, Death and Taxes

**Similar Decks:** Maverick, Cradle Control
Shares the green creature toolbox approach of Maverick but eschews the [Knight of the Reliquary](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Knight+of+the+Reliquary%22) package for energy threats. Uses a similar [Green Sun's Zenith](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Green+Sun%27s+Zenith%22) shell.

### Key Cards Explained

<img src="https://api.scryfall.com/cards/named?exact=Ocelot+Pride&format=image&version=normal&set=mh3" alt="Ocelot Pride" width="217"> <img src="https://api.scryfall.com/cards/named?exact=Guide+of+Souls&format=image&version=normal&set=mh3" alt="Guide of Souls" width="217"> <img src="https://api.scryfall.com/cards/named?exact=Amped+Raptor&format=image&version=normal&set=mh3" alt="Amped Raptor" width="217">

- **Ocelot Pride:** One-mana 1/1 with lifelink that creates cat tokens whenever you gain life and deal combat damage. Generates massive board presence.
- **Guide of Souls:** Energy-generating creature that makes tokens fly temporarily, enabling evasive damage for [Ocelot Pride](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Ocelot+Pride%22) triggers.
- **Amped Raptor:** Energy creature with cascade for MV equal to energy spent, providing card advantage in a creature shell.
- **Galvanic Discharge:** Energy-based removal spell that scales up, handling even large threats like [Murktide Regent](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Murktide+Regent%22).

### Historical Timeline

**2024** (tier 2, ~4%)
Deck created after MH3 prints [Ocelot Pride](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Ocelot+Pride%22), [Guide of Souls](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Guide+of+Souls%22), and [Amped Raptor](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Amped+Raptor%22). Energy package gives non-blue decks a competitive creature suite. Naya builds with [Green Sun's Zenith](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Green+Sun%27s+Zenith%22) emerge.
- [Ocelot Pride](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Ocelot+Pride%22) as token engine
- [Guide of Souls](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Guide+of+Souls%22) for energy and evasion
- [Amped Raptor](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Amped+Raptor%22) for cascade value
- [Galvanic Discharge](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Galvanic+Discharge%22) as scalable removal

**2025** (tier 1, ~7%)
Deck rises to tier 1 as pilots optimize the mana base and sideboard. Proves it can compete with blue decks through raw board presence and [Swords to Plowshares](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Swords+to+Plowshares%22).
- [Urza's Saga](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Urza%27s+Saga%22) added for artifact tutoring
- [Endurance](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Endurance%22) as green pitch answer to graveyards

**2026** (tier 1, ~8.5%)
Second most-played deck at 8.5%. Favorable matchup against Dimir Tempo keeps it popular. The best non-blue deck in Legacy.
- Stable core
- [Ajani, Nacatl Pariah](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Ajani%2C+Nacatl+Pariah%22) as additional threat

**Frequency of Change:** medium
**Change Notes:** Relatively new archetype still being optimized. Naya vs Selesnya builds are both viable. [Amped Raptor](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Amped+Raptor%22) cascade hits vary by build.

---

## Oops! All Spells

**Also known as:** Oops, [Balustrade Spy](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Balustrade+Spy%22) Combo, [Undercity Informer](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Undercity+Informer%22) Combo

**Archetype:** combo
**Colors:** B, G, U, W
**Tier:** tier 1
**Meta Share:** 8.2%
**Win Rate Estimate:** 52-54%
**Cost Estimate:** $800 (driven by [Force of Will](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Force+of+Will%22), [Chrome Mox](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Chrome+Mox%22), [Pact of Negation](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Pact+of+Negation%22))
**First Appeared:** 2013
**Peak Meta Share:** 2025-2026
**Deck Count in Sample:** 128

A blazing-fast combo deck that wins by milling its entire library using [Balustrade Spy](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Balustrade+Spy%22) or [Undercity Informer](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Undercity+Informer%22) (the deck plays zero lands, using only mana-producing artifacts and MDFCs). Once the library is milled, it uses [Narcomoeba](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Narcomoeba%22) triggers and [Dread Return](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Dread+Return%22) to reanimate a win condition. Among the fastest combo decks in the format.

### Decklist

**Main Deck:**

- 4 [Balustrade Spy](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Balustrade+Spy%22)
- 4 [Undercity Informer](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Undercity+Informer%22)
- 4 [Narcomoeba](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Narcomoeba%22)
- 3 [Shield Sphere](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Shield+Sphere%22)
- 1 [Thassa's Oracle](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Thassa%27s+Oracle%22)
- 1 [Dread Return](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Dread+Return%22)
- 4 [LothlÃ³rien Adventurer](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22LothlÃ³rien+Adventurer%22)
- 4 [Agadeem's Awakening](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Agadeem%27s+Awakening%22)
- 4 [Sea Gate Restoration](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Sea+Gate+Restoration%22)
- 4 [Turntimber Symbiosis](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Turntimber+Symbiosis%22)
- 4 [Hagra Mauling](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Hagra+Mauling%22)
- 4 [Lotus Petal](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Lotus+Petal%22)
- 4 [Chrome Mox](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Chrome+Mox%22)
- 4 [Elvish Spirit Guide](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Elvish+Spirit+Guide%22)
- 4 [Dark Ritual](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Dark+Ritual%22)
- 4 [Summoner's Pact](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Summoner%27s+Pact%22)
- 3 [Pact of Negation](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Pact+of+Negation%22)

**Sideboard:**

- 4 [Force of Will](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Force+of+Will%22)
- 4 [Grief](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Grief%22)
- 3 [Unmask](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Unmask%22)
- 2 [Thoughtseize](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Thoughtseize%22)
- 2 [Chain of Vapor](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Chain+of+Vapor%22)

### Key Matchups

- **Favorable:** Beanstalk Control, Lands, Cradle Control, Elves
- **Unfavorable:** Dimir Tempo, Red Stompy, Painter
- **Even:** Sneak and Show, The EPIC Storm, [Doomsday](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Doomsday%22)

**Similar Decks:** LED Dredge, [Doomsday](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Doomsday%22)
Shares the all-in graveyard combo approach with LED Dredge but is generally faster and more fragile. Both use free countermagic from the sideboard.

### Key Cards Explained

<img src="https://api.scryfall.com/cards/named?exact=Balustrade+Spy&format=image&version=normal&set=gtc" alt="Balustrade Spy" width="217"> <img src="https://api.scryfall.com/cards/named?exact=Undercity+Informer&format=image&version=normal&set=gtc" alt="Undercity Informer" width="217"> <img src="https://api.scryfall.com/cards/named?exact=Narcomoeba&format=image&version=normal&set=fut" alt="Narcomoeba" width="217">

- **Balustrade Spy:** Mills your entire library since you play zero actual lands. This enables the whole combo.
- **Undercity Informer:** Redundant copy of the Spy effect, ensuring consistency.
- **Narcomoeba:** Free creatures from milling that enable [Dread Return](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Dread+Return%22).
- **Dread Return:** Flashback reanimates [Thassa's Oracle](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Thassa%27s+Oracle%22) for the win.
- **LothlÃ³rien Adventurer:** MDFC that counts as a spell for the combo but taps for mana as a land.

### Historical Timeline

**2013** (tier 3, ~1%)
Deck first appears after Gatecrash prints [Balustrade Spy](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Balustrade+Spy%22) and [Undercity Informer](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Undercity+Informer%22). The zero-land combo using [Narcomoeba](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Narcomoeba%22) and [Dread Return](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Dread+Return%22) is discovered.
- [Balustrade Spy](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Balustrade+Spy%22) + [Undercity Informer](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Undercity+Informer%22) as combo enablers
- [Narcomoeba](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Narcomoeba%22) + [Dread Return](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Dread+Return%22) for win condition
- [Dark Ritual](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Dark+Ritual%22), [Chrome Mox](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Chrome+Mox%22), [Lotus Petal](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Lotus+Petal%22) for fast mana

**2014** (tier 3, ~1%)
Deck remains a fringe but explosive combo option. Consistency issues keep it from tier 1. Occasionally spikes tournaments.
- [Cabal Therapy](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Cabal+Therapy%22) added for protection
- [Shield Sphere](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Shield+Sphere%22) as free creature for Informer

**2020** (tier 2, ~3%)
Zendikar Rising MDFCs ([Agadeem's Awakening](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Agadeem%27s+Awakening%22), [Sea Gate Restoration](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Sea+Gate+Restoration%22), etc.) massively boost consistency. Spell-lands that count as spells for the combo but provide mana. Deck jumps in viability.
- [Agadeem's Awakening](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Agadeem%27s+Awakening%22) as spell-land
- [Sea Gate Restoration](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Sea+Gate+Restoration%22) as spell-land
- [Turntimber Symbiosis](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Turntimber+Symbiosis%22) and other MDFCs
- Consistency dramatically improved

**2021** (tier 2, ~3%)
Continued refinement with MDFCs. [Thassa's Oracle](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Thassa%27s+Oracle%22) replaces older win conditions as a cleaner finish.
- [Thassa's Oracle](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Thassa%27s+Oracle%22) as primary win condition
- [Summoner's Pact](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Summoner%27s+Pact%22) for consistency

**2023** (tier 2, ~4%)
LotR set adds Lothlorien Adventurer, another useful spell-creature. Deck continues to perform as a fast combo option.
- Lothlorien Adventurer added
- Refined mana base with new MDFCs

**2025** (tier 1, ~7%)
[Entomb](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Entomb%22) ban devastates Reanimator, and combo players migrate to Oops as the premier fast combo deck. Meta share spikes significantly.
- Absorbs former Reanimator players
- Becomes top combo deck in the format

**2026** (tier 1, ~8.2%)
Third most-played deck at 8.2% meta share. The fastest goldfish in the format keeps it popular despite vulnerability to graveyard hate.
- Stable optimized lists
- [Chrome Mox](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Chrome+Mox%22) and [Mox Opal](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Mox+Opal%22) as acceleration

**Frequency of Change:** low
**Change Notes:** Core combo is static. Flex slots are the protection suite ([Pact of Negation](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Pact+of+Negation%22) vs [Force of Will](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Force+of+Will%22) main) and the exact MDFC package. [LothlÃ³rien Adventurer](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22LothlÃ³rien+Adventurer%22) from LTR was a significant upgrade.

---

## Sneak and Show

**Also known as:** Sneak & Show, SnS, [Sneak Attack](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Sneak+Attack%22)

**Archetype:** combo
**Colors:** U, R
**Tier:** tier 1
**Meta Share:** 6.7%
**Win Rate Estimate:** 50-52%
**Cost Estimate:** $2,800 (driven by [Volcanic Island](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Volcanic+Island%22), [Force of Will](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Force+of+Will%22), [City of Traitors](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22City+of+Traitors%22), [Emrakul, the Aeons Torn](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Emrakul%2C+the+Aeons+Torn%22))
**First Appeared:** 2011
**Peak Meta Share:** 2013-2015
**Deck Count in Sample:** 105

A classic Legacy combo deck that cheats [Emrakul, the Aeons Torn](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Emrakul%2C+the+Aeons+Torn%22) or [Atraxa, Grand Unifier](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Atraxa%2C+Grand+Unifier%22) into play via [Show and Tell](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Show+and+Tell%22) or [Sneak Attack](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Sneak+Attack%22). Uses blue cantrips and countermagic to find and protect the combo. One of the most enduring archetypes in Legacy history.

### Decklist

**Main Deck:**

- 4 [Brainstorm](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Brainstorm%22)
- 4 [Ponder](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Ponder%22)
- 4 [Force of Will](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Force+of+Will%22)
- 2 [Daze](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Daze%22)
- 2 [Spell Pierce](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Spell+Pierce%22)
- 4 [Show and Tell](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Show+and+Tell%22)
- 4 [Sneak Attack](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Sneak+Attack%22)
- 4 [Emrakul, the Aeons Torn](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Emrakul%2C+the+Aeons+Torn%22)
- 2 [Atraxa, Grand Unifier](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Atraxa%2C+Grand+Unifier%22)
- 1 [Griselbrand](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Griselbrand%22)
- 4 [Lotus Petal](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Lotus+Petal%22)
- 4 [Ancient Tomb](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Ancient+Tomb%22)
- 3 [City of Traitors](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22City+of+Traitors%22)
- 4 [Polluted Delta](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Polluted+Delta%22)
- 3 [Scalding Tarn](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Scalding+Tarn%22)
- 3 [Volcanic Island](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Volcanic+Island%22)
- 3 [Island](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Island%22)
- 2 [Preordain](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Preordain%22)
- 2 [Flooded Strand](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Flooded+Strand%22)
- 1 [Flusterstorm](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Flusterstorm%22)

**Sideboard:**

- 2 [Flusterstorm](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Flusterstorm%22)
- 2 [Pyroclasm](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Pyroclasm%22)
- 2 [Blood Moon](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Blood+Moon%22)
- 2 [Subtlety](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Subtlety%22)
- 2 [Surgical Extraction](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Surgical+Extraction%22)
- 1 [Hydroblast](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Hydroblast%22)
- 2 [Veil of Summer](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Veil+of+Summer%22)
- 1 [Kozilek's Return](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Kozilek%27s+Return%22)
- 1 [Through the Breach](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Through+the+Breach%22)

### Key Matchups

- **Favorable:** [Ocelot Pride](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Ocelot+Pride%22) Midrange, Lands, Eldrazi, Maverick
- **Unfavorable:** Dimir Tempo, Painter, Death and Taxes
- **Even:** Oops! All Spells, The EPIC Storm, Izzet Delver

**Similar Decks:** Omni-Tell, [Doomsday](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Doomsday%22)
Omni-Tell shares [Show and Tell](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Show+and+Tell%22) but uses [Omniscience](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Omniscience%22) instead of [Sneak Attack](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Sneak+Attack%22). Both are blue combo decks using the same cantrip and counter shell.

### Key Cards Explained

<img src="https://api.scryfall.com/cards/named?exact=Show+and+Tell&format=image&version=normal&set=usg" alt="Show and Tell" width="217"> <img src="https://api.scryfall.com/cards/named?exact=Sneak+Attack&format=image&version=normal&set=usg" alt="Sneak Attack" width="217"> <img src="https://api.scryfall.com/cards/named?exact=Emrakul%2C+the+Aeons+Torn&format=image&version=normal&set=roe" alt="Emrakul, the Aeons Torn" width="217">

- **Show and Tell:** Puts Emrakul or Atraxa directly into play for just 2U, bypassing their enormous mana costs.
- **Sneak Attack:** Gives haste to cheated creatures, enabling immediate attacks with Emrakul's annihilator and extra turn triggers.
- **Emrakul, the Aeons Torn:** The premier win condition. Annihilator 6 and an extra turn usually ends the game in one attack.
- **Atraxa, Grand Unifier:** Backup threat that draws 7+ cards off [Show and Tell](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Show+and+Tell%22), burying the opponent in card advantage even if they have an answer.

### Historical Timeline

**2011** (tier 2, ~4%)
Deck solidifies as a Legacy archetype using [Sneak Attack](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Sneak+Attack%22) and [Show and Tell](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Show+and+Tell%22) to cheat [Emrakul, the Aeons Torn](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Emrakul%2C+the+Aeons+Torn%22) and [Griselbrand](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Griselbrand%22) into play. Blue shell provides [Force of Will](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Force+of+Will%22) protection.
- [Sneak Attack](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Sneak+Attack%22) + [Show and Tell](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Show+and+Tell%22) as cheat engines
- [Emrakul, the Aeons Torn](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Emrakul%2C+the+Aeons+Torn%22) as primary threat
- [Force of Will](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Force+of+Will%22), [Brainstorm](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Brainstorm%22), [Ponder](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Ponder%22) shell

**2012** (tier 1, ~6%)
[Griselbrand](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Griselbrand%22) printed in Avacyn Restored gives the deck its best [Show and Tell](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Show+and+Tell%22) target. Drawing 7 cards makes the combo almost unbeatable when it resolves.
- [Griselbrand](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Griselbrand%22) added as premier [Show and Tell](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Show+and+Tell%22) target
- [Omniscience](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Omniscience%22) sometimes used as alternative

**2015** (tier 1, ~5%)
Remains a top combo deck through multiple metagame shifts. Very stable core means bans rarely affect it directly.
- Core stable
- Sideboard adapts to Miracles-heavy meta

**2017** (tier 1, ~5%)
Benefits somewhat from [Sensei's Divining Top](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Sensei%27s+Divining+Top%22) ban gutting Miracles, as [Counterbalance](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Counterbalance%22) was a strong answer to [Show and Tell](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Show+and+Tell%22). Continues as tier 1 combo.
- Miracles (a tough matchup) weakened by Top ban
- [Cunning Wish](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Cunning+Wish%22) for silver bullets

**2021** (tier 2, ~4%)
MH2 Delver threats make tempo matchups harder. Deck endures but faces more efficient counterplay.
- Faces tougher Delver matchups with Murktide/Ragavan
- [Veil of Summer](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Veil+of+Summer%22) in sideboard

**2023** (tier 2, ~4%)
[Orcish Bowmasters](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Orcish+Bowmasters%22) doesn't directly affect the deck. Remains a consistent tier 2 combo strategy that punishes slow blue decks.
- Core unchanged
- [Atraxa, Grand Unifier](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Atraxa%2C+Grand+Unifier%22) as alternative fatty

**2025** (tier 1, ~6%)
[Entomb](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Entomb%22) ban removes Reanimator competition. Sneak and Show rises as players want a cheat-into-play strategy.
- Benefits from Reanimator decline
- [Atraxa, Grand Unifier](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Atraxa%2C+Grand+Unifier%22) alongside [Griselbrand](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Griselbrand%22)/Emrakul

**2026** (tier 1, ~6.7%)
Fourth most-played deck at 6.7%. The most stable combo archetype in Legacy's history, with a nearly unchanged core since 2012.
- Stable core
- Occasional [Show and Tell](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Show+and+Tell%22) target updates

**Frequency of Change:** low
**Change Notes:** Extremely stable archetype. Main innovation was adding Atraxa as a [Show and Tell](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Show+and+Tell%22) target alongside Emrakul. Sol land counts flex based on metagame speed.

---

## Izzet Delver

**Also known as:** UR Delver, UR Tempo

**Archetype:** tempo
**Colors:** U, R
**Tier:** tier 2
**Meta Share:** 4.3%
**Win Rate Estimate:** 49-51%
**Cost Estimate:** $3,200 (driven by [Volcanic Island](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Volcanic+Island%22), [Force of Will](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Force+of+Will%22), [Wasteland](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Wasteland%22), [Scalding Tarn](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Scalding+Tarn%22))
**First Appeared:** 2012
**Peak Meta Share:** 2020-2022
**Deck Count in Sample:** 67

The original Delver tempo shell using [Delver of Secrets](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Delver+of+Secrets%22) alongside [Lightning Bolt](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Lightning+Bolt%22) and red sideboard cards. Once the dominant deck in Legacy, it has lost ground to Dimir Tempo since [Orcish Bowmasters](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Orcish+Bowmasters%22) was printed, but remains competitive with its unique strengths: direct damage reach and superior red removal.

### Decklist

**Main Deck:**

- 4 [Delver of Secrets](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Delver+of+Secrets%22)
- 3 [Murktide Regent](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Murktide+Regent%22)
- 4 [Tamiyo, Inquisitive Student](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Tamiyo%2C+Inquisitive+Student%22)
- 4 [Dragon's Rage Channeler](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Dragon%27s+Rage+Channeler%22)
- 4 [Brainstorm](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Brainstorm%22)
- 4 [Ponder](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Ponder%22)
- 4 [Force of Will](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Force+of+Will%22)
- 4 [Daze](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Daze%22)
- 4 [Lightning Bolt](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Lightning+Bolt%22)
- 1 [Spell Pierce](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Spell+Pierce%22)
- 2 [Unholy Heat](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Unholy+Heat%22)
- 4 [Polluted Delta](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Polluted+Delta%22)
- 3 [Scalding Tarn](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Scalding+Tarn%22)
- 2 [Flooded Strand](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Flooded+Strand%22)
- 4 [Volcanic Island](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Volcanic+Island%22)
- 4 [Wasteland](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Wasteland%22)
- 1 [Island](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Island%22)
- 2 [Mountain](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Mountain%22)
- 2 [Misty Rainforest](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Misty+Rainforest%22)

**Sideboard:**

- 2 [Pyroblast](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Pyroblast%22)
- 1 [Red Elemental Blast](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Red+Elemental+Blast%22)
- 2 [Flusterstorm](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Flusterstorm%22)
- 2 [Surgical Extraction](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Surgical+Extraction%22)
- 2 [Smash to Smithereens](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Smash+to+Smithereens%22)
- 1 [Meltdown](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Meltdown%22)
- 1 [Subtlety](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Subtlety%22)
- 1 [End the Festivities](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22End+the+Festivities%22)
- 1 [Force of Negation](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Force+of+Negation%22)
- 1 [Null Rod](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Null+Rod%22)
- 1 [Price of Progress](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Price+of+Progress%22)

### Key Matchups

- **Favorable:** Lands, Beanstalk Control, Elves
- **Unfavorable:** [Ocelot Pride](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Ocelot+Pride%22) Midrange, Eldrazi, Red Stompy
- **Even:** Dimir Tempo, Sneak and Show, The EPIC Storm

**Similar Decks:** Dimir Tempo, Sultai Tempo
The original template from which Dimir Tempo diverged. Shares the core [Brainstorm](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Brainstorm%22)/[Ponder](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Ponder%22)/Force/[Daze](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Daze%22) engine but uses red for removal over black for disruption.

### Key Cards Explained

<img src="https://api.scryfall.com/cards/named?exact=Delver+of+Secrets&format=image&version=normal&set=isd" alt="Delver of Secrets" width="217"> <img src="https://api.scryfall.com/cards/named?exact=Lightning+Bolt&format=image&version=normal&set=lea" alt="Lightning Bolt" width="217"> <img src="https://api.scryfall.com/cards/named?exact=Dragon%27s+Rage+Channeler&format=image&version=normal&set=mh2" alt="Dragon's Rage Channeler" width="217">

- **Delver of Secrets:** The namesake one-drop that flips into a 3/2 flyer. With 30+ instants/sorceries, it flips reliably.
- **Lightning Bolt:** The key advantage over Dimir: efficient removal that also goes face, providing reach to close games.
- **Dragon's Rage Channeler:** Surveil on cast fuels delirium for a 3/3 flyer and fills the graveyard for [Murktide Regent](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Murktide+Regent%22).

### Historical Timeline

**2011** (tier 1, ~10%)
[Delver of Secrets](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Delver+of+Secrets%22) printed in Innistrad. RUG Delver (Canadian Threshold) immediately becomes the best tempo deck, using Delver, Nimble Mongoose, [Tarmogoyf](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Tarmogoyf%22) with [Daze](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Daze%22), Force, [Wasteland](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Wasteland%22), and [Stifle](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Stifle%22).
- [Delver of Secrets](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Delver+of+Secrets%22) as transformative one-drop
- Core: [Daze](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Daze%22), [Force of Will](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Force+of+Will%22), [Wasteland](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Wasteland%22), [Stifle](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Stifle%22), [Lightning Bolt](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Lightning+Bolt%22)
- Nimble Mongoose and [Tarmogoyf](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Tarmogoyf%22) as threats

**2012** (tier 1, ~10%)
RUG Delver and Miracles define the format. RUG is the premier tempo strategy. [Snapcaster Mage](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Snapcaster+Mage%22) adopted in some builds.
- [Snapcaster Mage](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Snapcaster+Mage%22) in some lists
- Format revolves around RUG vs Miracles

**2013** (tier 2, ~6%)
[Deathrite Shaman](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Deathrite+Shaman%22) pushes BUG Delver ahead of RUG. [True-Name Nemesis](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22True-Name+Nemesis%22) (November) gives blue tempo an uncounterable threat. Some RUG pilots switch to BUG.
- BUG Delver overtakes RUG due to [Deathrite Shaman](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Deathrite+Shaman%22)
- Some players add [True-Name Nemesis](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22True-Name+Nemesis%22)

**2015** (tier 2, ~4%)
BUG/Sultai Delver with [Deathrite Shaman](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Deathrite+Shaman%22) dominates the tempo slot. RUG Delver still viable but clearly second best.
- [Monastery Swiftspear](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Monastery+Swiftspear%22) experimented with
- [Lightning Bolt](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Lightning+Bolt%22) remains key advantage over BUG

**2018** (tier 1, ~8%)
[Deathrite Shaman](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Deathrite+Shaman%22) BANNED (July). RUG Delver immediately returns to prominence. Gitaxian Probe ban also impacts tempo strategies.
- DRS ban brings players back to RUG
- Format diversifies significantly

**2019** (tier 1, ~12%)
[Wrenn and Six](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Wrenn+and+Six%22) from MH1 makes RUG Delver oppressive — recurring [Wasteland](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Wasteland%22) is devastating. Wrenn and Six BANNED in November.
- [Wrenn and Six](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Wrenn+and+Six%22) added (then banned)
- [Wasteland](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Wasteland%22) recursion was format-warping

**2021** (tier 1, ~14%)
MH2 transforms the deck: [Dragon's Rage Channeler](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Dragon%27s+Rage+Channeler%22), [Murktide Regent](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Murktide+Regent%22), and [Ragavan, Nimble Pilferer](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Ragavan%2C+Nimble+Pilferer%22) replace the old threats. UR Delver becomes the clear best deck, dropping green entirely.
- [Dragon's Rage Channeler](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Dragon%27s+Rage+Channeler%22) replaces Nimble Mongoose
- [Murktide Regent](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Murktide+Regent%22) replaces [Tarmogoyf](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Tarmogoyf%22)
- [Ragavan, Nimble Pilferer](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Ragavan%2C+Nimble+Pilferer%22) added
- Deck shifts from RUG to UR

**2022** (tier 1, ~15%)
UR Delver with Ragavan dominates Legacy. [Expressive Iteration](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Expressive+Iteration%22) provides exceptional card advantage. Deck is ~15% of the meta and the best deck.
- [Expressive Iteration](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Expressive+Iteration%22) as card advantage engine
- Ragavan era peaks

**2023** (tier 2, ~6%)
[Orcish Bowmasters](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Orcish+Bowmasters%22) punishes cantrips and small creatures, weakening Delver mirrors. [Expressive Iteration](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Expressive+Iteration%22) banned (March). Many players switch to Dimir Tempo for Bowmasters. UR Delver drops.
- [Expressive Iteration](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Expressive+Iteration%22) BANNED
- [Orcish Bowmasters](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Orcish+Bowmasters%22) punishes the strategy
- Many pilots migrate to Dimir Tempo

**2026** (tier 2, ~4.3%)
Remains a solid tier 2 option at 4.3%. UR shell with Delver, DRC, Murktide, and [Lightning Bolt](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Lightning+Bolt%22) for players who prefer red over black.
- Stable UR core
- Plays Delver where Dimir plays Tamiyo

### Bans Impact

- **Expressive Iteration** (2023-03): Lost the deck's best card advantage engine. Contributed to the shift from UR to UB.
- **Dreadhorde Arcanist** (2021-02): Removed a key threat that gave the deck recurring card advantage.

**Frequency of Change:** medium
**Change Notes:** Lost [Expressive Iteration](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Expressive+Iteration%22) to a ban in 2023. [Dragon's Rage Channeler](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Dragon%27s+Rage+Channeler%22) and [Murktide Regent](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Murktide+Regent%22) were major additions from MH2. Still searching for the right threat mix post-Bowmasters.

---

## Painter

**Also known as:** [Painter's Servant](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Painter%27s+Servant%22) Combo, Red Painter, Imperial Painter

**Archetype:** combo
**Colors:** R
**Tier:** tier 2
**Meta Share:** 4.1%
**Win Rate Estimate:** 50-52%
**Cost Estimate:** $1,500 (driven by [City of Traitors](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22City+of+Traitors%22), [Grindstone](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Grindstone%22), [Urza's Saga](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Urza%27s+Saga%22))
**First Appeared:** 2009
**Peak Meta Share:** 2024-2026
**Deck Count in Sample:** 64

A mono-red combo deck that wins by combining [Painter's Servant](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Painter%27s+Servant%22) with [Grindstone](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Grindstone%22) to mill the opponent's entire library in one activation. Backed by blood moon effects and prison elements to slow opponents while assembling the combo. [Urza's Saga](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Urza%27s+Saga%22) provides a tutor for Grindstone.

### Decklist

**Main Deck:**

- 4 [Painter's Servant](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Painter%27s+Servant%22)
- 4 [Grindstone](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Grindstone%22)
- 3 [Goblin Welder](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Goblin+Welder%22)
- 4 [Goblin Engineer](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Goblin+Engineer%22)
- 3 [Simian Spirit Guide](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Simian+Spirit+Guide%22)
- 4 [Red Elemental Blast](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Red+Elemental+Blast%22)
- 4 [Pyroblast](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Pyroblast%22)
- 2 [Blood Moon](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Blood+Moon%22)
- 1 [Magus of the Moon](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Magus+of+the+Moon%22)
- 4 [Lotus Petal](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Lotus+Petal%22)
- 4 [Urza's Saga](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Urza%27s+Saga%22)
- 4 [Ancient Tomb](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Ancient+Tomb%22)
- 2 [City of Traitors](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22City+of+Traitors%22)
- 1 [Great Furnace](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Great+Furnace%22)
- 8 [Mountain](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Mountain%22)
- 3 [Fable of the Mirror-Breaker](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Fable+of+the+Mirror-Breaker%22)
- 1 [Fury](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Fury%22)
- 1 [Fiery Confluence](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Fiery+Confluence%22)
- 1 [Retrofitter Foundry](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Retrofitter+Foundry%22)
- 1 [Ensnaring Bridge](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Ensnaring+Bridge%22)
- 1 [Shadowspear](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Shadowspear%22)

**Sideboard:**

- 2 [Chalice of the Void](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Chalice+of+the+Void%22)
- 1 [Trinisphere](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Trinisphere%22)
- 2 [Unlicensed Hearse](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Unlicensed+Hearse%22)
- 2 [Torpor Orb](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Torpor+Orb%22)
- 2 [Cast into the Fire](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Cast+into+the+Fire%22)
- 2 [Shattering Spree](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Shattering+Spree%22)
- 2 [Null Rod](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Null+Rod%22)
- 1 [Fury](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Fury%22)
- 1 [Ensnaring Bridge](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Ensnaring+Bridge%22)

### Key Matchups

- **Favorable:** Sneak and Show, Dimir Tempo, Beanstalk Control
- **Unfavorable:** [Ocelot Pride](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Ocelot+Pride%22) Midrange, Affinity Stompy, Cradle Control
- **Even:** Oops! All Spells, The EPIC Storm, Lands

**Similar Decks:** Red Stompy, Blue Artifacts
Shares the [Ancient Tomb](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Ancient+Tomb%22) / [Blood Moon](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Blood+Moon%22) prison plan with Red Stompy, but adds the Painter-[Grindstone](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Grindstone%22) combo as an instant-win condition.

### Key Cards Explained

<img src="https://api.scryfall.com/cards/named?exact=Painter%27s+Servant&format=image&version=normal&set=shm" alt="Painter's Servant" width="217"> <img src="https://api.scryfall.com/cards/named?exact=Grindstone&format=image&version=normal&set=tmp" alt="Grindstone" width="217"> <img src="https://api.scryfall.com/cards/named?exact=Goblin+Welder&format=image&version=normal&set=usg" alt="Goblin Welder" width="217">

- **Painter's Servant:** Names blue, making all cards in the opponent's library blue, which enables [Grindstone](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Grindstone%22) to mill the entire library at once.
- **Grindstone:** With [Painter's Servant](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Painter%27s+Servant%22) in play, mills the entire library since every pair of cards shares a color.
- **Goblin Welder:** Recurs [Grindstone](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Grindstone%22) from the graveyard and enables artifact synergies.
- **Red Elemental Blast:** With Painter naming blue, this counters or destroys any permanent, acting as one-mana universal removal.

### Historical Timeline

**2009** (tier 3, ~1%)
[Painter's Servant](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Painter%27s+Servant%22) + [Grindstone](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Grindstone%22) combo deck first appears in Legacy. Uses [Imperial Recruiter](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Imperial+Recruiter%22) to find Painter and fast mana from [Ancient Tomb](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Ancient+Tomb%22).
- [Painter's Servant](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Painter%27s+Servant%22) + [Grindstone](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Grindstone%22) combo
- [Imperial Recruiter](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Imperial+Recruiter%22) as tutor
- [Ancient Tomb](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Ancient+Tomb%22) for fast mana

**2012** (tier 3, ~1.5%)
Deck maintains fringe presence. [Red Elemental Blast](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Red+Elemental+Blast%22) becomes a hard counter against everything with [Painter's Servant](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Painter%27s+Servant%22) naming blue.
- [Blood Moon](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Blood+Moon%22) from sideboard
- [Red Elemental Blast](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Red+Elemental+Blast%22) as universal counter with Painter

**2017** (tier 3, ~1.5%)
Top ban opens space for non-Miracles combo-control decks. Painter remains a consistent fringe option.
- Less [Counterbalance](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Counterbalance%22) in the format benefits Painter
- [Goblin Engineer](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Goblin+Engineer%22) experimented with

**2021** (tier 2, ~3%)
[Urza's Saga](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Urza%27s+Saga%22) from MH2 is transformative — tutors for [Grindstone](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Grindstone%22), creates tokens, and provides an alternative win condition. Deck jumps in power level.
- [Urza's Saga](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Urza%27s+Saga%22) tutors [Grindstone](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Grindstone%22)
- Saga tokens as backup plan
- [Goblin Engineer](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Goblin+Engineer%22) for artifact recursion

**2023** (tier 2, ~3%)
[Fable of the Mirror-Breaker](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Fable+of+the+Mirror-Breaker%22) experimented with. Deck remains solid tier 2 with [Urza's Saga](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Urza%27s+Saga%22) giving it staying power.
- Various red creature options explored
- Consistent tier 2 performer

**2026** (tier 2, ~4.1%)
Stable at 4.1% meta share as a tier 2 combo-stompy deck. [Urza's Saga](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Urza%27s+Saga%22) and the Painter combo give it redundancy few other decks have.
- Refined and optimized lists
- Emrakul as sideboard plan

**Frequency of Change:** medium
**Change Notes:** [Urza's Saga](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Urza%27s+Saga%22) was a major upgrade, providing a tutor for [Grindstone](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Grindstone%22). [Goblin Engineer](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Goblin+Engineer%22) replaced some older tutor options. [Fable of the Mirror-Breaker](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Fable+of+the+Mirror-Breaker%22) added as value/filtering.

---

## Lands

**Also known as:** RG Lands, Punishing Lands, [Dark Depths](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Dark+Depths%22) Lands

**Archetype:** control
**Colors:** R, G
**Tier:** tier 2
**Meta Share:** 3.8%
**Win Rate Estimate:** 50-52%
**Cost Estimate:** $5,500 (driven by [The Tabernacle at Pendrell Vale](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22The+Tabernacle+at+Pendrell+Vale%22), [Dark Depths](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Dark+Depths%22), [Wasteland](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Wasteland%22), [Grove of the Burnwillows](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Grove+of+the+Burnwillows%22))
**First Appeared:** 2012
**Peak Meta Share:** 2015-2017
**Deck Count in Sample:** 59

A land-based control deck that uses [Life from the Loam](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Life+from+the+Loam%22), [Wasteland](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Wasteland%22) recursion, and [Maze of Ith](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Maze+of+Ith%22) to control the board while assembling the [Dark Depths](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Dark+Depths%22) + [Thespian's Stage](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Thespian%27s+Stage%22) combo to create a 20/20 Marit Lage token. One of the most unique decks in Legacy, barely playing any spells.

### Decklist

**Main Deck:**

- 4 [Life from the Loam](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Life+from+the+Loam%22)
- 4 [Crop Rotation](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Crop+Rotation%22)
- 4 [Exploration](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Exploration%22)
- 4 [Elvish Reclaimer](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Elvish+Reclaimer%22)
- 2 [Endurance](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Endurance%22)
- 1 [Sylvan Library](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Sylvan+Library%22)
- 3 [Punishing Fire](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Punishing+Fire%22)
- 1 [Manabond](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Manabond%22)
- 3 [Dark Depths](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Dark+Depths%22)
- 4 [Thespian's Stage](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Thespian%27s+Stage%22)
- 4 [Wasteland](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Wasteland%22)
- 3 [Maze of Ith](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Maze+of+Ith%22)
- 1 [The Tabernacle at Pendrell Vale](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22The+Tabernacle+at+Pendrell+Vale%22)
- 4 [Grove of the Burnwillows](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Grove+of+the+Burnwillows%22)
- 1 [Taiga](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Taiga%22)
- 2 [Urza's Saga](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Urza%27s+Saga%22)
- 1 [Yavimaya, Cradle of Growth](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Yavimaya%2C+Cradle+of+Growth%22)
- 1 [Blast Zone](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Blast+Zone%22)
- 1 [Boseiju, Who Endures](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Boseiju%2C+Who+Endures%22)
- 4 [Windswept Heath](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Windswept+Heath%22)
- 2 [Forest](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Forest%22)
- 1 [Sheltered Thicket](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Sheltered+Thicket%22)
- 3 [Rishadan Port](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Rishadan+Port%22)
- 1 [Field of the Dead](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Field+of+the+Dead%22)
- 1 [Tranquil Thicket](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Tranquil+Thicket%22)

**Sideboard:**

- 3 [Force of Vigor](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Force+of+Vigor%22)
- 2 [Chalice of the Void](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Chalice+of+the+Void%22)
- 2 [Sphere of Resistance](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Sphere+of+Resistance%22)
- 2 [Pyroblast](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Pyroblast%22)
- 2 [Surgical Extraction](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Surgical+Extraction%22)
- 1 [Tireless Tracker](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Tireless+Tracker%22)
- 1 [Choke](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Choke%22)
- 1 [Drop of Honey](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Drop+of+Honey%22)
- 1 [Pithing Needle](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Pithing+Needle%22)

### Key Matchups

- **Favorable:** Dimir Tempo, Izzet Delver, Death and Taxes
- **Unfavorable:** Sneak and Show, Oops! All Spells, [Doomsday](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Doomsday%22)
- **Even:** Painter, Eldrazi, [Ocelot Pride](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Ocelot+Pride%22) Midrange

**Similar Decks:** Selesnya Depths, Cradle Control
Selesnya Depths shares the [Dark Depths](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Dark+Depths%22) combo but in a creature-based shell. Lands is more controlling and land-focused.

### Key Cards Explained

<img src="https://api.scryfall.com/cards/named?exact=Dark+Depths&format=image&version=normal&set=csp" alt="Dark Depths" width="217"> <img src="https://api.scryfall.com/cards/named?exact=Thespian%27s+Stage&format=image&version=normal&set=gtc" alt="Thespian's Stage" width="217"> <img src="https://api.scryfall.com/cards/named?exact=Life+from+the+Loam&format=image&version=normal&set=rav" alt="Life from the Loam" width="217">

- **Dark Depths:** Combines with [Thespian's Stage](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Thespian%27s+Stage%22) to instantly create a 20/20 flying indestructible Marit Lage token.
- **Thespian's Stage:** Copies [Dark Depths](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Dark+Depths%22), and since it enters with no ice counters, immediately creates Marit Lage.
- **Life from the Loam:** Engine card that recurs [Wasteland](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Wasteland%22), cycling lands, and combo pieces from the graveyard.
- **The Tabernacle at Pendrell Vale:** Forces opponents to pay for their creatures each turn or sacrifice them. Devastating against creature decks.
- **Maze of Ith:** Free repeatable removal that negates any single attacker.

### Historical Timeline

**2012** (tier 2, ~3%)
Lands establishes itself as a Legacy archetype using [Life from the Loam](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Life+from+the+Loam%22), [Wasteland](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Wasteland%22) lock, [Maze of Ith](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Maze+of+Ith%22), and [The Tabernacle at Pendrell Vale](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22The+Tabernacle+at+Pendrell+Vale%22) to control the board. [Punishing Fire](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Punishing+Fire%22) + [Grove of the Burnwillows](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Grove+of+the+Burnwillows%22) provides creature removal.
- [Life from the Loam](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Life+from+the+Loam%22) + [Wasteland](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Wasteland%22) recursion
- [Maze of Ith](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Maze+of+Ith%22) and Tabernacle for creature control
- [Punishing Fire](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Punishing+Fire%22) + [Grove of the Burnwillows](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Grove+of+the+Burnwillows%22)
- [Exploration](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Exploration%22) and [Manabond](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Manabond%22) for acceleration

**2015** (tier 2, ~3%)
[Dark Depths](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Dark+Depths%22) + [Thespian's Stage](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Thespian%27s+Stage%22) combo becomes a core part of the deck, giving it a 20/20 indestructible flying win condition alongside the Loam grind plan.
- [Dark Depths](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Dark+Depths%22) + [Thespian's Stage](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Thespian%27s+Stage%22) as primary win condition
- [Crop Rotation](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Crop+Rotation%22) as combo tutor

**2018** (tier 2, ~4%)
DRS ban helps Lands significantly — [Deathrite Shaman](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Deathrite+Shaman%22) was excellent graveyard hate against the Loam engine. Format becomes more favorable.
- [Deathrite Shaman](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Deathrite+Shaman%22) ban removes key hate piece
- [Field of the Dead](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Field+of+the+Dead%22) experimented with later

**2021** (tier 2, ~4%)
[Urza's Saga](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Urza%27s+Saga%22) from MH2 adds a powerful threat and tutor to the deck. Can find [Expedition Map](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Expedition+Map%22) or [Pithing Needle](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Pithing+Needle%22) while making Construct tokens.
- [Urza's Saga](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Urza%27s+Saga%22) as threat and tutor
- [Yavimaya, Cradle of Growth](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Yavimaya%2C+Cradle+of+Growth%22) enables easier Depths combo

**2023** (tier 2, ~3%)
Minsc & Boo or [Orcish Bowmasters](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Orcish+Bowmasters%22) in some RG or BG Lands builds. Deck continues as a consistent tier 2 option that punishes greedy mana bases.
- Various splash color experiments
- [Boseiju, Who Endures](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Boseiju%2C+Who+Endures%22) as uncounterable removal

**2026** (tier 2, ~3.8%)
Steady at 3.8% meta share. Favorable matchup against Dimir Tempo keeps it relevant. The [Wasteland](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Wasteland%22) + Loam lock remains one of Legacy's most punishing strategies.
- Stable core
- [Endurance](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Endurance%22) in sideboard for graveyard matchups

**Frequency of Change:** low
**Change Notes:** Very stable core. [Elvish Reclaimer](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Elvish+Reclaimer%22) was the most significant addition in recent years. [Urza's Saga](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Urza%27s+Saga%22) provides additional utility and Construct tokens. [Field of the Dead](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Field+of+the+Dead%22) is a newer addition for grindy games.

---

## The EPIC Storm

**Also known as:** TES, Epic Storm, Storm

**Archetype:** combo
**Colors:** U, B, R
**Tier:** tier 2
**Meta Share:** 3.5%
**Win Rate Estimate:** 50-52%
**Cost Estimate:** $2,400 (driven by [Lion's Eye Diamond](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Lion%27s+Eye+Diamond%22), [Underground Sea](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Underground+Sea%22), [Volcanic Island](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Volcanic+Island%22), [Badlands](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Badlands%22))
**First Appeared:** 2010
**Peak Meta Share:** 2018-2020
**Deck Count in Sample:** 55

A fast storm combo deck that uses mana acceleration and tutors to generate a lethal storm count, typically winning with [Tendrils of Agony](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Tendrils+of+Agony%22) or burning through the deck with [Ad Nauseam](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Ad+Nauseam%22). Faster and more aggressive than ANT, trading consistency for speed with [Chrome Mox](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Chrome+Mox%22) and [Rite of Flame](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Rite+of+Flame%22).

### Decklist

**Main Deck:**

- 4 [Dark Ritual](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Dark+Ritual%22)
- 4 [Lotus Petal](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Lotus+Petal%22)
- 4 [Lion's Eye Diamond](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Lion%27s+Eye+Diamond%22)
- 4 [Chrome Mox](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Chrome+Mox%22)
- 4 [Rite of Flame](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Rite+of+Flame%22)
- 4 [Brainstorm](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Brainstorm%22)
- 4 [Ponder](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Ponder%22)
- 4 [Thoughtseize](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Thoughtseize%22)
- 4 [Burning Wish](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Burning+Wish%22)
- 3 [Ad Nauseam](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Ad+Nauseam%22)
- 1 [Tendrils of Agony](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Tendrils+of+Agony%22)
- 2 [Galvanic Relay](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Galvanic+Relay%22)
- 2 [Beseech the Mirror](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Beseech+the+Mirror%22)
- 4 [Polluted Delta](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Polluted+Delta%22)
- 3 [Scalding Tarn](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Scalding+Tarn%22)
- 2 [Bloodstained Mire](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Bloodstained+Mire%22)
- 1 [Underground Sea](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Underground+Sea%22)
- 2 [Volcanic Island](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Volcanic+Island%22)
- 1 [Badlands](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Badlands%22)
- 1 [Swamp](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Swamp%22)
- 2 [Mishra's Bauble](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Mishra%27s+Bauble%22)

**Sideboard:**

- 1 [Tendrils of Agony](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Tendrils+of+Agony%22)
- 1 [Galvanic Relay](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Galvanic+Relay%22)
- 1 [Empty the Warrens](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Empty+the+Warrens%22)
- 1 [Echo of Eons](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Echo+of+Eons%22)
- 1 [Peer into the Abyss](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Peer+into+the+Abyss%22)
- 1 [Grapeshot](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Grapeshot%22)
- 1 [Shattering Spree](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Shattering+Spree%22)
- 1 [Pulverize](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Pulverize%22)
- 2 [Chain of Vapor](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Chain+of+Vapor%22)
- 2 [Veil of Summer](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Veil+of+Summer%22)
- 2 [Defense Grid](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Defense+Grid%22)
- 1 [Carpet of Flowers](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Carpet+of+Flowers%22)

### Key Matchups

- **Favorable:** Lands, [Ocelot Pride](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Ocelot+Pride%22) Midrange, Eldrazi
- **Unfavorable:** Dimir Tempo, Izzet Delver, Red Stompy
- **Even:** Sneak and Show, Oops! All Spells, [Doomsday](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Doomsday%22)

**Similar Decks:** [Doomsday](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Doomsday%22)
Both are UBx storm-adjacent combo decks, but TES wins through traditional storm count while [Doomsday](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Doomsday%22) uses a specific five-card pile.

### Key Cards Explained

<img src="https://api.scryfall.com/cards/named?exact=Ad+Nauseam&format=image&version=normal&set=ala" alt="Ad Nauseam" width="217"> <img src="https://api.scryfall.com/cards/named?exact=Lion%27s+Eye+Diamond&format=image&version=normal&set=mir" alt="Lion's Eye Diamond" width="217"> <img src="https://api.scryfall.com/cards/named?exact=Burning+Wish&format=image&version=normal&set=jud" alt="Burning Wish" width="217">

- **Ad Nauseam:** Draws cards equal to your life total (effectively), providing enough gas to generate lethal storm count in one big turn.
- **Lion's Eye Diamond:** The deck's [Black Lotus](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Black+Lotus%22) equivalent. Discarding your hand is mitigated by LED in response to [Burning Wish](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Burning+Wish%22) or [Brainstorm](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Brainstorm%22).
- **Burning Wish:** Tutors for [Tendrils of Agony](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Tendrils+of+Agony%22), [Empty the Warrens](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Empty+the+Warrens%22), or silver bullets from the sideboard, providing versatility.
- **Galvanic Relay:** Storm-count payoff that exiles cards for next turn, providing a resilient way to continue comboing through disruption.

### Historical Timeline

**2010** (tier 2, ~3%)
TES evolves from older Legacy Storm lists, focusing on speed over resilience compared to [Ad Nauseam](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Ad+Nauseam%22) Tendrils (ANT). Uses [Burning Wish](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Burning+Wish%22), [Rite of Flame](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Rite+of+Flame%22), and [Lion's Eye Diamond](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Lion%27s+Eye+Diamond%22).
- [Burning Wish](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Burning+Wish%22) for toolbox access
- [Rite of Flame](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Rite+of+Flame%22), [Dark Ritual](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Dark+Ritual%22), [Lion's Eye Diamond](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Lion%27s+Eye+Diamond%22) for mana
- Infernal Tutor, [Ad Nauseam](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Ad+Nauseam%22) as engines

**2011** (tier 2, ~3%)
Mental Misstep ban is positive for Storm — Misstep was devastating against [Dark Ritual](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Dark+Ritual%22) and [Rite of Flame](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Rite+of+Flame%22). Deck improves.
- Mental Misstep ban removes key hate piece
- Core storm package stable

**2015** (tier 2, ~2.5%)
[Treasure Cruise](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Treasure+Cruise%22) / Dig Through Time ban is neutral. Storm remains a consistent combo option. Gitaxian Probe used for information.
- Gitaxian Probe for free information
- Sideboard adapts to Miracles-heavy meta

**2018** (tier 2, ~2%)
Gitaxian Probe BANNED (July). Storm loses its best free cantrip and information spell. Deck adapts but takes a hit.
- Gitaxian Probe banned
- Adapts with more [Ponder](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Ponder%22)/[Preordain](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Preordain%22)

**2021** (tier 2, ~2.5%)
Continues adapting. [Galvanic Relay](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Galvanic+Relay%22) from MH2 provides a new engine for grinding through disruption. Deck gets new tools.
- [Galvanic Relay](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Galvanic+Relay%22) as new engine
- Deck pivots between speed and resilience builds

**2023** (tier 2, ~3%)
[Orcish Bowmasters](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Orcish+Bowmasters%22) is irrelevant to TES since it doesn't play creatures. Storm exists in a meta where creature decks draw the hate.
- Benefits from creature-focused meta hate
- [Beseech the Mirror](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Beseech+the+Mirror%22) experimented with

**2026** (tier 2, ~3.5%)
Stable tier 2 at 3.5% meta share. One of Legacy's most enduring archetypes with a dedicated player base that continuously optimizes.
- Stable core with ongoing optimization
- [Burning Wish](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Burning+Wish%22) targets updated regularly

**Frequency of Change:** high
**Change Notes:** Constant tuning by its dedicated community. [Galvanic Relay](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Galvanic+Relay%22) and [Beseech the Mirror](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Beseech+the+Mirror%22) are relatively recent additions that replaced older cards like Infernal Tutor. The deck evolves significantly with each new set.

---

## Eldrazi

**Also known as:** Eldrazi Stompy, Eldrazi Aggro, Colorless Eldrazi

**Archetype:** aggro
**Colors:**
**Tier:** tier 2
**Meta Share:** 3.1%
**Win Rate Estimate:** 50-52%
**Cost Estimate:** $1,200 (driven by [City of Traitors](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22City+of+Traitors%22), [Chalice of the Void](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Chalice+of+the+Void%22), [Ancient Tomb](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Ancient+Tomb%22), [Cavern of Souls](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Cavern+of+Souls%22))
**First Appeared:** 2016
**Peak Meta Share:** 2016-2017
**Deck Count in Sample:** 48

A colorless aggro-prison deck using sol lands and Eldrazi creatures to deploy oversized threats ahead of curve while disrupting opponents with [Chalice of the Void](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Chalice+of+the+Void%22) and [Thought-Knot Seer](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Thought-Knot+Seer%22). Preys on cantrip-heavy decks with Chalice on 1.

### Decklist

**Main Deck:**

- 4 [Thought-Knot Seer](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Thought-Knot+Seer%22)
- 4 [Reality Smasher](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Reality+Smasher%22)
- 4 [Eldrazi Mimic](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Eldrazi+Mimic%22)
- 4 [Matter Reshaper](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Matter+Reshaper%22)
- 2 [Endbringer](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Endbringer%22)
- 1 [Walking Ballista](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Walking+Ballista%22)
- 4 [Chalice of the Void](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Chalice+of+the+Void%22)
- 1 [Trinisphere](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Trinisphere%22)
- 4 [Lotus Petal](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Lotus+Petal%22)
- 3 [Urza's Saga](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Urza%27s+Saga%22)
- 1 [Shadowspear](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Shadowspear%22)
- 1 [Expedition Map](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Expedition+Map%22)
- 4 [Eldrazi Temple](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Eldrazi+Temple%22)
- 4 [Ancient Tomb](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Ancient+Tomb%22)
- 4 [City of Traitors](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22City+of+Traitors%22)
- 4 [Wasteland](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Wasteland%22)
- 2 [Mishra's Factory](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Mishra%27s+Factory%22)
- 1 [Eye of Ugin](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Eye+of+Ugin%22)
- 1 [Cave of the Frost Dragon](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Cave+of+the+Frost+Dragon%22)
- 1 [Ghost Quarter](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Ghost+Quarter%22)
- 2 [Mutavault](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Mutavault%22)
- 2 [Cavern of Souls](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Cavern+of+Souls%22)
- 2 [Endless One](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Endless+One%22)

**Sideboard:**

- 2 [Warping Wail](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Warping+Wail%22)
- 2 [Ratchet Bomb](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Ratchet+Bomb%22)
- 2 [Ensnaring Bridge](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Ensnaring+Bridge%22)
- 2 [Grafdigger's Cage](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Grafdigger%27s+Cage%22)
- 2 [Tormod's Crypt](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Tormod%27s+Crypt%22)
- 2 [Null Rod](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Null+Rod%22)
- 1 [All Is Dust](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22All+Is+Dust%22)
- 2 [Dismember](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Dismember%22)

### Key Matchups

- **Favorable:** Dimir Tempo, Izzet Delver, [Doomsday](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Doomsday%22)
- **Unfavorable:** Sneak and Show, Lands, The EPIC Storm
- **Even:** [Ocelot Pride](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Ocelot+Pride%22) Midrange, Painter, Red Stompy

**Similar Decks:** Red Stompy, Affinity Stompy
Shares the sol land + Chalice prison plan with Red Stompy but uses colorless Eldrazi instead of red threats. Both attack from a similar angle.

### Key Cards Explained

<img src="https://api.scryfall.com/cards/named?exact=Chalice+of+the+Void&format=image&version=normal&set=mrd" alt="Chalice of the Void" width="217"> <img src="https://api.scryfall.com/cards/named?exact=Thought-Knot+Seer&format=image&version=normal&set=ogw" alt="Thought-Knot Seer" width="217"> <img src="https://api.scryfall.com/cards/named?exact=Eldrazi+Temple&format=image&version=normal&set=roe" alt="Eldrazi Temple" width="217">

- **Chalice of the Void:** On X=1, shuts down [Brainstorm](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Brainstorm%22), [Ponder](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Ponder%22), Swords, Bolt, and most other one-mana staples in the format.
- **Thought-Knot Seer:** Disrupts the opponent's hand while providing a 4/4 body. The exile effect dodges graveyard synergies.
- **Eldrazi Temple:** Provides 2 mana toward Eldrazi spells, enabling turn-2 [Thought-Knot Seer](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Thought-Knot+Seer%22).
- **Ancient Tomb:** Two colorless mana at the cost of life, powering out early threats and lock pieces.

### Historical Timeline

**2016** (tier 1, ~8%)
Eldrazi menace begins after Oath of the Gatewatch prints [Thought-Knot Seer](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Thought-Knot+Seer%22) and [Reality Smasher](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Reality+Smasher%22). [Eye of Ugin](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Eye+of+Ugin%22) and [Eldrazi Temple](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Eldrazi+Temple%22) provide broken mana. Deck immediately tier 1 across multiple formats.
- [Thought-Knot Seer](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Thought-Knot+Seer%22) and [Reality Smasher](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Reality+Smasher%22) as threats
- [Eye of Ugin](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Eye+of+Ugin%22) and [Eldrazi Temple](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Eldrazi+Temple%22) for fast mana
- [Chalice of the Void](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Chalice+of+the+Void%22) to lock out cantrips

**2017** (tier 2, ~4%)
Post-Eldrazi winter. [Eye of Ugin](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Eye+of+Ugin%22) not banned in Legacy (unlike Modern). Deck settles into tier 2 as players learn to fight it. Various builds: mono-colorless, WE, BE.
- Format adapts to fight Eldrazi
- Various color splash experiments

**2020** (tier 2, ~3%)
Initiative creatures from Commander Legends: Battle for Baldur's Gate add a new dimension. [Caves of Chaos Adventurer](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Caves+of+Chaos+Adventurer%22) and similar cards work well with Eldrazi fast mana.
- Initiative creatures added (various Baldur's Gate cards)
- Eldrazi Stompy blends with Initiative strategies

**2023** (tier 2, ~3%)
Deck continues as a Chalice-based stompy strategy. Not directly affected by [Orcish Bowmasters](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Orcish+Bowmasters%22) since its creatures are large.
- Core stable
- Sideboard evolution for changing meta

**2026** (tier 2, ~3.1%)
Steady at 3.1%. [Chalice of the Void](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Chalice+of+the+Void%22) on one shuts down cantrip-heavy decks, keeping Eldrazi relevant as a meta foil.
- Sowing Mycospawn from MH3 as additional threat
- Stable Chalice stompy strategy

### Bans Impact

- **Eye of Ugin** (2016-04 (Modern only)): Eye was banned in Modern but remains legal in Legacy as a 1-of tutor. The deck adapted around [Eldrazi Temple](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Eldrazi+Temple%22) as the primary accelerant.

**Frequency of Change:** low
**Change Notes:** Very stable core since 2016. [Urza's Saga](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Urza%27s+Saga%22) was the biggest recent addition, providing Construct tokens and artifact tutoring.

---

## Mystic Forge Combo

**Also known as:** [Mystic Forge](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Mystic+Forge%22), Karn Forge, Mono Brown Combo

**Archetype:** combo
**Colors:**
**Tier:** tier 2
**Meta Share:** 3%
**Win Rate Estimate:** 50-52%
**Cost Estimate:** $1,800 (driven by [City of Traitors](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22City+of+Traitors%22), [Grim Monolith](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Grim+Monolith%22), [Mox Opal](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Mox+Opal%22), [Chalice of the Void](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Chalice+of+the+Void%22))
**First Appeared:** 2023
**Peak Meta Share:** 2025-2026
**Deck Count in Sample:** 47

A colorless artifact combo deck that uses [Mystic Forge](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Mystic+Forge%22) with [Sensei's Divining Top](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Sensei%27s+Divining+Top%22) and cost reducers to draw the entire deck, winning with [Walking Ballista](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Walking+Ballista%22) or [Karn, the Great Creator](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Karn%2C+the+Great+Creator%22). Combines the prison elements of Stompy with a deterministic combo kill.

### Decklist

**Main Deck:**

- 4 [Mystic Forge](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Mystic+Forge%22)
- 4 [Sensei's Divining Top](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Sensei%27s+Divining+Top%22)
- 4 [Karn, the Great Creator](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Karn%2C+the+Great+Creator%22)
- 2 [Walking Ballista](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Walking+Ballista%22)
- 3 [Thought Monitor](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Thought+Monitor%22)
- 1 [Trinisphere](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Trinisphere%22)
- 4 [Chalice of the Void](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Chalice+of+the+Void%22)
- 4 [Lotus Petal](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Lotus+Petal%22)
- 4 [Grim Monolith](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Grim+Monolith%22)
- 4 [Mox Opal](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Mox+Opal%22)
- 4 [Mishra's Bauble](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Mishra%27s+Bauble%22)
- 4 [Urza's Saga](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Urza%27s+Saga%22)
- 4 [Ancient Tomb](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Ancient+Tomb%22)
- 4 [City of Traitors](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22City+of+Traitors%22)
- 3 [Wasteland](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Wasteland%22)
- 2 [Darksteel Citadel](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Darksteel+Citadel%22)
- 2 [Inventor's Fair](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Inventor%27s+Fair%22)
- 1 [Shadowspear](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Shadowspear%22)
- 1 [Haywire Mite](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Haywire+Mite%22)
- 1 [Retrofitter Foundry](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Retrofitter+Foundry%22)

**Sideboard:**

- 1 [Ensnaring Bridge](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Ensnaring+Bridge%22)
- 1 [Tormod's Crypt](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Tormod%27s+Crypt%22)
- 1 [Pithing Needle](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Pithing+Needle%22)
- 1 [Liquimetal Coating](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Liquimetal+Coating%22)
- 1 [Mycosynth Lattice](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Mycosynth+Lattice%22)
- 1 [Wurmcoil Engine](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Wurmcoil+Engine%22)
- 1 [Spine of Ish Sah](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Spine+of+Ish+Sah%22)
- 1 [Trinisphere](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Trinisphere%22)
- 1 [Grafdigger's Cage](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Grafdigger%27s+Cage%22)
