- 1 [Null Rod](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Null+Rod%22)
- 2 [Phyrexian Revoker](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Phyrexian+Revoker%22)
- 2 [Dismember](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Dismember%22)
- 1 [Ratchet Bomb](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Ratchet+Bomb%22)

### Key Matchups

- **Favorable:** Dimir Tempo, Izzet Delver, Beanstalk Control
- **Unfavorable:** [Ocelot Pride](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Ocelot+Pride%22) Midrange, Cradle Control, Painter
- **Even:** Sneak and Show, Eldrazi, Red Stompy

**Similar Decks:** Blue Artifacts, Eldrazi, Painter
Shares the sol land + Chalice shell with Eldrazi but adds a deterministic combo finish. Blue Artifacts is a colored variant with [Thought Monitor](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Thought+Monitor%22) and Emry.

### Key Cards Explained

<img src="https://api.scryfall.com/cards/named?exact=Mystic+Forge&format=image&version=normal&set=m20" alt="Mystic Forge" width="217"> <img src="https://api.scryfall.com/cards/named?exact=Sensei%27s+Divining+Top&format=image&version=normal&set=chk" alt="Sensei's Divining Top" width="217"> <img src="https://api.scryfall.com/cards/named?exact=Karn%2C+the+Great+Creator&format=image&version=normal&set=war" alt="Karn, the Great Creator" width="217">

- **Mystic Forge:** With [Sensei's Divining Top](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Sensei%27s+Divining+Top%22) and a cost reducer, creates an infinite draw loop to find [Walking Ballista](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Walking+Ballista%22) for the kill.
- **Sensei's Divining Top:** Key combo piece that draws a card and goes to the top of library, looping with [Mystic Forge](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Mystic+Forge%22).
- **Karn, the Great Creator:** Tutors silver bullets from the sideboard and shuts off opponent's artifacts. -2 finds the missing combo piece.
- **Grim Monolith:** Fast mana that powers out early [Mystic Forge](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Mystic+Forge%22) or Karn. Acts as the cost reducer for the combo loop.

### Historical Timeline

**2023** (tier 3, ~1%)
[Mystic Forge](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Mystic+Forge%22) combo deck emerges using Mystic Forge with artifact cost reducers to draw through the deck and generate lethal artifact synergies.
- [Mystic Forge](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Mystic+Forge%22) as engine
- Artifact cost reducers (Foundry Inspector, Etherium Sculptor)
- [Karn, the Great Creator](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Karn%2C+the+Great+Creator%22) as tutor/lock

**2024** (tier 2, ~2%)
Deck refines its combo lines and gains MH3 artifacts. Becomes more consistent and rises in the meta.
- MH3 artifact support cards
- Improved combo consistency

**2026** (tier 2, ~3.0%)
Solid tier 2 at 3.0%. A colorless combo deck that punishes fair blue strategies with [Chalice of the Void](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Chalice+of+the+Void%22) and [Trinisphere](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Trinisphere%22).
- Optimized artifact shell
- Karn wishboard refined

**Frequency of Change:** medium
**Change Notes:** Relatively new archetype that emerged with [Mystic Forge](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Mystic+Forge%22) + Top. [Karn, the Great Creator](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Karn%2C+the+Great+Creator%22) acts as both a toolbox and a combo piece. The wishboard is heavily metagame dependent.

---

## Doomsday

**Also known as:** DDFT, [Doomsday](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Doomsday%22) Fetchland Tendrils

**Archetype:** combo
**Colors:** U, B
**Tier:** tier 2
**Meta Share:** 2.7%
**Win Rate Estimate:** 50-52%
**Cost Estimate:** $2,600 (driven by [Underground Sea](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Underground+Sea%22), [Force of Will](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Force+of+Will%22), [Polluted Delta](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Polluted+Delta%22))
**First Appeared:** 2012
**Peak Meta Share:** 2021-2022
**Deck Count in Sample:** 42

A combo deck that casts [Doomsday](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Doomsday%22) to stack a five-card pile that wins the game, typically with [Thassa's Oracle](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Thassa%27s+Oracle%22). Extremely skill-intensive, requiring knowledge of many different piles for various game states. Thassa's Oracle simplified the win condition significantly from earlier Oracle-less builds.

### Decklist

**Main Deck:**

- 4 [Doomsday](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Doomsday%22)
- 1 [Thassa's Oracle](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Thassa%27s+Oracle%22)
- 4 [Dark Ritual](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Dark+Ritual%22)
- 4 [Brainstorm](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Brainstorm%22)
- 4 [Ponder](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Ponder%22)
- 3 [Preordain](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Preordain%22)
- 3 [Personal Tutor](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Personal+Tutor%22)
- 4 [Force of Will](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Force+of+Will%22)
- 4 [Daze](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Daze%22)
- 3 [Thoughtseize](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Thoughtseize%22)
- 2 [Street Wraith](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Street+Wraith%22)
- 1 [Edge of Autumn](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Edge+of+Autumn%22)
- 2 [Consider](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Consider%22)
- 2 [Ideas Unbound](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Ideas+Unbound%22)
- 4 [Lotus Petal](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Lotus+Petal%22)
- 4 [Polluted Delta](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Polluted+Delta%22)
- 4 [Misty Rainforest](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Misty+Rainforest%22)
- 4 [Underground Sea](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Underground+Sea%22)
- 1 [Island](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Island%22)
- 1 [Swamp](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Swamp%22)
- 1 [Flooded Strand](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Flooded+Strand%22)

**Sideboard:**

- 2 [Flusterstorm](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Flusterstorm%22)
- 2 [Surgical Extraction](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Surgical+Extraction%22)
- 2 [Sheoldred's Edict](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Sheoldred%27s+Edict%22)
- 1 [Massacre](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Massacre%22)
- 2 [Hydroblast](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Hydroblast%22)
- 2 [Orcish Bowmasters](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Orcish+Bowmasters%22)
- 1 [Nihil Spellbomb](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Nihil+Spellbomb%22)
- 1 [Force of Negation](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Force+of+Negation%22)
- 1 [Shelldock Isle](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Shelldock+Isle%22)
- 1 [Emrakul, the Aeons Torn](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Emrakul%2C+the+Aeons+Torn%22)

### Key Matchups

- **Favorable:** Lands, [Ocelot Pride](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Ocelot+Pride%22) Midrange, Elves
- **Unfavorable:** Dimir Tempo, Eldrazi, Red Stompy
- **Even:** Sneak and Show, The EPIC Storm, Oops! All Spells

**Similar Decks:** The EPIC Storm, Dimir Tempo
Shares the UB cantrip + disruption shell with Dimir Tempo but uses it to set up a combo kill rather than tempo pressure. Shares the storm adjacency with TES.

### Key Cards Explained

<img src="https://api.scryfall.com/cards/named?exact=Doomsday&format=image&version=normal&set=wth" alt="Doomsday" width="217"> <img src="https://api.scryfall.com/cards/named?exact=Thassa%27s+Oracle&format=image&version=normal&set=thb" alt="Thassa's Oracle" width="217"> <img src="https://api.scryfall.com/cards/named?exact=Ideas+Unbound&format=image&version=normal&set=sok" alt="Ideas Unbound" width="217">

- **Doomsday:** The namesake card. For BBB, you stack your library with exactly five cards that win the game, then draw into the pile.
- **Thassa's Oracle:** Win condition that wins when it enters the battlefield if your devotion to blue exceeds your library size. After [Doomsday](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Doomsday%22), this is trivially achieved.
- **Ideas Unbound:** Draws three cards from the [Doomsday](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Doomsday%22) pile for UU, enabling compact winning piles.
- **Street Wraith:** Free cantrip that draws through the [Doomsday](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Doomsday%22) pile without costing mana.

### Historical Timeline

**2012** (tier 3, ~0.5%)
[Doomsday](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Doomsday%22) exists as a fringe Legacy combo deck using the namesake card to stack a five-card library and win deterministically. Complex execution keeps it niche.
- [Doomsday](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Doomsday%22) as combo engine
- Laboratory Maniac as win condition
- [Brainstorm](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Brainstorm%22), [Ponder](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Ponder%22) for setup

**2019** (tier 2, ~2%)
[Thassa's Oracle](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Thassa%27s+Oracle%22) printed (Theros Beyond Death). Dramatically simplifies [Doomsday](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Doomsday%22) piles — Oracle is much easier to win with than Laboratory Maniac. Deck viability jumps.
- [Thassa's Oracle](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Thassa%27s+Oracle%22) replaces Laboratory Maniac
- [Doomsday](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Doomsday%22) piles become much simpler
- Deck accessibility improves significantly

**2021** (tier 2, ~2.5%)
Continues as a strong combo option. [Personal Tutor](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Personal+Tutor%22) and other cantrips help find [Doomsday](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Doomsday%22) consistently. Compact combo footprint allows flexible shell.
- [Personal Tutor](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Personal+Tutor%22) for consistency
- [Dark Ritual](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Dark+Ritual%22) acceleration

**2023** (tier 2, ~2.5%)
[Up the Beanstalk](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Up+the+Beanstalk%22) and other card draw options explored. Deck remains a skill-testing tier 2 combo option.
- Various cantrip configurations tested
- [Cavern of Souls](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Cavern+of+Souls%22) for Oracle resolution

**2026** (tier 2, ~2.7%)
Consistent tier 2 at 2.7%. Rewards mastery and punishes opponents who can't interact with the stack.
- Refined pile construction
- Stable combo core

**Frequency of Change:** medium
**Change Notes:** [Thassa's Oracle](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Thassa%27s+Oracle%22) revolutionized the deck by simplifying pile construction. The protection suite and draw spells flex based on metagame.

---

## Red Stompy

**Also known as:** Mono Red Prison, Red Prison, Dragon Stompy

**Archetype:** prison
**Colors:** R
**Tier:** tier 2
**Meta Share:** 2.7%
**Win Rate Estimate:** 50-52%
**Cost Estimate:** $1,300 (driven by [City of Traitors](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22City+of+Traitors%22), [Chalice of the Void](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Chalice+of+the+Void%22), [Chrome Mox](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Chrome+Mox%22))
**First Appeared:** 2008
**Peak Meta Share:** 2019-2020
**Deck Count in Sample:** 42

A mono-red prison deck that uses sol lands to deploy [Blood Moon](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Blood+Moon%22), [Chalice of the Void](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Chalice+of+the+Void%22), and [Trinisphere](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Trinisphere%22) to lock opponents out of the game while attacking with efficient red threats like [Goblin Rabblemaster](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Goblin+Rabblemaster%22) and [Fury](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Fury%22). Punishes greedy mana bases.

### Decklist

**Main Deck:**

- 4 [Goblin Rabblemaster](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Goblin+Rabblemaster%22)
- 3 [Legion Warboss](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Legion+Warboss%22)
- 2 [Fury](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Fury%22)
- 4 [Caves of Chaos Adventurer](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Caves+of+Chaos+Adventurer%22)
- 2 [Fable of the Mirror-Breaker](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Fable+of+the+Mirror-Breaker%22)
- 2 [Laelia, the Blade Reforged](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Laelia%2C+the+Blade+Reforged%22)
- 4 [Blood Moon](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Blood+Moon%22)
- 4 [Chalice of the Void](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Chalice+of+the+Void%22)
- 1 [Trinisphere](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Trinisphere%22)
- 4 [Chrome Mox](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Chrome+Mox%22)
- 4 [Lotus Petal](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Lotus+Petal%22)
- 3 [Fiery Confluence](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Fiery+Confluence%22)
- 4 [Ancient Tomb](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Ancient+Tomb%22)
- 4 [City of Traitors](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22City+of+Traitors%22)
- 9 [Mountain](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Mountain%22)
- 2 [Den of the Bugbear](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Den+of+the+Bugbear%22)
- 2 [Urza's Saga](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Urza%27s+Saga%22)
- 1 [Shadowspear](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Shadowspear%22)
- 1 [Retrofitter Foundry](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Retrofitter+Foundry%22)

**Sideboard:**

- 2 [Torpor Orb](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Torpor+Orb%22)
- 2 [Ensnaring Bridge](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Ensnaring+Bridge%22)
- 2 [Shattering Spree](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Shattering+Spree%22)
- 2 [Unlicensed Hearse](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Unlicensed+Hearse%22)
- 2 [Magus of the Moon](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Magus+of+the+Moon%22)
- 2 [Pyrokinesis](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Pyrokinesis%22)
- 1 [Cast into the Fire](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Cast+into+the+Fire%22)
- 2 [Null Rod](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Null+Rod%22)

### Key Matchups

- **Favorable:** The EPIC Storm, [Doomsday](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Doomsday%22), Oops! All Spells, Izzet Delver
- **Unfavorable:** Sneak and Show, Lands, [Ocelot Pride](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Ocelot+Pride%22) Midrange
- **Even:** Dimir Tempo, Eldrazi, Painter

**Similar Decks:** Painter, Eldrazi
Shares the sol land + Chalice + [Blood Moon](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Blood+Moon%22) shell with Painter but lacks the combo finish, relying on creature damage instead.

### Key Cards Explained

<img src="https://api.scryfall.com/cards/named?exact=Blood+Moon&format=image&version=normal&set=drk" alt="Blood Moon" width="217"> <img src="https://api.scryfall.com/cards/named?exact=Chalice+of+the+Void&format=image&version=normal&set=mrd" alt="Chalice of the Void" width="217"> <img src="https://api.scryfall.com/cards/named?exact=Goblin+Rabblemaster&format=image&version=normal&set=m15" alt="Goblin Rabblemaster" width="217">

- **Blood Moon:** Turns all nonbasic lands into Mountains, devastating multi-color decks that rely on fetchlands and duals.
- **Chalice of the Void:** On 1, shuts down most of the format's cantrips and interaction. The deck's spells are designed to avoid being hit.
- **Goblin Rabblemaster:** Generates tokens every turn and grows itself. Ends games quickly once the opponent is locked under prison pieces.
- **Caves of Chaos Adventurer:** Initiative creature that generates value from the undercity, providing card advantage in a prison shell.

### Historical Timeline

**2008** (tier 3, ~1.5%)
Mono-Red Stompy (Dragon Stompy) emerges as a Legacy archetype using [Blood Moon](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Blood+Moon%22), [Chalice of the Void](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Chalice+of+the+Void%22), and [Chrome Mox](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Chrome+Mox%22) to lock opponents out while beating down with aggressive red threats.
- [Blood Moon](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Blood+Moon%22) + [Chalice of the Void](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Chalice+of+the+Void%22) lock pieces
- [Chrome Mox](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Chrome+Mox%22), [Simian Spirit Guide](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Simian+Spirit+Guide%22) for fast mana
- [Ancient Tomb](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Ancient+Tomb%22) and [City of Traitors](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22City+of+Traitors%22)

**2014** (tier 3, ~1.5%)
Deck remains a budget-friendly way into Legacy. Various threat suites tried including [Goblin Rabblemaster](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Goblin+Rabblemaster%22).
- [Goblin Rabblemaster](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Goblin+Rabblemaster%22) as efficient threat
- [Magus of the Moon](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Magus+of+the+Moon%22) as redundancy

**2019** (tier 2, ~2%)
Modern Horizons adds Seasoned Pyromancer. Chandra, Torch of Defiance provides card advantage and a win condition.
- Seasoned Pyromancer for card filtering
- Chandra, Torch of Defiance as planeswalker threat

**2022** (tier 2, ~2.5%)
[Fable of the Mirror-Breaker](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Fable+of+the+Mirror-Breaker%22) adds powerful three-drop. Initiative creatures ([Caves of Chaos Adventurer](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Caves+of+Chaos+Adventurer%22)) give the deck a new powerful angle.
- [Fable of the Mirror-Breaker](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Fable+of+the+Mirror-Breaker%22) for value
- Initiative creatures experimented with

**2024** (tier 2, ~2.5%)
MH3 energy cards not useful for mono-red. Deck continues with prison + threats strategy.
- [Broadside Bombardiers](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Broadside+Bombardiers%22) and other new red threats
- Stable prison shell

**2026** (tier 2, ~2.7%)
Solid at 2.7%. [Blood Moon](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Blood+Moon%22) and Chalice remain devastating against greedy mana bases and cantrip-heavy decks.
- Core lock pieces unchanged
- Threat suite modernized

**Frequency of Change:** medium
**Change Notes:** [Caves of Chaos Adventurer](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Caves+of+Chaos+Adventurer%22) from Commander Legends was a significant upgrade. [Urza's Saga](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Urza%27s+Saga%22) provides additional value. The threat suite rotates frequently.

---

## Affinity Stompy

**Also known as:** Affinity, Artifact Aggro, All-In Affinity

**Archetype:** aggro
**Colors:**
**Tier:** tier 2
**Meta Share:** 2.4%
**Win Rate Estimate:** 50-52%
**Cost Estimate:** $1,100 (driven by [Mox Opal](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Mox+Opal%22), [Ancient Tomb](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Ancient+Tomb%22), [Chalice of the Void](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Chalice+of+the+Void%22))
**First Appeared:** 2023
**Peak Meta Share:** 2025-2026
**Deck Count in Sample:** 38

A colorless artifact aggro deck that leverages affinity creatures, [Urza's Saga](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Urza%27s+Saga%22) constructs, and [Cranial Plating](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Cranial+Plating%22) to deal massive damage quickly. Plays cheap or free artifact creatures alongside [Chalice of the Void](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Chalice+of+the+Void%22) to combine aggression with disruption.

### Decklist

**Main Deck:**

- 4 [Frogmite](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Frogmite%22)
- 4 [Sojourner's Companion](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Sojourner%27s+Companion%22)
- 4 [Thought Monitor](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Thought+Monitor%22)
- 4 [Myr Enforcer](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Myr+Enforcer%22)
- 4 [Ornithopter](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Ornithopter%22)
- 4 [Cranial Plating](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Cranial+Plating%22)
- 2 [Nettlecyst](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Nettlecyst%22)
- 4 [Mox Opal](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Mox+Opal%22)
- 4 [Springleaf Drum](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Springleaf+Drum%22)
- 4 [Mishra's Bauble](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Mishra%27s+Bauble%22)
- 3 [Chalice of the Void](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Chalice+of+the+Void%22)
- 4 [Urza's Saga](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Urza%27s+Saga%22)
- 4 [Ancient Tomb](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Ancient+Tomb%22)
- 4 [Darksteel Citadel](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Darksteel+Citadel%22)
- 2 [Seat of the Synod](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Seat+of+the+Synod%22)
- 3 [Treasure Vault](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Treasure+Vault%22)
- 1 [Shadowspear](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Shadowspear%22)
- 1 [Retrofitter Foundry](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Retrofitter+Foundry%22)

**Sideboard:**

- 2 [Chalice of the Void](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Chalice+of+the+Void%22)
- 2 [Torpor Orb](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Torpor+Orb%22)
- 2 [Grafdigger's Cage](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Grafdigger%27s+Cage%22)
- 2 [Dismember](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Dismember%22)
- 2 [Relic of Progenitus](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Relic+of+Progenitus%22)
- 2 [Ratchet Bomb](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Ratchet+Bomb%22)
- 0 [Null Rod](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Null+Rod%22)
- 1 [Haywire Mite](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Haywire+Mite%22)
- 1 [Pithing Needle](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Pithing+Needle%22)
- 1 [Phyrexian Revoker](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Phyrexian+Revoker%22)

### Key Matchups

- **Favorable:** Dimir Tempo, Izzet Delver, Beanstalk Control
- **Unfavorable:** Painter, [Ocelot Pride](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Ocelot+Pride%22) Midrange, Cradle Control
- **Even:** Eldrazi, Red Stompy, Sneak and Show

**Similar Decks:** [Mystic Forge](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Mystic+Forge%22) Combo, Blue Artifacts, Eldrazi
Shares the artifact-heavy strategy with [Mystic Forge](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Mystic+Forge%22) and Blue Artifacts but is more aggressive with affinity creatures and [Cranial Plating](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Cranial+Plating%22).

### Key Cards Explained

<img src="https://api.scryfall.com/cards/named?exact=Cranial+Plating&format=image&version=normal&set=5dn" alt="Cranial Plating" width="217"> <img src="https://api.scryfall.com/cards/named?exact=Urza%27s+Saga&format=image&version=normal&set=mh2" alt="Urza's Saga" width="217"> <img src="https://api.scryfall.com/cards/named?exact=Thought+Monitor&format=image&version=normal&set=mh2" alt="Thought Monitor" width="217">

- **Cranial Plating:** Attaches to any creature for lethal damage in a deck full of artifacts. Can be moved at instant speed.
- **Urza's Saga:** Tutors for [Cranial Plating](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Cranial+Plating%22), [Mox Opal](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Mox+Opal%22), or [Springleaf Drum](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Springleaf+Drum%22) while creating Construct tokens that scale with artifact count.
- **Thought Monitor:** Affinity for artifacts makes this a 1-2 mana 2/2 flyer that draws 2 cards.
- **Mox Opal:** Free mana that enables explosive starts and contributes to affinity counts.

### Historical Timeline

**2023** (tier 3, ~1%)
Modern artifact cards and new printings make an artifact aggro deck viable in Legacy. [Thought Monitor](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Thought+Monitor%22), [Sojourner's Companion](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Sojourner%27s+Companion%22), and [Nettlecyst](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Nettlecyst%22) create a critical mass of artifact synergies.
- [Thought Monitor](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Thought+Monitor%22) for card draw
- [Nettlecyst](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Nettlecyst%22) as equipment threat
- [Urza's Saga](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Urza%27s+Saga%22) as land/threat/tutor

**2024** (tier 2, ~2%)
Deck refined with MH3 artifacts. Cranial Ram and other new printings add power. [Chalice of the Void](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Chalice+of+the+Void%22) gives it disruption.
- Cranial Ram as efficient equipment
- [Chalice of the Void](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Chalice+of+the+Void%22) for disruption
- [Frogmite](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Frogmite%22) and [Myr Enforcer](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Myr+Enforcer%22) as cheap threats

**2026** (tier 2, ~2.4%)
Established tier 2 at 2.4%. A fast artifact aggro deck with Chalice disruption that can race combo and go under control.
- Optimized artifact creature base
- Stable [Urza's Saga](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Urza%27s+Saga%22) + Chalice shell

**Frequency of Change:** medium
**Change Notes:** [Urza's Saga](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Urza%27s+Saga%22) elevated the entire artifact aggro archetype. Modern Horizons printings have steadily improved the creature base.

---

## Beanstalk Control

**Also known as:** 4C Control, Beanstalk Midrange, Jeskai Beanstalk

**Archetype:** control
**Colors:** W, U, R, G
**Tier:** tier 2
**Meta Share:** 2.3%
**Win Rate Estimate:** 49-51%
**Cost Estimate:** $4,200 (driven by [Underground Sea](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Underground+Sea%22), [Volcanic Island](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Volcanic+Island%22), [Tundra](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Tundra%22), [Tropical Island](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Tropical+Island%22), [Force of Will](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Force+of+Will%22))
**First Appeared:** 2023
**Peak Meta Share:** 2024
**Deck Count in Sample:** 36

A four-color control deck built around [Up the Beanstalk](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Up+the+Beanstalk%22) as a card advantage engine. Playing 5+ mana value cards like [Force of Will](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Force+of+Will%22), [Leyline Binding](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Leyline+Binding%22), and [Solitude](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Solitude%22) for free triggers Beanstalk's draw ability. Grinds opponents out with removal and card advantage.

### Decklist

**Main Deck:**

- 4 [Up the Beanstalk](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Up+the+Beanstalk%22)
- 4 [Brainstorm](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Brainstorm%22)
- 4 [Ponder](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Ponder%22)
- 4 [Force of Will](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Force+of+Will%22)
- 4 [Swords to Plowshares](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Swords+to+Plowshares%22)
- 4 [Leyline Binding](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Leyline+Binding%22)
- 2 [Prismatic Ending](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Prismatic+Ending%22)
- 4 [Orcish Bowmasters](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Orcish+Bowmasters%22)
- 3 [Endurance](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Endurance%22)
- 2 [Subtlety](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Subtlety%22)
- 2 [Solitude](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Solitude%22)
- 2 [LÃ³rien Revealed](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22LÃ³rien+Revealed%22)
- 4 [Polluted Delta](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Polluted+Delta%22)
- 3 [Flooded Strand](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Flooded+Strand%22)
- 2 [Misty Rainforest](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Misty+Rainforest%22)
- 1 [Underground Sea](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Underground+Sea%22)
- 1 [Volcanic Island](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Volcanic+Island%22)
- 1 [Tundra](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Tundra%22)
- 1 [Tropical Island](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Tropical+Island%22)
- 1 [Hallowed Fountain](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Hallowed+Fountain%22)
- 1 [Island](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Island%22)
- 1 [Plains](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Plains%22)
- 3 [Wasteland](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Wasteland%22)
- 1 [Mystic Sanctuary](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Mystic+Sanctuary%22)
- 1 [Otawara, Soaring City](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Otawara%2C+Soaring+City%22)

**Sideboard:**

- 2 [Flusterstorm](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Flusterstorm%22)
- 2 [Surgical Extraction](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Surgical+Extraction%22)
- 2 [Hydroblast](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Hydroblast%22)
- 1 [Pyroblast](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Pyroblast%22)
- 1 [Force of Negation](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Force+of+Negation%22)
- 2 [Veil of Summer](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Veil+of+Summer%22)
- 2 [Containment Priest](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Containment+Priest%22)
- 2 [Terminus](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Terminus%22)
- 1 [Back to Basics](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Back+to+Basics%22)

### Key Matchups

- **Favorable:** Lands, Death and Taxes, Elves
- **Unfavorable:** Dimir Tempo, Painter, [Mystic Forge](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Mystic+Forge%22) Combo, Affinity Stompy
- **Even:** Sneak and Show, [Ocelot Pride](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Ocelot+Pride%22) Midrange, Izzet Delver

**Similar Decks:** Jeskai Control
Jeskai Control is a leaner three-color version that trades Beanstalk card advantage for more countermagic. Both are blue control decks with white removal.

### Key Cards Explained

<img src="https://api.scryfall.com/cards/named?exact=Up+the+Beanstalk&format=image&version=normal&set=woe" alt="Up the Beanstalk" width="217"> <img src="https://api.scryfall.com/cards/named?exact=Leyline+Binding&format=image&version=normal&set=dmu" alt="Leyline Binding" width="217"> <img src="https://api.scryfall.com/cards/named?exact=Solitude&format=image&version=normal&set=mh2" alt="Solitude" width="217">

- **Up the Beanstalk:** Draws a card on ETB and whenever you cast a 5+ MV spell. Free-cast evoke creatures and [Force of Will](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Force+of+Will%22) all trigger it.
- **Leyline Binding:** Six-mana removal spell that costs W with enough domain, triggering Beanstalk while being efficient removal.
- **Solitude:** Evoke for free exile removal that triggers Beanstalk. Provides a 3/2 lifelink body when hard-cast.
- **LÃ³rien Revealed:** Draws 3 cards for 5 mana (triggering Beanstalk) or island-cycles for 1 to fix mana early.

### Historical Timeline

**2023** (tier 2, ~3%)
[Up the Beanstalk](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Up+the+Beanstalk%22) from Wilds of Eldraine enables 4-color control piles. Drawing a card whenever you cast a 5+ MV spell (including [Force of Will](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Force+of+Will%22), [Solitude](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Solitude%22), etc.) provides incredible card advantage.
- [Up the Beanstalk](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Up+the+Beanstalk%22) as card engine
- [Leyline Binding](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Leyline+Binding%22) as efficient removal
- 4-color mana base with Triomes
- Free pitch spells trigger Beanstalk

**2024** (tier 2, ~3%)
Deck establishes itself as the premier control strategy. Various builds from Jeskai to 4-color. Competes with Miracles-style UW as the control deck of choice.
- Refined mana bases
- [Uro, Titan of Nature's Wrath](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Uro%2C+Titan+of+Nature%27s+Wrath%22) in some builds

**2026** (tier 2, ~2.3%)
Steady at 2.3%. The format's primary multicolor control strategy, though vulnerable to [Wasteland](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Wasteland%22)-heavy decks and fast combo.
- Stable 4c control shell
- Sideboard heavily tuned to meta

**Frequency of Change:** high
**Change Notes:** The exact color combination and threat/removal suite shifts frequently. Some builds lean Jeskai, others splash black or green more heavily. [Up the Beanstalk](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Up+the+Beanstalk%22) from Wilds of Eldraine was the catalyst for the archetype.

---

## Cradle Control

**Also known as:** GW Elves Control, [Gaea's Cradle](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Gaea%27s+Cradle%22) Control, Green Stompy

**Archetype:** midrange
**Colors:** G
**Tier:** tier 2
**Meta Share:** 2.3%
**Win Rate Estimate:** 50-52%
**Cost Estimate:** $3,800 (driven by [Gaea's Cradle](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Gaea%27s+Cradle%22), [Savannah](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Savannah%22), [Force of Vigor](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Force+of+Vigor%22))
**First Appeared:** 2022
**Peak Meta Share:** 2025-2026
**Deck Count in Sample:** 36

A green-based midrange deck that leverages [Gaea's Cradle](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Gaea%27s+Cradle%22) to generate enormous amounts of mana, deploying powerful creatures and planeswalkers. Uses [Green Sun's Zenith](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Green+Sun%27s+Zenith%22) as a creature toolbox. Combines mana acceleration with disruptive elements like [Collector Ouphe](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Collector+Ouphe%22).

### Decklist

**Main Deck:**

- 4 [Green Sun's Zenith](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Green+Sun%27s+Zenith%22)
- 4 [Elvish Reclaimer](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Elvish+Reclaimer%22)
- 1 [Dryad Arbor](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Dryad+Arbor%22)
- 4 [Noble Hierarch](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Noble+Hierarch%22)
- 2 [Collector Ouphe](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Collector+Ouphe%22)
- 3 [Endurance](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Endurance%22)
- 2 [Titania, Protector of Argoth](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Titania%2C+Protector+of+Argoth%22)
- 1 [Primeval Titan](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Primeval+Titan%22)
- 1 [Craterhoof Behemoth](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Craterhoof+Behemoth%22)
- 1 [Scavenging Ooze](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Scavenging+Ooze%22)
- 2 [Sylvan Library](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Sylvan+Library%22)
- 4 [Once Upon a Time](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Once+Upon+a+Time%22)
- 4 [Swords to Plowshares](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Swords+to+Plowshares%22)
- 3 [Gaea's Cradle](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Gaea%27s+Cradle%22)
- 2 [Dark Depths](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Dark+Depths%22)
- 2 [Thespian's Stage](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Thespian%27s+Stage%22)
- 3 [Wasteland](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Wasteland%22)
- 4 [Windswept Heath](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Windswept+Heath%22)
- 2 [Savannah](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Savannah%22)
- 4 [Forest](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Forest%22)
- 1 [Yavimaya, Cradle of Growth](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Yavimaya%2C+Cradle+of+Growth%22)
- 1 [Boseiju, Who Endures](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Boseiju%2C+Who+Endures%22)
- 2 [Urza's Saga](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Urza%27s+Saga%22)
- 1 [Karakas](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Karakas%22)
- 2 [Verdant Catacombs](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Verdant+Catacombs%22)

**Sideboard:**

- 3 [Force of Vigor](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Force+of+Vigor%22)
- 2 [Mindbreak Trap](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Mindbreak+Trap%22)
- 2 [Choke](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Choke%22)
- 2 [Chalice of the Void](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Chalice+of+the+Void%22)
- 2 [Containment Priest](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Containment+Priest%22)
- 1 [Haywire Mite](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Haywire+Mite%22)
- 1 [Reclamation Sage](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Reclamation+Sage%22)
- 1 [Pithing Needle](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Pithing+Needle%22)
- 1 [Torpor Orb](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Torpor+Orb%22)

### Key Matchups

- **Favorable:** Painter, [Mystic Forge](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Mystic+Forge%22) Combo, Affinity Stompy
- **Unfavorable:** Sneak and Show, Oops! All Spells, The EPIC Storm
- **Even:** Dimir Tempo, [Ocelot Pride](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Ocelot+Pride%22) Midrange, Lands

**Similar Decks:** Elves, Maverick, [Ocelot Pride](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Ocelot+Pride%22) Midrange
Shares the [Green Sun's Zenith](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Green+Sun%27s+Zenith%22) toolbox and [Gaea's Cradle](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Gaea%27s+Cradle%22) engine with Elves but is slower and more controlling. Maverick is a more creature-focused GW approach.

### Key Cards Explained

<img src="https://api.scryfall.com/cards/named?exact=Gaea%27s+Cradle&format=image&version=normal&set=usg" alt="Gaea's Cradle" width="217"> <img src="https://api.scryfall.com/cards/named?exact=Green+Sun%27s+Zenith&format=image&version=normal&set=mbs" alt="Green Sun's Zenith" width="217"> <img src="https://api.scryfall.com/cards/named?exact=Collector+Ouphe&format=image&version=normal&set=mh1" alt="Collector Ouphe" width="217">

- **Gaea's Cradle:** Taps for one green mana per creature you control. With even 3-4 creatures, provides enormous mana advantage.
- **Green Sun's Zenith:** Creature toolbox that finds the right answer for any situation, from [Dryad Arbor](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Dryad+Arbor%22) on turn 1 to Craterhoof for the kill.
- **Collector Ouphe:** Shuts down all activated abilities of artifacts, devastating against [Urza's Saga](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Urza%27s+Saga%22), [Mox Opal](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Mox+Opal%22), and artifact combo decks.
- **Titania, Protector of Argoth:** Creates 5/3 tokens whenever a land goes to the graveyard, synergizing with [Wasteland](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Wasteland%22) and fetchlands.

### Historical Timeline

**2022** (tier 3, ~1%)
Green stompy/toolbox deck built around [Gaea's Cradle](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Gaea%27s+Cradle%22) and [Green Sun's Zenith](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Green+Sun%27s+Zenith%22) emerges. Uses [Elvish Reclaimer](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Elvish+Reclaimer%22), [Collector Ouphe](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Collector+Ouphe%22), and other green creatures with Cradle for explosive mana.
- [Gaea's Cradle](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Gaea%27s+Cradle%22) as mana engine
- [Green Sun's Zenith](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Green+Sun%27s+Zenith%22) toolbox
- [Elvish Reclaimer](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Elvish+Reclaimer%22) for land tutoring
- [Collector Ouphe](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Collector+Ouphe%22) as artifact hate

**2024** (tier 2, ~2%)
MH3 energy creatures ([Ocelot Pride](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Ocelot+Pride%22), etc.) can splash into Cradle builds. Some overlap with Ocelot Pride Midrange but Cradle Control focuses on the mana engine.
- MH3 creature options
- [Boseiju, Who Endures](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Boseiju%2C+Who+Endures%22) for interaction

**2026** (tier 2, ~2.3%)
Tier 2 at 2.3%. A [Gaea's Cradle](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Gaea%27s+Cradle%22)-powered creature deck that goes over the top with mana advantage.
- Refined creature toolbox
- Stable Cradle + GSZ shell

**Frequency of Change:** medium
**Change Notes:** [Once Upon a Time](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Once+Upon+a+Time%22) provided significant consistency. The Depths combo package is a flex slot some builds omit for more controlling options.

---

## Death and Taxes

**Also known as:** D&T, DnT, Yorion Death and Taxes, BW Taxes

**Archetype:** aggro
**Colors:** W, B
**Tier:** tier 2
**Meta Share:** 2%
**Win Rate Estimate:** 49-51%
**Cost Estimate:** $2,500 (driven by [Scrubland](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Scrubland%22), [Rishadan Port](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Rishadan+Port%22), [Wasteland](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Wasteland%22), [Solitude](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Solitude%22), [Stoneforge Mystic](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Stoneforge+Mystic%22))
**First Appeared:** 2012
**Peak Meta Share:** 2017-2019
**Deck Count in Sample:** 32

A white-based creature deck that disrupts opponents with [Thalia, Guardian of Thraben](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Thalia%2C+Guardian+of+Thraben%22), [Wasteland](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Wasteland%22) + [Rishadan Port](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Rishadan+Port%22) mana denial, and [Aether Vial](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Aether+Vial%22) to deploy threats at instant speed. The Yorion 80-card version with a black splash has become standard, providing more consistency in grindy matchups.

### Decklist

**Main Deck:**

- 4 [Thalia, Guardian of Thraben](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Thalia%2C+Guardian+of+Thraben%22)
- 4 [Stoneforge Mystic](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Stoneforge+Mystic%22)
- 4 [Flickerwisp](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Flickerwisp%22)
- 4 [Skyclave Apparition](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Skyclave+Apparition%22)
- 3 [Solitude](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Solitude%22)
- 3 [Archon of Emeria](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Archon+of+Emeria%22)
- 4 [Orcish Bowmasters](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Orcish+Bowmasters%22)
- 3 [Recruiter of the Guard](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Recruiter+of+the+Guard%22)
- 1 [Phyrexian Revoker](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Phyrexian+Revoker%22)
- 4 [Aether Vial](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Aether+Vial%22)
- 4 [Swords to Plowshares](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Swords+to+Plowshares%22)
- 1 [Kaldra Compleat](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Kaldra+Compleat%22)
- 1 [Batterskull](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Batterskull%22)
- 1 [Umezawa's Jitte](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Umezawa%27s+Jitte%22)

- 1 [Yorion, Sky Nomad](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Yorion%2C+Sky+Nomad%22)
- 4 [Rishadan Port](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Rishadan+Port%22)

- 1 [Swamp](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Swamp%22)
- 3 [Scrubland](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Scrubland%22)
- 1 [Godless Shrine](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Godless+Shrine%22)
- 4 [Marsh Flats](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Marsh+Flats%22)
- 2 [Flooded Strand](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Flooded+Strand%22)
- 1 [Silent Clearing](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Silent+Clearing%22)
- 1 [Eiganjo, Seat of the Empire](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Eiganjo%2C+Seat+of+the+Empire%22)
- 1 [Shizo, Death's Storehouse](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Shizo%2C+Death%27s+Storehouse%22)

**Sideboard:**

- 1 [Yorion, Sky Nomad](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Yorion%2C+Sky+Nomad%22)

- 2 [Containment Priest](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Containment+Priest%22)
- 2 [Mindbreak Trap](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Mindbreak+Trap%22)
- 2 [Chalice of the Void](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Chalice+of+the+Void%22)
- 1 [Torpor Orb](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Torpor+Orb%22)

- 1 [Plague Engineer](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Plague+Engineer%22)

### Key Matchups

- **Favorable:** Sneak and Show, The EPIC Storm, [Doomsday](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Doomsday%22)
- **Unfavorable:** Lands, Beanstalk Control, [Ocelot Pride](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Ocelot+Pride%22) Midrange
- **Even:** Dimir Tempo, Izzet Delver, Painter

**Similar Decks:** [Ocelot Pride](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Ocelot+Pride%22) Midrange, Maverick
Shares the white creature-based disruption plan with Maverick. [Ocelot Pride](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Ocelot+Pride%22) Midrange is the newer energy-based competitor for the non-blue aggro slot.

### Key Cards Explained

<img src="https://api.scryfall.com/cards/named?exact=Thalia%2C+Guardian+of+Thraben&format=image&version=normal&set=dka" alt="Thalia, Guardian of Thraben" width="217"> <img src="https://api.scryfall.com/cards/named?exact=Aether+Vial&format=image&version=normal&set=dst" alt="Aether Vial" width="217"> <img src="https://api.scryfall.com/cards/named?exact=Stoneforge+Mystic&format=image&version=normal&set=wwk" alt="Stoneforge Mystic" width="217">

- **Thalia, Guardian of Thraben:** Taxes noncreature spells by 1, slowing down cantrip and combo decks significantly.
- **Aether Vial:** Deploys creatures at instant speed without paying mana, circumventing Thalia's own tax and enabling tricks with [Flickerwisp](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Flickerwisp%22).
- **Stoneforge Mystic:** Tutors and cheats equipment into play. [Kaldra Compleat](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Kaldra+Compleat%22) or [Batterskull](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Batterskull%22) provides a devastating threat.
- **Yorion, Sky Nomad:** Companion that blinks permanents for value. Enables the 80-card build with extra silver bullets.
- **Orcish Bowmasters:** The black splash payoff. Punishes cantrips and provides removal.

### Historical Timeline

**2012** (tier 2, ~4%)
Death and Taxes becomes a Legacy staple as a mono-white hatebear deck. [Thalia, Guardian of Thraben](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Thalia%2C+Guardian+of+Thraben%22) from Dark Ascension is the signature card, taxing the cantrip-heavy format. [Aether Vial](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Aether+Vial%22) provides tempo.
- [Thalia, Guardian of Thraben](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Thalia%2C+Guardian+of+Thraben%22) as format-defining hatebear
- [Aether Vial](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Aether+Vial%22) for tempo
- [Rishadan Port](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Rishadan+Port%22) + [Wasteland](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Wasteland%22) mana denial
- [Stoneforge Mystic](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Stoneforge+Mystic%22) + [Batterskull](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Batterskull%22)/Jitte

**2014** (tier 2, ~4%)
Consistent tier 2 presence. Spirit of the Labyrinth from Born of the Gods added as [Brainstorm](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Brainstorm%22) hoser.
- Spirit of the Labyrinth added
- [Recruiter of the Guard](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Recruiter+of+the+Guard%22) for toolbox access

**2017** (tier 1, ~6%)
Top ban guts Miracles, and D&T benefits from less [Terminus](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Terminus%22) in the format. Rises in meta share as one of the best fair decks.
- Benefits from Miracles decline
- Less [Terminus](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Terminus%22) means creatures survive better

**2019** (tier 2, ~3%)
[Once Upon a Time](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Once+Upon+a+Time%22) briefly legal. [Palace Jailer](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Palace+Jailer%22) provides card advantage. Steady performer through multiple metagame shifts.
- [Palace Jailer](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Palace+Jailer%22) for card advantage
- Gideon, Ally of Zendikar in some builds

**2020** (tier 2, ~3%)
[Yorion, Sky Nomad](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Yorion%2C+Sky+Nomad%22) companion explored in 80-card builds. [Skyclave Apparition](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Skyclave+Apparition%22) adds flexible removal.
- Yorion companion 80-card builds experimented with
- [Skyclave Apparition](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Skyclave+Apparition%22) as removal creature

**2023** (tier 2, ~2.5%)
[Orcish Bowmasters](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Orcish+Bowmasters%22) pushes some builds toward BW (Orzhov). Bowmasters is excellent in the shell, and [Plague Engineer](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Plague+Engineer%22) was already played. [Grief](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Grief%22) adds disruption.
- BW/Orzhov builds with [Orcish Bowmasters](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Orcish+Bowmasters%22)
- [Grief](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Grief%22) for hand disruption
- Mono-white and BW builds coexist

**2026** (tier 2, ~2.0%)
Tier 2 at 2.0%. Adapts to every meta but never dominates. One of Legacy's most beloved and enduring fair decks.
- Both mono-W and BW builds viable
- Stable Thalia + Vial + Stoneforge core

**Frequency of Change:** high
**Change Notes:** The shift to 80-card Yorion with black splash for [Orcish Bowmasters](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Orcish+Bowmasters%22) and [Thoughtseize](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Thoughtseize%22) was the biggest change. The deck constantly adapts its creature suite to the metagame.

---

## Omni-Tell

**Also known as:** OmniTell, [Omniscience](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Omniscience%22) Show, Show and Omni

**Archetype:** combo
**Colors:** U
**Tier:** tier 2
**Meta Share:** 1.7%
**Win Rate Estimate:** 49-51%
**Cost Estimate:** $1,800 (driven by [Force of Will](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Force+of+Will%22), [Ancient Tomb](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Ancient+Tomb%22), [Omniscience](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Omniscience%22))
**First Appeared:** 2013
**Peak Meta Share:** 2015-2016
**Deck Count in Sample:** 27

A combo deck that uses [Show and Tell](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Show+and+Tell%22) to put [Omniscience](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Omniscience%22) into play, then casts free spells to win the game with [Cunning Wish](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Cunning+Wish%22) into [Release the Ants](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Release+the+Ants%22) or simply casting Emrakul. More resilient than Sneak and Show against creature removal but more vulnerable to enchantment removal.

### Decklist

**Main Deck:**

- 4 [Show and Tell](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Show+and+Tell%22)
- 4 [Omniscience](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Omniscience%22)
- 2 [Emrakul, the Aeons Torn](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Emrakul%2C+the+Aeons+Torn%22)
- 4 [Cunning Wish](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Cunning+Wish%22)
- 4 [Brainstorm](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Brainstorm%22)
- 4 [Ponder](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Ponder%22)
- 3 [Preordain](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Preordain%22)
- 4 [Force of Will](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Force+of+Will%22)
- 2 [Spell Pierce](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Spell+Pierce%22)
- 2 [Daze](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Daze%22)
- 3 [Veil of Summer](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Veil+of+Summer%22)
- 4 [Lotus Petal](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Lotus+Petal%22)
- 4 [Polluted Delta](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Polluted+Delta%22)
- 2 [Scalding Tarn](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Scalding+Tarn%22)
- 2 [Flooded Strand](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Flooded+Strand%22)
- 6 [Island](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Island%22)
- 3 [Ancient Tomb](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Ancient+Tomb%22)
- 3 [Misty Rainforest](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Misty+Rainforest%22)

**Sideboard:**

- 1 [Release the Ants](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Release+the+Ants%22)
- 2 [Flusterstorm](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Flusterstorm%22)
- 2 [Surgical Extraction](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Surgical+Extraction%22)
- 2 [Hydroblast](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Hydroblast%22)
- 1 [Trickbind](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Trickbind%22)
- 2 [Subtlety](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Subtlety%22)
- 1 [Wipe Away](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Wipe+Away%22)
- 1 [Firemind's Foresight](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Firemind%27s+Foresight%22)
- 1 [Pact of Negation](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Pact+of+Negation%22)
- 1 [Chain of Vapor](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Chain+of+Vapor%22)
- 1 [Echoing Truth](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Echoing+Truth%22)

### Key Matchups

- **Favorable:** Lands, [Ocelot Pride](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Ocelot+Pride%22) Midrange, Eldrazi
- **Unfavorable:** Dimir Tempo, Death and Taxes, Painter
- **Even:** Sneak and Show, The EPIC Storm, Izzet Delver

**Similar Decks:** Sneak and Show
Both use [Show and Tell](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Show+and+Tell%22) as the combo enabler but diverge on the payoff: [Omniscience](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Omniscience%22) vs [Sneak Attack](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Sneak+Attack%22). Omni-Tell is more all-in on the enchantment plan.

### Key Cards Explained

<img src="https://api.scryfall.com/cards/named?exact=Omniscience&format=image&version=normal&set=m13" alt="Omniscience" width="217"> <img src="https://api.scryfall.com/cards/named?exact=Cunning+Wish&format=image&version=normal&set=jud" alt="Cunning Wish" width="217"> <img src="https://api.scryfall.com/cards/named?exact=Release+the+Ants&format=image&version=normal&set=mor" alt="Release the Ants" width="217">

- **Omniscience:** Allows casting all spells for free. Once in play, chain [Cunning Wish](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Cunning+Wish%22) into the winning combo or just cast Emrakul.
- **Cunning Wish:** With [Omniscience](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Omniscience%22) in play, tutors for the win condition from the sideboard.
- **Release the Ants:** Win condition with [Omniscience](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Omniscience%22): clash repeatedly, always winning since Emrakul has the highest MV, dealing infinite damage.

### Historical Timeline

**2013** (tier 2, ~2%)
Omni-Tell splits from Sneak and Show, focusing on [Show and Tell](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Show+and+Tell%22) into [Omniscience](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Omniscience%22) rather than [Sneak Attack](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Sneak+Attack%22). Casts Emrakul for free or uses [Cunning Wish](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Cunning+Wish%22) to chain spells.
- [Omniscience](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Omniscience%22) as primary [Show and Tell](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Show+and+Tell%22) target
- [Cunning Wish](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Cunning+Wish%22) for silver bullets
- [Release the Ants](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Release+the+Ants%22) / Emrakul as win conditions

**2015** (tier 2, ~2.5%)
Dig Through Time briefly makes Omni-Tell insane before being banned. The deck could consistently find combo pieces. Remains viable after the ban.
- Dig Through Time briefly incredible (then banned)
- Deck adjusts post-ban

**2019** (tier 2, ~1.5%)
[Thassa's Oracle](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Thassa%27s+Oracle%22) win condition simplifies some builds. [Omniscience](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Omniscience%22) + Oracle + cantrips is cleaner than older wins.
- [Thassa's Oracle](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Thassa%27s+Oracle%22) as cleaner win condition
- Cantrip-heavy build for Oracle

**2026** (tier 2, ~1.7%)
Tier 2 at 1.7%. Exists alongside Sneak and Show as the slower but more resilient [Show and Tell](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Show+and+Tell%22) variant.
- Stable combo core
- Competes with Sneak and Show for players

**Frequency of Change:** low
**Change Notes:** Very stable combo. The [Cunning Wish](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Cunning+Wish%22) targets in the sideboard rotate based on metagame. [Veil of Summer](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Veil+of+Summer%22) is a key recent addition for protection.

---

## Mono Black Midrange

**Also known as:** Mono Black Control, MBC, The Gate

**Archetype:** midrange
**Colors:** B
**Tier:** tier 2
**Meta Share:** 1.3%
**Win Rate Estimate:** 49-51%
**Cost Estimate:** $1,500 (driven by [Wasteland](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Wasteland%22), [Chrome Mox](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Chrome+Mox%22), [Grief](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Grief%22), [Urza's Saga](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Urza%27s+Saga%22))
**First Appeared:** 2023
**Peak Meta Share:** 2025-2026
**Deck Count in Sample:** 20

A mono-black midrange deck leveraging the power of [Orcish Bowmasters](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Orcish+Bowmasters%22), [Sheoldred, the Apocalypse](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Sheoldred%2C+the+Apocalypse%22), and discard-based disruption. Eschews blue cantrips for a more consistent mana base and powerful black staples. Uses [Urza's Saga](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Urza%27s+Saga%22) and [Dark Ritual](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Dark+Ritual%22) for acceleration.

### Decklist

**Main Deck:**

- 4 [Orcish Bowmasters](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Orcish+Bowmasters%22)
- 3 [Sheoldred, the Apocalypse](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Sheoldred%2C+the+Apocalypse%22)
- 4 [Grief](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Grief%22)
- 2 [Tourach, Dread Cantor](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Tourach%2C+Dread+Cantor%22)
- 1 [Archon of Cruelty](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Archon+of+Cruelty%22)
- 4 [Thoughtseize](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Thoughtseize%22)
- 4 [Hymn to Tourach](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Hymn+to+Tourach%22)
- 4 [Dark Ritual](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Dark+Ritual%22)
- 2 [Snuff Out](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Snuff+Out%22)
- 2 [Fatal Push](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Fatal+Push%22)
- 3 [Reanimate](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Reanimate%22)
- 1 [Animate Dead](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Animate+Dead%22)
- 4 [Lotus Petal](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Lotus+Petal%22)
- 2 [Chrome Mox](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Chrome+Mox%22)
- 3 [Urza's Saga](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Urza%27s+Saga%22)
- 9 [Swamp](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Swamp%22)
- 4 [Wasteland](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Wasteland%22)
- 2 [Mishra's Factory](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Mishra%27s+Factory%22)
- 1 [Witch Cottage](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Witch+Cottage%22)
- 1 [Shadowspear](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Shadowspear%22)

**Sideboard:**

- 2 [Surgical Extraction](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Surgical+Extraction%22)
- 2 [Leyline of the Void](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Leyline+of+the+Void%22)
- 2 [Torpor Orb](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Torpor+Orb%22)
- 2 [Plague Engineer](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Plague+Engineer%22)
- 2 [Sheoldred's Edict](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Sheoldred%27s+Edict%22)
- 2 [Chalice of the Void](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Chalice+of+the+Void%22)
- 1 [Nihil Spellbomb](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Nihil+Spellbomb%22)
- 1 [Pithing Needle](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Pithing+Needle%22)
- 1 [Ensnaring Bridge](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Ensnaring+Bridge%22)

### Key Matchups

- **Favorable:** Izzet Delver, Beanstalk Control, Jeskai Control
- **Unfavorable:** Sneak and Show, Oops! All Spells, Lands
- **Even:** Dimir Tempo, [Ocelot Pride](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Ocelot+Pride%22) Midrange, Painter

**Similar Decks:** Dimir Tempo, [Death's Shadow](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Death%27s+Shadow%22)
Shares the black disruption core of Dimir Tempo but trades blue cantrips for more raw power and a simpler mana base. A more midrange approach than Dimir Tempo's tempo plan.

### Key Cards Explained

<img src="https://api.scryfall.com/cards/named?exact=Grief&format=image&version=normal&set=mh2" alt="Grief" width="217"> <img src="https://api.scryfall.com/cards/named?exact=Sheoldred%2C+the+Apocalypse&format=image&version=normal&set=dmu" alt="Sheoldred, the Apocalypse" width="217"> <img src="https://api.scryfall.com/cards/named?exact=Hymn+to+Tourach&format=image&version=normal&set=fem" alt="Hymn to Tourach" width="217">

- **Grief:** Evoked on turn 1 with [Reanimate](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Reanimate%22) provides a discard effect plus a 3/2 menace body, recreating the Scam strategy.
- **Sheoldred, the Apocalypse:** Gains life when you draw and drains opponent when they draw. Punishes blue cantrips mercilessly.
- **Hymn to Tourach:** Random discard of two cards for BB. One of the most powerful disruption spells in the format.
- **Reanimate:** Brings back [Grief](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Grief%22), [Archon of Cruelty](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Archon+of+Cruelty%22), or stolen creatures for just 1 mana.

### Historical Timeline

**2023** (tier 2, ~1.5%)
Mono-Black Midrange / Scam decks emerge using [Grief](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Grief%22) + [Reanimate](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Reanimate%22) for turn-1 disruption alongside [Orcish Bowmasters](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Orcish+Bowmasters%22) and [Sheoldred, the Apocalypse](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Sheoldred%2C+the+Apocalypse%22).
- [Grief](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Grief%22) + [Reanimate](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Reanimate%22) package
- [Orcish Bowmasters](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Orcish+Bowmasters%22)
- [Sheoldred, the Apocalypse](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Sheoldred%2C+the+Apocalypse%22)
- [Dark Ritual](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Dark+Ritual%22) for explosive starts

**2024** (tier 2, ~1.5%)
[Necrodominance](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Necrodominance%22) from MH3 provides a Necropotence-like card advantage engine. Some builds incorporate it.
- [Necrodominance](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Necrodominance%22) as card advantage engine
- Refined threat suite

**2026** (tier 2, ~1.3%)
Tier 2 at 1.3%. A pure black disruption deck that leverages the best black cards in the format.
- Stable mono-B shell
- [Tourach, Dread Cantor](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Tourach%2C+Dread+Cantor%22) and other black threats

**Frequency of Change:** medium
**Change Notes:** Bowmasters and Sheoldred made mono-black viable. The reanimation package ([Grief](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Grief%22) + [Reanimate](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Reanimate%22)) gives explosive starts. Still a relatively new archetype being refined.

---

## Aluren

**Also known as:** [Aluren](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Aluren%22) Combo, BUG Aluren

**Archetype:** combo
**Colors:** B, U, G
**Tier:** tier 2
**Meta Share:** 1.2%
**Win Rate Estimate:** 49-51%
**Cost Estimate:** $3,200 (driven by [Underground Sea](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Underground+Sea%22), [Tropical Island](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Tropical+Island%22), [Bayou](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Bayou%22), [Force of Will](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Force+of+Will%22))
**First Appeared:** 2004
**Peak Meta Share:** 2013-2014
**Deck Count in Sample:** 19

A combo deck built around the enchantment [Aluren](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Aluren%22), which allows creatures with MV 3 or less to be cast for free at instant speed. Combines with [Acererak the Archlich](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Acererak+the+Archlich%22) to repeatedly venture into the dungeon, draining the opponent's life to zero with Tomb of Annihilation.

### Decklist

**Main Deck:**

- 4 [Aluren](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Aluren%22)
- 3 [Acererak the Archlich](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Acererak+the+Archlich%22)
- 4 [Orcish Bowmasters](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Orcish+Bowmasters%22)
- 3 [Ice-Fang Coatl](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Ice-Fang+Coatl%22)
- 2 [Endurance](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Endurance%22)
- 1 [Collector Ouphe](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Collector+Ouphe%22)
- 4 [Brainstorm](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Brainstorm%22)
- 4 [Ponder](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Ponder%22)
- 4 [Force of Will](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Force+of+Will%22)
- 4 [Thoughtseize](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Thoughtseize%22)
- 2 [Green Sun's Zenith](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Green+Sun%27s+Zenith%22)
- 2 [Abrupt Decay](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Abrupt+Decay%22)
- 1 [Dryad Arbor](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Dryad+Arbor%22)
- 4 [Polluted Delta](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Polluted+Delta%22)
- 4 [Misty Rainforest](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Misty+Rainforest%22)
- 2 [Verdant Catacombs](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Verdant+Catacombs%22)
- 3 [Underground Sea](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Underground+Sea%22)
- 1 [Tropical Island](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Tropical+Island%22)
- 2 [Bayou](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Bayou%22)
- 1 [Island](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Island%22)
- 1 [Forest](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Forest%22)
- 2 [Wasteland](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Wasteland%22)
- 1 [Boseiju, Who Endures](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Boseiju%2C+Who+Endures%22)
- 1 [Cavern of Souls](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Cavern+of+Souls%22)

**Sideboard:**

- 2 [Flusterstorm](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Flusterstorm%22)
- 2 [Surgical Extraction](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Surgical+Extraction%22)
- 2 [Veil of Summer](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Veil+of+Summer%22)
- 1 [Hydroblast](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Hydroblast%22)
- 2 [Plague Engineer](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Plague+Engineer%22)
- 1 [Force of Negation](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Force+of+Negation%22)
- 1 [Massacre](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Massacre%22)
- 1 [Leovold, Emissary of Trest](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Leovold%2C+Emissary+of+Trest%22)
- 2 [Carpet of Flowers](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Carpet+of+Flowers%22)
- 1 [Nihil Spellbomb](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Nihil+Spellbomb%22)

### Key Matchups

- **Favorable:** Lands, Eldrazi, Death and Taxes
- **Unfavorable:** Dimir Tempo, Red Stompy, Painter
- **Even:** Sneak and Show, [Ocelot Pride](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Ocelot+Pride%22) Midrange, The EPIC Storm

**Similar Decks:** Cradle Control, Sultai Tempo
Shares the BUG shell and some creature overlap with Sultai Tempo. The GSZ package is similar to Cradle Control but aimed at finding combo pieces.

### Key Cards Explained

<img src="https://api.scryfall.com/cards/named?exact=Aluren&format=image&version=normal&set=tmp" alt="Aluren" width="217"> <img src="https://api.scryfall.com/cards/named?exact=Acererak+the+Archlich&format=image&version=normal&set=afr" alt="Acererak the Archlich" width="217"> <img src="https://api.scryfall.com/cards/named?exact=Ice-Fang+Coatl&format=image&version=normal&set=mh1" alt="Ice-Fang Coatl" width="217">

- **Aluren:** Enchantment that lets both players cast creatures with MV 3 or less for free. Enables the combo.
- **Acererak the Archlich:** With [Aluren](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Aluren%22), cast for free, ventures into dungeon, bounces to hand if you haven't completed Tomb of Annihilation. Repeat for infinite drain.
- **Ice-Fang Coatl:** Flash deathtouch creature that draws a card. Excellent with [Aluren](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Aluren%22) and provides interaction.
- **Cavern of Souls:** Names Zombie for Acererak, ensuring the combo piece resolves through countermagic.

### Historical Timeline

**2004** (tier 3, ~1%)
[Aluren](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Aluren%22) combo deck exists in early Legacy, using the enchantment Aluren to cast creatures for free and generate infinite loops with [Cavern Harpy](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Cavern+Harpy%22).
- [Aluren](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Aluren%22) as combo engine
- [Cavern Harpy](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Cavern+Harpy%22) + [Imperial Recruiter](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Imperial+Recruiter%22) loop
- Parasitic Strix / Dream Stalker for win

**2013** (tier 2, ~1.5%)
[Deathrite Shaman](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Deathrite+Shaman%22) era. BUG [Aluren](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Aluren%22) lists use DRS and other value creatures alongside the combo. [True-Name Nemesis](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22True-Name+Nemesis%22) gives a fair plan B.
- [Deathrite Shaman](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Deathrite+Shaman%22) in BUG shell
- [True-Name Nemesis](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22True-Name+Nemesis%22) as backup plan

**2018** (tier 3, ~0.5%)
DRS ban hurts the deck's fair game plan. [Aluren](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Aluren%22) adapts but loses a key mana creature.
- [Deathrite Shaman](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Deathrite+Shaman%22) banned
- Rebuilds around other value creatures

**2023** (tier 2, ~1%)
[Orcish Bowmasters](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Orcish+Bowmasters%22) can be cast for free off [Aluren](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Aluren%22), adding removal to the creature combo shell. Deck gets a resurgence.
- [Orcish Bowmasters](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Orcish+Bowmasters%22) free off [Aluren](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Aluren%22)
- Renewed interest from combo-control players

**2026** (tier 2, ~1.2%)
Tier 2 at 1.2%. A unique creature combo deck with a loyal player base and the ability to play a fair game.
- Stable combo shell
- Bowmasters enhances interaction

**Frequency of Change:** low
**Change Notes:** [Acererak the Archlich](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Acererak+the+Archlich%22) from AFR was a transformative addition, providing a compact infinite combo with [Aluren](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Aluren%22). Previous versions used more complex loops with [Cavern Harpy](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Cavern+Harpy%22).

---

## Blue Artifacts

**Also known as:** Urza Artifacts, UB Artifacts, Emry Artifacts

**Archetype:** midrange
**Colors:** U, B
**Tier:** tier 2
**Meta Share:** 1.1%
**Win Rate Estimate:** 49-51%
**Cost Estimate:** $2,800 (driven by [Underground Sea](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Underground+Sea%22), [Force of Will](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Force+of+Will%22), [Mox Opal](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Mox+Opal%22))
**First Appeared:** 2023
**Peak Meta Share:** 2024-2025
**Deck Count in Sample:** 17

A blue-black artifact deck that combines [Thought Monitor](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Thought+Monitor%22), [Emry, Lurker of the Loch](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Emry%2C+Lurker+of+the+Loch%22), and [Urza's Saga](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Urza%27s+Saga%22) to create an artifact-synergy midrange strategy backed by blue countermagic. More interactive than pure Affinity builds.

### Decklist

**Main Deck:**

- 4 [Thought Monitor](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Thought+Monitor%22)
- 4 [Emry, Lurker of the Loch](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Emry%2C+Lurker+of+the+Loch%22)
- 3 [Orcish Bowmasters](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Orcish+Bowmasters%22)
- 4 [Force of Will](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Force+of+Will%22)
- 4 [Brainstorm](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Brainstorm%22)
- 2 [Thoughtseize](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Thoughtseize%22)
- 4 [Mox Opal](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Mox+Opal%22)
- 4 [Lotus Petal](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Lotus+Petal%22)
- 4 [Mishra's Bauble](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Mishra%27s+Bauble%22)
- 2 [Cranial Plating](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Cranial+Plating%22)
- 1 [Nettlecyst](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Nettlecyst%22)
- 4 [Springleaf Drum](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Springleaf+Drum%22)
- 1 [Shadowspear](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Shadowspear%22)
- 4 [Urza's Saga](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Urza%27s+Saga%22)
- 3 [Polluted Delta](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Polluted+Delta%22)
- 2 [Underground Sea](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Underground+Sea%22)
- 1 [Island](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Island%22)
- 3 [Seat of the Synod](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Seat+of+the+Synod%22)
- 3 [Darksteel Citadel](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Darksteel+Citadel%22)
- 2 [Wasteland](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Wasteland%22)
- 1 [Retrofitter Foundry](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Retrofitter+Foundry%22)

**Sideboard:**

- 2 [Flusterstorm](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Flusterstorm%22)
- 2 [Surgical Extraction](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Surgical+Extraction%22)
- 2 [Hydroblast](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Hydroblast%22)
- 1 [Nihil Spellbomb](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Nihil+Spellbomb%22)
- 1 [Pithing Needle](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Pithing+Needle%22)
- 1 [Ratchet Bomb](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Ratchet+Bomb%22)
- 0 [Null Rod](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Null+Rod%22)
- 2 [Dismember](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Dismember%22)
- 2 [Plague Engineer](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Plague+Engineer%22)
- 1 [Force of Negation](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Force+of+Negation%22)
- 1 [Haywire Mite](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Haywire+Mite%22)

### Key Matchups

- **Favorable:** Izzet Delver, Beanstalk Control, Jeskai Control
- **Unfavorable:** [Ocelot Pride](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Ocelot+Pride%22) Midrange, Cradle Control, Painter
- **Even:** Dimir Tempo, Sneak and Show, Eldrazi

**Similar Decks:** Affinity Stompy, [Mystic Forge](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Mystic+Forge%22) Combo
Shares the artifact creature base with Affinity Stompy but adds blue interaction. Less combo-focused than [Mystic Forge](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Mystic+Forge%22) but more resilient.

### Key Cards Explained

<img src="https://api.scryfall.com/cards/named?exact=Emry%2C+Lurker+of+the+Loch&format=image&version=normal&set=eld" alt="Emry, Lurker of the Loch" width="217"> <img src="https://api.scryfall.com/cards/named?exact=Thought+Monitor&format=image&version=normal&set=mh2" alt="Thought Monitor" width="217"> <img src="https://api.scryfall.com/cards/named?exact=Mox+Opal&format=image&version=normal&set=som" alt="Mox Opal" width="217">

- **Emry, Lurker of the Loch:** Costs as little as U with enough artifacts. Recurs artifacts from the graveyard each turn, providing incredible value.
- **Thought Monitor:** Draws two cards for as little as U when you have enough artifacts. The deck's premier card advantage.
- **Mox Opal:** Free mana that enables explosive starts and is recurrable with Emry.

### Historical Timeline

**2023** (tier 3, ~0.5%)
Blue-based artifact combo-control deck emerges using [Emry, Lurker of the Loch](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Emry%2C+Lurker+of+the+Loch%22), [Urza's Saga](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Urza%27s+Saga%22), and various artifact synergies. Blue provides [Force of Will](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Force+of+Will%22) backup.
- [Emry, Lurker of the Loch](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Emry%2C+Lurker+of+the+Loch%22) as engine
- [Urza's Saga](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Urza%27s+Saga%22) for tutoring and threats
- [Force of Will](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Force+of+Will%22) for protection
- [Mishra's Bauble](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Mishra%27s+Bauble%22) and artifact cantrips

**2024** (tier 2, ~1%)
MH3 artifact support helps the deck. Refines into a more consistent strategy.
- MH3 artifact additions
- Improved combo consistency

**2026** (tier 2, ~1.1%)
Tier 2 at 1.1%. A niche artifact strategy that leverages blue permission alongside artifact synergies.
- Optimized artifact shell
- Stable blue + artifacts core

**Frequency of Change:** medium
**Change Notes:** Relatively new archetype combining the best of artifact aggro with blue interaction. Emry provides recursion that pure Affinity lacks.

---

## LED Dredge

**Also known as:** Dredge, Manaless Dredge, [Lion's Eye Diamond](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Lion%27s+Eye+Diamond%22) Dredge

**Archetype:** combo
**Colors:** B, R, G
**Tier:** tier 2
**Meta Share:** 1.1%
**Win Rate Estimate:** 49-51%
**Cost Estimate:** $1,200 (driven by [Lion's Eye Diamond](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Lion%27s+Eye+Diamond%22), [Force of Will](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Force+of+Will%22), [Cephalid Coliseum](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Cephalid+Coliseum%22))
**First Appeared:** 2009
**Peak Meta Share:** 2016-2017
**Deck Count in Sample:** 17

A graveyard combo deck that uses the dredge mechanic to fill its graveyard, then wins with [Narcomoeba](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Narcomoeba%22), [Bridge from Below](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Bridge+from+Below%22), and [Dread Return](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Dread+Return%22) into a win condition. [Lion's Eye Diamond](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Lion%27s+Eye+Diamond%22) enables explosive starts by providing mana while filling the graveyard.

### Decklist

**Main Deck:**

- 4 [Golgari Grave-Troll](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Golgari+Grave-Troll%22)
- 4 [Stinkweed Imp](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Stinkweed+Imp%22)
- 3 [Golgari Thug](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Golgari+Thug%22)
- 1 [Shambling Shell](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Shambling+Shell%22)
- 4 [Narcomoeba](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Narcomoeba%22)
- 4 [Ichorid](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Ichorid%22)
- 2 [Silversmote Ghoul](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Silversmote+Ghoul%22)
- 1 [Ashen Rider](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Ashen+Rider%22)
- 1 [Thassa's Oracle](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Thassa%27s+Oracle%22)
- 4 [Bridge from Below](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Bridge+from+Below%22)
- 3 [Dread Return](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Dread+Return%22)
- 4 [Faithless Looting](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Faithless+Looting%22)
- 3 [Careful Study](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Careful+Study%22)
- 4 [Lion's Eye Diamond](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Lion%27s+Eye+Diamond%22)
- 4 [Lotus Petal](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Lotus+Petal%22)
- 2 [Breakthrough](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Breakthrough%22)
- 4 [Cephalid Coliseum](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Cephalid+Coliseum%22)
- 3 [Gemstone Mine](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Gemstone+Mine%22)
- 2 [City of Brass](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22City+of+Brass%22)
- 1 [Mana Confluence](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Mana+Confluence%22)
- 1 [Undiscovered Paradise](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Undiscovered+Paradise%22)
- 1 [Takenuma, Abandoned Mire](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Takenuma%2C+Abandoned+Mire%22)

**Sideboard:**

- 4 [Force of Will](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Force+of+Will%22)
- 2 [Mindbreak Trap](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Mindbreak+Trap%22)
- 2 [Chain of Vapor](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Chain+of+Vapor%22)
- 2 [Nature's Claim](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Nature%27s+Claim%22)
- 3 [Grief](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Grief%22)
- 2 [Flusterstorm](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Flusterstorm%22)

### Key Matchups

- **Favorable:** Beanstalk Control, Jeskai Control, Lands
- **Unfavorable:** Dimir Tempo, Red Stompy, [Ocelot Pride](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Ocelot+Pride%22) Midrange
- **Even:** Sneak and Show, Oops! All Spells, Eldrazi

**Similar Decks:** Oops! All Spells
Both are graveyard combo decks using [Narcomoeba](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Narcomoeba%22) and [Dread Return](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Dread+Return%22), but Dredge is more resilient and grindy while Oops is faster and more fragile.

### Key Cards Explained

<img src="https://api.scryfall.com/cards/named?exact=Golgari+Grave-Troll&format=image&version=normal&set=rav" alt="Golgari Grave-Troll" width="217"> <img src="https://api.scryfall.com/cards/named?exact=Bridge+from+Below&format=image&version=normal&set=fut" alt="Bridge from Below" width="217"> <img src="https://api.scryfall.com/cards/named?exact=Lion%27s+Eye+Diamond&format=image&version=normal&set=mir" alt="Lion's Eye Diamond" width="217">

- **Golgari Grave-Troll:** Dredge 6 is the highest dredge count, milling six cards each time you would draw. Fills the graveyard rapidly.
- **Bridge from Below:** Creates zombie tokens whenever a creature you control dies, provided it's in your graveyard. Powers the [Dread Return](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Dread+Return%22) chain.
- **Lion's Eye Diamond:** Discarding your hand feeds dredge cards into the graveyard while providing 3 mana for [Faithless Looting](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Faithless+Looting%22) flashback.
- **Ichorid:** Recurs from the graveyard each turn for free, providing sacrifice fodder and triggering [Bridge from Below](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Bridge+from+Below%22).

### Historical Timeline

**2009** (tier 2, ~3%)
LED Dredge establishes itself as Legacy's premier graveyard deck. Uses [Lion's Eye Diamond](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Lion%27s+Eye+Diamond%22) to enable dredge cards, [Narcomoeba](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Narcomoeba%22), [Ichorid](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Ichorid%22), and [Bridge from Below](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Bridge+from+Below%22) for an army of zombies.
- [Lion's Eye Diamond](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Lion%27s+Eye+Diamond%22) enables Dredge
- [Golgari Grave-Troll](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Golgari+Grave-Troll%22), [Stinkweed Imp](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Stinkweed+Imp%22) as dredgers
- [Narcomoeba](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Narcomoeba%22), [Ichorid](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Ichorid%22), [Bridge from Below](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Bridge+from+Below%22) as payoffs
- [Cabal Therapy](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Cabal+Therapy%22) for disruption

**2013** (tier 3, ~1%)
[Deathrite Shaman](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Deathrite+Shaman%22) everywhere is devastating for Dredge. Incidental graveyard hate on a maindeckable creature crushes the strategy.
- [Deathrite Shaman](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Deathrite+Shaman%22) makes graveyard strategies much worse
- Deck struggles in DRS meta

**2018** (tier 2, ~3%)
DRS ban is hugely positive for Dredge. Creeping Chill from Guilds of Ravnica adds free damage from the graveyard. Deck surges.
- DRS ban removes mainboard hate
- Creeping Chill adds free damage

**2021** (tier 2, ~2%)
[Endurance](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Endurance%22) from MH2 is a devastating hate card — instant-speed graveyard shuffle. Deck takes a hit.
