- [Endurance](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Endurance%22) as major new hate card
- Deck adapts with more resilience

**2023** (tier 2, ~1.5%)
[Orcish Bowmasters](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Orcish+Bowmasters%22) incidentally punishes some Dredge plays. [Surgical Extraction](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Surgical+Extraction%22) and other hate remain widespread.
- Adapts to Bowmasters meta
- Consistent but not dominant

**2026** (tier 2, ~1.1%)
Tier 2 at 1.1%. Graveyard hate keeps it in check, but the raw power of dredging remains formidable against unprepared opponents.
- Stable dredge core
- Adapts threat suite to current hate

### Bans Impact

- **Gitaxian Probe** (2018-07): Lost a free cantrip that helped enable turn-1 kills. Reduced consistency slightly.

**Frequency of Change:** low
**Change Notes:** Very stable core. [Silversmote Ghoul](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Silversmote+Ghoul%22) was a meaningful addition. [Thassa's Oracle](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Thassa%27s+Oracle%22) provides a backup win condition. The deck adapts primarily through its sideboard.

---

## Jeskai Control

**Also known as:** UWR Control, Jeskai Miracles

**Archetype:** control
**Colors:** U, W, R
**Tier:** tier 3
**Meta Share:** 0.9%
**Win Rate Estimate:** 49-51%
**Cost Estimate:** $3,800 (driven by [Volcanic Island](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Volcanic+Island%22), [Tundra](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Tundra%22), [Underground Sea](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Underground+Sea%22), [Force of Will](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Force+of+Will%22))
**First Appeared:** 2017
**Peak Meta Share:** 2018-2019
**Deck Count in Sample:** 14

A traditional three-color control deck using countermagic, removal, and card advantage to grind opponents out. The spiritual successor to Miracles after the [Sensei's Divining Top](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Sensei%27s+Divining+Top%22) ban, now using [Monastery Mentor](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Monastery+Mentor%22) or [Entreat the Angels](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Entreat+the+Angels%22) as win conditions alongside efficient Jeskai interaction.

### Decklist

**Main Deck:**

- 4 [Brainstorm](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Brainstorm%22)
- 4 [Ponder](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Ponder%22)
- 4 [Force of Will](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Force+of+Will%22)
- 4 [Swords to Plowshares](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Swords+to+Plowshares%22)
- 4 [Lightning Bolt](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Lightning+Bolt%22)
- 3 [Prismatic Ending](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Prismatic+Ending%22)
- 3 [Counterspell](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Counterspell%22)
- 1 [Spell Pierce](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Spell+Pierce%22)
- 2 [Monastery Mentor](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Monastery+Mentor%22)
- 2 [Orcish Bowmasters](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Orcish+Bowmasters%22)
- 3 [Snapcaster Mage](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Snapcaster+Mage%22)
- 1 [Narset, Parter of Veils](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Narset%2C+Parter+of+Veils%22)
- 2 [Terminus](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Terminus%22)
- 1 [Entreat the Angels](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Entreat+the+Angels%22)
- 2 [Shark Typhoon](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Shark+Typhoon%22)
- 4 [Polluted Delta](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Polluted+Delta%22)
- 4 [Flooded Strand](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Flooded+Strand%22)
- 2 [Scalding Tarn](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Scalding+Tarn%22)
- 2 [Volcanic Island](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Volcanic+Island%22)
- 2 [Tundra](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Tundra%22)
- 1 [Underground Sea](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Underground+Sea%22)
- 2 [Island](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Island%22)
- 1 [Plains](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Plains%22)
- 1 [Mystic Sanctuary](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Mystic+Sanctuary%22)
- 1 [Otawara, Soaring City](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Otawara%2C+Soaring+City%22)

**Sideboard:**

- 2 [Flusterstorm](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Flusterstorm%22)
- 2 [Pyroblast](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Pyroblast%22)
- 1 [Hydroblast](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Hydroblast%22)
- 2 [Surgical Extraction](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Surgical+Extraction%22)
- 2 [Containment Priest](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Containment+Priest%22)
- 2 [Veil of Summer](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Veil+of+Summer%22)
- 1 [Force of Negation](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Force+of+Negation%22)
- 1 [Terminus](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Terminus%22)
- 1 [Blood Moon](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Blood+Moon%22)
- 1 [Wear // Tear](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Wear+//+Tear%22)

### Key Matchups

- **Favorable:** Lands, LED Dredge, Death and Taxes
- **Unfavorable:** Dimir Tempo, Painter, Mono Black Midrange
- **Even:** Sneak and Show, [Ocelot Pride](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Ocelot+Pride%22) Midrange, Izzet Delver

**Similar Decks:** Beanstalk Control
Beanstalk Control is the four-color evolution of this strategy. Jeskai Control is leaner and more focused on countermagic over Beanstalk card advantage.

### Key Cards Explained

<img src="https://api.scryfall.com/cards/named?exact=Monastery+Mentor&format=image&version=normal&set=frf" alt="Monastery Mentor" width="217"> <img src="https://api.scryfall.com/cards/named?exact=Terminus&format=image&version=normal&set=avr" alt="Terminus" width="217"> <img src="https://api.scryfall.com/cards/named?exact=Snapcaster+Mage&format=image&version=normal&set=isd" alt="Snapcaster Mage" width="217">

- **Monastery Mentor:** Creates monk tokens on every noncreature spell, turning cantrips into a lethal army.
- **Terminus:** Miracle for W puts all creatures on the bottom of libraries. Devastating board wipe that can be set up with [Brainstorm](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Brainstorm%22).
- **Snapcaster Mage:** Recurs any instant or sorcery from the graveyard, providing flexibility and card advantage.

### Historical Timeline

**2017** (tier 2, ~3%)
After [Sensei's Divining Top](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Sensei%27s+Divining+Top%22) ban guts Miracles, UW/Jeskai Control rebuilds without the [Counterbalance](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Counterbalance%22)-Top lock. Slower but more traditional control approach with [Snapcaster Mage](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Snapcaster+Mage%22), Jace, and Supreme Verdict.
- Rebuilds from Miracles shell post-Top ban
- [Snapcaster Mage](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Snapcaster+Mage%22) + [Jace, the Mind Sculptor](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Jace%2C+the+Mind+Sculptor%22)
- [Terminus](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Terminus%22) still playable via [Brainstorm](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Brainstorm%22)
- Search for Azcanta as card advantage

**2020** (tier 2, ~2%)
[Shark Typhoon](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Shark+Typhoon%22) provides a flexible win condition. [Uro, Titan of Nature's Wrath](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Uro%2C+Titan+of+Nature%27s+Wrath%22) in Bant or 4c versions. Jeskai with [Pyroblast](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Pyroblast%22) preferred by some.
- [Shark Typhoon](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Shark+Typhoon%22) as uncounterable win condition
- [Pyroblast](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Pyroblast%22) for blue mirrors

**2023** (tier 2, ~1.5%)
Competes with Beanstalk Control for the control slot. Jeskai offers [Pyroblast](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Pyroblast%22) and [Lightning Bolt](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Lightning+Bolt%22) but Beanstalk offers more raw card advantage.
- Competes with Beanstalk Control
- [Day's Undoing](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Day%27s+Undoing%22) experimented with
- [Monastery Mentor](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Monastery+Mentor%22) as threat

**2026** (tier 3, ~0.9%)
Tier 3 at 0.9%. Still viable but overshadowed by Beanstalk Control as the control deck of choice.
- Stable UWR control shell
- Niche pick for [Pyroblast](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Pyroblast%22) access

### Bans Impact

- **Sensei's Divining Top** (2017-04): Ended the Miracles era. The deck evolved from [Counterbalance](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Counterbalance%22)/Top lock to a more traditional control build.

**Frequency of Change:** medium
**Change Notes:** Has been somewhat eclipsed by Beanstalk Control as the control deck of choice. Remains viable for players who prefer a tighter mana base.

---

## Selesnya Depths

**Also known as:** GW Depths, Turbo Depths, Depths Combo

**Archetype:** combo
**Colors:** G, W
**Tier:** tier 3
**Meta Share:** 0.8%
**Win Rate Estimate:** 49-51%
**Cost Estimate:** $2,400 (driven by [Mox Diamond](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Mox+Diamond%22), [Savannah](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Savannah%22), [Dark Depths](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Dark+Depths%22))
**First Appeared:** 2015
**Peak Meta Share:** 2019-2020
**Deck Count in Sample:** 13

A combo deck focused on assembling [Dark Depths](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Dark+Depths%22) + [Thespian's Stage](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Thespian%27s+Stage%22) as quickly as possible using [Crop Rotation](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Crop+Rotation%22), [Elvish Reclaimer](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Elvish+Reclaimer%22), and [Knight of the Reliquary](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Knight+of+the+Reliquary%22). The GW version adds [Swords to Plowshares](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Swords+to+Plowshares%22) and Knight toolbox over the older BG version.

### Decklist

**Main Deck:**

- 4 [Elvish Reclaimer](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Elvish+Reclaimer%22)
- 4 [Knight of the Reliquary](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Knight+of+the+Reliquary%22)
- 1 [Dryad Arbor](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Dryad+Arbor%22)
- 2 [Endurance](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Endurance%22)
- 1 [Sylvan Safekeeper](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Sylvan+Safekeeper%22)
- 4 [Crop Rotation](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Crop+Rotation%22)
- 3 [Green Sun's Zenith](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Green+Sun%27s+Zenith%22)
- 4 [Swords to Plowshares](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Swords+to+Plowshares%22)
- 4 [Once Upon a Time](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Once+Upon+a+Time%22)
- 4 [Mox Diamond](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Mox+Diamond%22)
- 2 [Sylvan Library](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Sylvan+Library%22)
- 4 [Dark Depths](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Dark+Depths%22)
- 4 [Thespian's Stage](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Thespian%27s+Stage%22)
- 4 [Windswept Heath](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Windswept+Heath%22)
- 1 [Verdant Catacombs](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Verdant+Catacombs%22)
- 3 [Savannah](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Savannah%22)
- 3 [Forest](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Forest%22)
- 2 [Plains](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Plains%22)
- 1 [Yavimaya, Cradle of Growth](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Yavimaya%2C+Cradle+of+Growth%22)
- 2 [Wasteland](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Wasteland%22)
- 1 [Sejiri Steppe](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Sejiri+Steppe%22)
- 1 [Karakas](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Karakas%22)
- 1 [Boseiju, Who Endures](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Boseiju%2C+Who+Endures%22)

**Sideboard:**

- 3 [Force of Vigor](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Force+of+Vigor%22)
- 2 [Mindbreak Trap](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Mindbreak+Trap%22)
- 2 [Choke](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Choke%22)
- 2 [Containment Priest](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Containment+Priest%22)
- 2 [Torpor Orb](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Torpor+Orb%22)
- 1 [Collector Ouphe](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Collector+Ouphe%22)
- 1 [Reclamation Sage](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Reclamation+Sage%22)
- 1 [Pithing Needle](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Pithing+Needle%22)
- 1 [Surgical Extraction](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Surgical+Extraction%22)

### Key Matchups

- **Favorable:** Dimir Tempo, Izzet Delver, Beanstalk Control
- **Unfavorable:** Sneak and Show, Oops! All Spells, Painter
- **Even:** [Ocelot Pride](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Ocelot+Pride%22) Midrange, Lands, Death and Taxes

**Similar Decks:** Lands, Maverick, Cradle Control
Shares the Depths combo with Lands but in a more aggressive creature-based shell. Shares the GW creature toolbox with Maverick.

### Key Cards Explained

<img src="https://api.scryfall.com/cards/named?exact=Dark+Depths&format=image&version=normal&set=csp" alt="Dark Depths" width="217"> <img src="https://api.scryfall.com/cards/named?exact=Crop+Rotation&format=image&version=normal&set=usg" alt="Crop Rotation" width="217"> <img src="https://api.scryfall.com/cards/named?exact=Knight+of+the+Reliquary&format=image&version=normal&set=con" alt="Knight of the Reliquary" width="217">

- **Dark Depths:** Combines with [Thespian's Stage](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Thespian%27s+Stage%22) for a 20/20 flying indestructible token as early as turn 2.
- **Crop Rotation:** Instant-speed land tutor that finds [Dark Depths](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Dark+Depths%22) or [Thespian's Stage](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Thespian%27s+Stage%22) at the cost of sacrificing a land.
- **Knight of the Reliquary:** Tutors lands including combo pieces. Grows larger as lands enter the graveyard from fetches and sacrifices.
- **Sejiri Steppe:** Fetched by Knight to give Marit Lage protection from a color, ensuring the 20/20 connects.

### Historical Timeline

**2015** (tier 2, ~2%)
GW Depths focuses on the [Dark Depths](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Dark+Depths%22) + [Thespian's Stage](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Thespian%27s+Stage%22) combo with [Knight of the Reliquary](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Knight+of+the+Reliquary%22) as a land tutor and backup threat. [Green Sun's Zenith](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Green+Sun%27s+Zenith%22) toolbox.
- [Dark Depths](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Dark+Depths%22) + [Thespian's Stage](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Thespian%27s+Stage%22) combo
- [Knight of the Reliquary](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Knight+of+the+Reliquary%22) as tutor/threat
- [Green Sun's Zenith](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Green+Sun%27s+Zenith%22) toolbox
- [Crop Rotation](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Crop+Rotation%22) for speed

**2018** (tier 2, ~2%)
DRS ban helps the deck. Ramunap Excavator provides additional land recursion and [Wasteland](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Wasteland%22) synergy.
- DRS ban removes hate and competition
- Ramunap Excavator for [Wasteland](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Wasteland%22) recursion

**2021** (tier 2, ~1.5%)
[Yavimaya, Cradle of Growth](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Yavimaya%2C+Cradle+of+Growth%22) from MH2 makes the Depths combo easier to assemble — all lands become Forests for [Crop Rotation](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Crop+Rotation%22).
- [Yavimaya, Cradle of Growth](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Yavimaya%2C+Cradle+of+Growth%22) enables easier combo
- [Endurance](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Endurance%22) as pitch card

**2023** (tier 3, ~1%)
Competes with Lands for the land-combo slot. GW Depths is faster but less grindy.
- Competes with Lands archetype
- [Boseiju, Who Endures](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Boseiju%2C+Who+Endures%22) for interaction

**2026** (tier 3, ~0.8%)
Tier 3 at 0.8%. A focused [Dark Depths](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Dark+Depths%22) combo deck that rewards knowledge of the format's mana bases.
- Stable combo shell
- Occasional [Abrupt Decay](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Abrupt+Decay%22) splash for BG Depths

**Frequency of Change:** low
**Change Notes:** The shift from BG to GW happened gradually as [Swords to Plowshares](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Swords+to+Plowshares%22) and [Knight of the Reliquary](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Knight+of+the+Reliquary%22) proved more impactful. [Once Upon a Time](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Once+Upon+a+Time%22) added consistency.

---

## Sultai Tempo

**Also known as:** BUG Tempo, Sultai Delver, BUG Delver

**Archetype:** tempo
**Colors:** B, U, G
**Tier:** tier 3
**Meta Share:** 0.5%
**Win Rate Estimate:** 49-51%
**Cost Estimate:** $4,200 (driven by [Underground Sea](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Underground+Sea%22), [Tropical Island](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Tropical+Island%22), [Bayou](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Bayou%22), [Force of Will](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Force+of+Will%22))
**First Appeared:** 2013
**Peak Meta Share:** 2019-2020
**Deck Count in Sample:** 8

A three-color tempo deck that adds green to the UB shell for [Uro, Titan of Nature's Wrath](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Uro%2C+Titan+of+Nature%27s+Wrath%22) and [Endurance](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Endurance%22). Slightly grindier than Dimir Tempo with better long-game potential but a less consistent mana base.

### Decklist

**Main Deck:**

- 4 [Brainstorm](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Brainstorm%22)
- 4 [Ponder](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Ponder%22)
- 4 [Force of Will](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Force+of+Will%22)
- 4 [Daze](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Daze%22)
- 4 [Thoughtseize](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Thoughtseize%22)
- 2 [Fatal Push](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Fatal+Push%22)
- 2 [Abrupt Decay](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Abrupt+Decay%22)
- 4 [Orcish Bowmasters](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Orcish+Bowmasters%22)
- 4 [Tamiyo, Inquisitive Student](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Tamiyo%2C+Inquisitive+Student%22)
- 3 [Uro, Titan of Nature's Wrath](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Uro%2C+Titan+of+Nature%27s+Wrath%22)
- 2 [Endurance](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Endurance%22)
- 2 [Murktide Regent](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Murktide+Regent%22)
- 4 [Polluted Delta](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Polluted+Delta%22)
- 4 [Misty Rainforest](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Misty+Rainforest%22)
- 3 [Underground Sea](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Underground+Sea%22)
- 3 [Tropical Island](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Tropical+Island%22)
- 4 [Wasteland](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Wasteland%22)
- 1 [Island](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Island%22)
- 1 [Bayou](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Bayou%22)
- 1 [Swamp](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Swamp%22)

**Sideboard:**

- 2 [Surgical Extraction](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Surgical+Extraction%22)
- 2 [Hydroblast](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Hydroblast%22)
- 2 [Flusterstorm](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Flusterstorm%22)
- 1 [Force of Negation](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Force+of+Negation%22)
- 2 [Plague Engineer](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Plague+Engineer%22)
- 2 [Veil of Summer](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Veil+of+Summer%22)
- 1 [Nihil Spellbomb](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Nihil+Spellbomb%22)
- 1 [Sylvan Library](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Sylvan+Library%22)
- 1 [Massacre](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Massacre%22)
- 1 [Dismember](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Dismember%22)

### Key Matchups

- **Favorable:** Beanstalk Control, Lands, Jeskai Control
- **Unfavorable:** [Ocelot Pride](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Ocelot+Pride%22) Midrange, Red Stompy, Eldrazi
- **Even:** Dimir Tempo, Sneak and Show, Painter

**Similar Decks:** Dimir Tempo, [Aluren](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Aluren%22)
Essentially Dimir Tempo with a green splash. Trades mana consistency for Uro's grinding power and [Endurance](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Endurance%22) as graveyard hate.

### Key Cards Explained

<img src="https://api.scryfall.com/cards/named?exact=Uro%2C+Titan+of+Nature%27s+Wrath&format=image&version=normal&set=thb" alt="Uro, Titan of Nature's Wrath" width="217"> <img src="https://api.scryfall.com/cards/named?exact=Endurance&format=image&version=normal&set=mh2" alt="Endurance" width="217"> <img src="https://api.scryfall.com/cards/named?exact=Abrupt+Decay&format=image&version=normal&set=rtr" alt="Abrupt Decay" width="217">

- **Uro, Titan of Nature's Wrath:** The primary reason to splash green. Provides life, card draw, and ramp, then escapes as a 6/6 that does it all again.
- **Endurance:** Flash creature that shuffles graveyards, providing hate against Dredge, Reanimator, and [Doomsday](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Doomsday%22).
- **Abrupt Decay:** Uncounterable removal for permanents CMC 3 or less. Hits [Chalice of the Void](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Chalice+of+the+Void%22), [Blood Moon](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Blood+Moon%22), and most threats.

### Historical Timeline

**2013** (tier 1, ~10%)
BUG Delver rises to tier 1 with [Deathrite Shaman](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Deathrite+Shaman%22). Combines Delver, DRS, [Tarmogoyf](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Tarmogoyf%22), [True-Name Nemesis](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22True-Name+Nemesis%22) with [Abrupt Decay](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Abrupt+Decay%22), [Force of Will](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Force+of+Will%22), and [Hymn to Tourach](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Hymn+to+Tourach%22). The best deck in Legacy for several years.
- [Deathrite Shaman](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Deathrite+Shaman%22) as mana creature + graveyard hate + win condition
- [True-Name Nemesis](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22True-Name+Nemesis%22) from Commander 2013
- [Abrupt Decay](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Abrupt+Decay%22) for uncounterable removal
- [Hymn to Tourach](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Hymn+to+Tourach%22) for disruption

**2016** (tier 1, ~8%)
BUG Delver remains one of the two best decks alongside Miracles. DRS + [Wasteland](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Wasteland%22) + [Daze](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Daze%22) is the defining tempo shell.
- Core stable
- [Leovold, Emissary of Trest](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Leovold%2C+Emissary+of+Trest%22) added (then banned 2017)

**2018** (tier 3, ~1%)
[Deathrite Shaman](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Deathrite+Shaman%22) BANNED (July). BUG Delver completely collapses without its best card. Players scatter to RUG Delver and other shells.
- DRS ban devastates the archetype
- Most players switch to other Delver variants

**2023** (tier 3, ~0.5%)
[Orcish Bowmasters](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Orcish+Bowmasters%22) gives black a reason to exist in tempo again, but Dimir Tempo (UB) is preferred over BUG (adding green for Uro).
- UB Dimir Tempo preferred over BUG
- Some BUG lists with [Uro, Titan of Nature's Wrath](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Uro%2C+Titan+of+Nature%27s+Wrath%22)

**2026** (tier 3, ~0.5%)
Tier 3 at 0.5%. Niche option for players who want Uro alongside the UB tempo shell.
- Uro as key green reason
- Otherwise similar to Dimir Tempo

### Bans Impact

- **Oko, Thief of Crowns** (2020-03): Lost one of the best reasons to play green in a tempo shell. Contributed to the decline of Sultai builds.

**Frequency of Change:** medium
**Change Notes:** Has been largely supplanted by straight Dimir Tempo, which has a cleaner mana base. Green splash is only worthwhile if Uro and [Endurance](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Endurance%22) are particularly well positioned.

---

## Death's Shadow

**Also known as:** Shadow, Grixis Shadow, Dimir Shadow

**Archetype:** tempo
**Colors:** U, B, R
**Tier:** tier 3
**Meta Share:** 0.5%
**Win Rate Estimate:** 49-51%
**Cost Estimate:** $3,200 (driven by [Underground Sea](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Underground+Sea%22), [Force of Will](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Force+of+Will%22), [Wasteland](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Wasteland%22), [Polluted Delta](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Polluted+Delta%22))
**First Appeared:** 2020
**Peak Meta Share:** 2021-2022
**Deck Count in Sample:** 8

An aggressive tempo deck built around [Death's Shadow](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Death%27s+Shadow%22) as a massive undercosted threat. Uses fetchlands, [Watery Grave](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Watery+Grave%22), and other life-payment cards to reduce its own life total, making Shadow a 1-mana 8/8 or larger. Combines with the standard blue-black disruption package.

### Decklist

**Main Deck:**

- 4 [Death's Shadow](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Death%27s+Shadow%22)
- 4 [Orcish Bowmasters](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Orcish+Bowmasters%22)
- 2 [Murktide Regent](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Murktide+Regent%22)
- 4 [Tamiyo, Inquisitive Student](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Tamiyo%2C+Inquisitive+Student%22)
- 4 [Brainstorm](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Brainstorm%22)
- 4 [Ponder](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Ponder%22)
- 4 [Force of Will](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Force+of+Will%22)
- 4 [Daze](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Daze%22)
- 4 [Thoughtseize](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Thoughtseize%22)
- 2 [Snuff Out](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Snuff+Out%22)
- 2 [Street Wraith](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Street+Wraith%22)
- 2 [Reanimate](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Reanimate%22)
- 4 [Polluted Delta](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Polluted+Delta%22)
- 3 [Bloodstained Mire](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Bloodstained+Mire%22)
- 3 [Underground Sea](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Underground+Sea%22)
- 2 [Watery Grave](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Watery+Grave%22)
- 4 [Wasteland](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Wasteland%22)
- 1 [Island](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Island%22)
- 1 [Swamp](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Swamp%22)
- 1 [Spell Pierce](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Spell+Pierce%22)
- 1 [Fatal Push](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Fatal+Push%22)

**Sideboard:**

- 2 [Surgical Extraction](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Surgical+Extraction%22)
- 2 [Hydroblast](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Hydroblast%22)
- 2 [Flusterstorm](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Flusterstorm%22)
- 1 [Force of Negation](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Force+of+Negation%22)
- 2 [Plague Engineer](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Plague+Engineer%22)
- 1 [Nihil Spellbomb](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Nihil+Spellbomb%22)
- 2 [Dismember](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Dismember%22)
- 1 [Sheoldred's Edict](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Sheoldred%27s+Edict%22)
- 1 [Subtlety](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Subtlety%22)
- 1 [Stern Scolding](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Stern+Scolding%22)

### Key Matchups

- **Favorable:** Sneak and Show, Beanstalk Control, Jeskai Control
- **Unfavorable:** [Ocelot Pride](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Ocelot+Pride%22) Midrange, Red Stompy, Lands
- **Even:** Dimir Tempo, Izzet Delver, The EPIC Storm

**Similar Decks:** Dimir Tempo
Very close to Dimir Tempo but trades some consistency for the explosive power of [Death's Shadow](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Death%27s+Shadow%22). The life-payment theme makes the deck more aggressive but riskier.

### Key Cards Explained

<img src="https://api.scryfall.com/cards/named?exact=Death%27s+Shadow&format=image&version=normal&set=wwk" alt="Death's Shadow" width="217"> <img src="https://api.scryfall.com/cards/named?exact=Snuff+Out&format=image&version=normal&set=mmq" alt="Snuff Out" width="217"> <img src="https://api.scryfall.com/cards/named?exact=Street+Wraith&format=image&version=normal&set=fut" alt="Street Wraith" width="217">

- **Death's Shadow:** Gets bigger as your life total gets lower. At 7 life, it's a 1-mana 6/6. Fetchlands and [Thoughtseize](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Thoughtseize%22) naturally lower your life.
- **Snuff Out:** Free removal that costs 4 life, which is actually a benefit since it grows [Death's Shadow](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Death%27s+Shadow%22).
- **Street Wraith:** Cycles for 2 life, replacing itself while shrinking your life total for Shadow.
- **Reanimate:** Brings back Shadow or Bowmasters from the graveyard while paying life to fuel Shadow.

### Historical Timeline

**2020** (tier 3, ~0.5%)
[Death's Shadow](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Death%27s+Shadow%22) decks appear in Legacy, translating from Modern. Uses the format's free spells, fetchlands, and [Thoughtseize](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Thoughtseize%22) to fuel a cheap, massive threat.
- [Death's Shadow](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Death%27s+Shadow%22) as undercosted threat
- [Thoughtseize](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Thoughtseize%22) + fetchlands + Force for life payment
- Dimir or Grixis builds

**2021** (tier 3, ~1%)
MH2 gives [Dragon's Rage Channeler](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Dragon%27s+Rage+Channeler%22) and [Murktide Regent](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Murktide+Regent%22), which fit perfectly in the same shell. Grixis [Death's Shadow](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Death%27s+Shadow%22) gains power.
- DRC and Murktide alongside Shadow
- Grixis builds become standard

**2023** (tier 3, ~0.5%)
Bowmasters in Dimir Shadow is excellent. The UB shell is essentially Dimir Tempo with [Death's Shadow](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Death%27s+Shadow%22) as the payoff threat.
- [Orcish Bowmasters](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Orcish+Bowmasters%22) in UB Shadow
- Overlaps heavily with Dimir Tempo

**2026** (tier 3, ~0.5%)
Tier 3 at 0.5%. A more aggressive variant of the Dimir Tempo shell for players who like the Shadow playstyle.
- Dimir Shadow shell
- More aggressive than standard Dimir Tempo

**Frequency of Change:** medium
**Change Notes:** Has been largely absorbed into the broader Dimir Tempo category. Players who run Shadow tend to be specialists. [Reanimate](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Reanimate%22) adds a secondary plan of rebuying large threats.

---

## Infect

**Also known as:** UG Infect, Simic Infect

**Archetype:** aggro
**Colors:** U, G
**Tier:** tier 3
**Meta Share:** 0.4%
**Win Rate Estimate:** 49-51%
**Cost Estimate:** $2,200 (driven by [Tropical Island](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Tropical+Island%22), [Force of Will](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Force+of+Will%22), [Berserk](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Berserk%22))
**First Appeared:** 2011
**Peak Meta Share:** 2015-2016
**Deck Count in Sample:** 6

An aggressive combo-aggro deck that wins by dealing 10 poison counters using infect creatures pumped with free spells like [Invigorate](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Invigorate%22) and [Berserk](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Berserk%22). Can win as early as turn 2 and rarely later than turn 4 if uninterrupted.

### Decklist

**Main Deck:**

- 4 [Glistener Elf](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Glistener+Elf%22)
- 4 [Blighted Agent](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Blighted+Agent%22)
- 4 [Inkmoth Nexus](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Inkmoth+Nexus%22)
- 4 [Brainstorm](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Brainstorm%22)
- 4 [Force of Will](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Force+of+Will%22)
- 2 [Daze](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Daze%22)
- 1 [Spell Pierce](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Spell+Pierce%22)
- 4 [Vines of Vastwood](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Vines+of+Vastwood%22)
- 4 [Invigorate](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Invigorate%22)
- 3 [Berserk](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Berserk%22)
- 2 [Become Immense](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Become+Immense%22)
- 2 [Scale Up](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Scale+Up%22)
- 2 [Crop Rotation](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Crop+Rotation%22)
- 4 [Ponder](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Ponder%22)
- 1 [Pendelhaven](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Pendelhaven%22)
- 3 [Tropical Island](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Tropical+Island%22)
- 4 [Windswept Heath](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Windswept+Heath%22)
- 3 [Misty Rainforest](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Misty+Rainforest%22)
- 2 [Wasteland](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Wasteland%22)
- 3 [Forest](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Forest%22)

**Sideboard:**

- 2 [Flusterstorm](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Flusterstorm%22)
- 2 [Surgical Extraction](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Surgical+Extraction%22)
- 2 [Veil of Summer](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Veil+of+Summer%22)
- 1 [Force of Negation](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Force+of+Negation%22)
- 2 [Submerge](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Submerge%22)
- 2 [Hydroblast](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Hydroblast%22)
- 1 [Sylvan Library](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Sylvan+Library%22)
- 1 [Karakas](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Karakas%22)
- 2 [Endurance](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Endurance%22)

### Key Matchups

- **Favorable:** Sneak and Show, The EPIC Storm, [Doomsday](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Doomsday%22)
- **Unfavorable:** Dimir Tempo, [Ocelot Pride](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Ocelot+Pride%22) Midrange, Izzet Delver
- **Even:** Lands, Painter, Red Stompy

**Similar Decks:** Elves
Both are green creature-based aggro decks that can win quickly. Infect is more combo-oriented while Elves is more synergy-driven.

### Key Cards Explained

<img src="https://api.scryfall.com/cards/named?exact=Invigorate&format=image&version=normal&set=mmq" alt="Invigorate" width="217"> <img src="https://api.scryfall.com/cards/named?exact=Berserk&format=image&version=normal&set=lea" alt="Berserk" width="217"> <img src="https://api.scryfall.com/cards/named?exact=Blighted+Agent&format=image&version=normal&set=nph" alt="Blighted Agent" width="217">

- **Invigorate:** Free +4/+4 that enables turn-2 kills. The life gain to the opponent doesn't matter when you win with poison.
- **Berserk:** Doubles a creature's power for G. Combined with infect, this creates lethal damage on tiny investments.
- **Blighted Agent:** Unblockable infect creature. With any pump spell, represents a fast clock that can't be blocked.
- **Vines of Vastwood:** Dual-purpose card that protects creatures from removal and pumps them for +4/+4 when kicked.

### Historical Timeline

**2011** (tier 2, ~3%)
Infect emerges in Legacy with [Glistener Elf](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Glistener+Elf%22), [Blighted Agent](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Blighted+Agent%22), and [Invigorate](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Invigorate%22) (free pump spell). Can kill on turn 2. Uses [Brainstorm](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Brainstorm%22), [Force of Will](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Force+of+Will%22), and [Daze](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Daze%22) for protection.
- [Glistener Elf](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Glistener+Elf%22) and [Blighted Agent](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Blighted+Agent%22) as infect threats
- [Invigorate](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Invigorate%22) as free pump
- [Berserk](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Berserk%22) for massive damage
- [Noble Hierarch](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Noble+Hierarch%22) for exalted

**2013** (tier 2, ~2%)
DRS era is tough for Infect as the format has more incidental interaction. Deck remains viable but not dominant.
- [Deathrite Shaman](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Deathrite+Shaman%22) adds blockers everywhere
- Deck remains fast enough to compete

**2018** (tier 2, ~1.5%)
DRS ban removes a common roadblock. Gitaxian Probe ban hurts information gathering. Mixed impact.
- DRS ban positive
- Gitaxian Probe ban negative
- Net neutral impact

**2021** (tier 3, ~0.5%)
MH2 threats make other decks more efficient. Infect struggles against [Murktide Regent](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Murktide+Regent%22) and [Dragon's Rage Channeler](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Dragon%27s+Rage+Channeler%22).
- Faces more efficient threats
- Deck speed still relevant vs combo

**2026** (tier 3, ~0.4%)
Tier 3 at 0.4%. A glass cannon that can steal games but struggles in the Bowmasters era.
- Bowmasters punishes small creatures
- Still capable of turn-2 kills

### Bans Impact

- **Gitaxian Probe** (2018-07): Lost perfect information before going all-in on the combo turn. Reduced the deck's ability to play around removal.

**Frequency of Change:** low
**Change Notes:** [Scale Up](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Scale+Up%22) from MH1 was the last major addition. The deck is extremely stable but struggles against the prevalence of [Orcish Bowmasters](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Orcish+Bowmasters%22).

---

## Burn

**Also known as:** Mono Red Burn, Red Burn, [Mountain](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Mountain%22) Go

**Archetype:** aggro
**Colors:** R
**Tier:** fringe
**Meta Share:** 0.3%
**Win Rate Estimate:** 48-50%
**Cost Estimate:** $400 (driven by [Fiery Islet](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Fiery+Islet%22), [Sunbaked Canyon](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Sunbaked+Canyon%22), [Eidolon of the Great Revel](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Eidolon+of+the+Great+Revel%22))
**First Appeared:** 1993
**Peak Meta Share:** 2014-2015
**Deck Count in Sample:** 4

The oldest archetype in Magic. Aims to deal 20 damage to the opponent using direct damage spells as quickly as possible. Budget-friendly and straightforward but struggles against the format's efficient answers and life gain.

### Decklist

**Main Deck:**

- 4 [Goblin Guide](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Goblin+Guide%22)
- 4 [Monastery Swiftspear](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Monastery+Swiftspear%22)
- 4 [Eidolon of the Great Revel](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Eidolon+of+the+Great+Revel%22)
- 4 [Lightning Bolt](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Lightning+Bolt%22)
- 4 [Chain Lightning](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Chain+Lightning%22)
- 4 [Lava Spike](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Lava+Spike%22)
- 4 [Rift Bolt](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Rift+Bolt%22)
- 4 [Price of Progress](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Price+of+Progress%22)
- 4 [Fireblast](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Fireblast%22)
- 2 [Skullcrack](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Skullcrack%22)
- 2 [Searing Blaze](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Searing+Blaze%22)
- 10 [Mountain](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Mountain%22)
- 2 [Barbarian Ring](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Barbarian+Ring%22)
- 4 [Fiery Islet](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Fiery+Islet%22)
- 4 [Sunbaked Canyon](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Sunbaked+Canyon%22)

**Sideboard:**

- 3 [Smash to Smithereens](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Smash+to+Smithereens%22)
- 2 [Ensnaring Bridge](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Ensnaring+Bridge%22)
- 2 [Roiling Vortex](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Roiling+Vortex%22)
- 2 [Grafdigger's Cage](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Grafdigger%27s+Cage%22)
- 2 [Searing Blood](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Searing+Blood%22)
- 2 [Exquisite Firecraft](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Exquisite+Firecraft%22)
- 2 [Pyroblast](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Pyroblast%22)

### Key Matchups

- **Favorable:** The EPIC Storm, [Doomsday](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Doomsday%22), Oops! All Spells
- **Unfavorable:** Death and Taxes, [Ocelot Pride](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Ocelot+Pride%22) Midrange, Beanstalk Control
- **Even:** Izzet Delver, Dimir Tempo, Eldrazi

**Similar Decks:** Red Stompy
Both are mono-red but take very different approaches. Burn goes face while Red Stompy locks the opponent out with prison pieces.

### Key Cards Explained

<img src="https://api.scryfall.com/cards/named?exact=Price+of+Progress&format=image&version=normal&set=exo" alt="Price of Progress" width="217"> <img src="https://api.scryfall.com/cards/named?exact=Eidolon+of+the+Great+Revel&format=image&version=normal&set=jou" alt="Eidolon of the Great Revel" width="217"> <img src="https://api.scryfall.com/cards/named?exact=Fireblast&format=image&version=normal&set=vis" alt="Fireblast" width="217">

- **Price of Progress:** Deals 2 damage per nonbasic land the opponent controls. In Legacy, most decks play 12+ nonbasics, making this 6-10 damage for 1R.
- **Eidolon of the Great Revel:** Deals 2 damage to any player who casts a spell with MV 3 or less. In Legacy, nearly every spell triggers this.
- **Fireblast:** Free 4 damage by sacrificing two Mountains. The deck's finisher that lets you tap out for other spells then [Fireblast](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Fireblast%22) for lethal.

### Historical Timeline

**1993** (tier 3, ~2%)
Burn has existed since Magic's earliest days. Mountains and Lightning Bolts. The simplest and most direct strategy in the game.
- [Lightning Bolt](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Lightning+Bolt%22), [Chain Lightning](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Chain+Lightning%22), [Fireblast](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Fireblast%22)
- [Price of Progress](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Price+of+Progress%22) punishes nonbasic lands

**2009** (tier 3, ~2%)
Modern Legacy format. Burn is a budget-friendly entry point. [Goblin Guide](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Goblin+Guide%22) from Zendikar is a major addition.
- [Goblin Guide](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Goblin+Guide%22) as efficient one-drop
- [Eidolon of the Great Revel](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Eidolon+of+the+Great+Revel%22) added later (2014)

**2014** (tier 2, ~2.5%)
[Eidolon of the Great Revel](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Eidolon+of+the+Great+Revel%22) from Journey into Nyx is perfect for Legacy where most spells cost 1-2 mana. Punishes cantrip-heavy format.
- [Eidolon of the Great Revel](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Eidolon+of+the+Great+Revel%22) as format punisher
- [Monastery Swiftspear](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Monastery+Swiftspear%22) from Khans

**2021** (tier 3, ~0.5%)
MH2 power creep makes Burn less competitive. Ragavan and Murktide decks are too efficient.
- Power creep hurts linear aggro
- Still cheap entry point to Legacy

**2023** (fringe, ~0.3%)
[Orcish Bowmasters](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Orcish+Bowmasters%22) kills [Goblin Guide](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Goblin+Guide%22) and Eidolon. Burn takes a significant hit from the most-played creature in the format.
- Bowmasters devastating against Burn's creatures
- Deck drops in viability

**2026** (fringe, ~0.3%)
Fringe at 0.3%. Still exists as an ultra-budget entry to Legacy but not competitively viable against modern threats.
- Budget option only
- Fundamentally outclassed by format power level

**Frequency of Change:** low
**Change Notes:** Extremely stable. Horizon lands ([Fiery Islet](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Fiery+Islet%22), [Sunbaked Canyon](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Sunbaked+Canyon%22)) were the last meaningful additions. The deck's power level hasn't kept pace with format upgrades.

---

## Elves

**Also known as:** Elf Combo, GW Elves, [Natural Order](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Natural+Order%22) Elves

**Archetype:** combo
**Colors:** G
**Tier:** fringe
**Meta Share:** 0.2%
**Win Rate Estimate:** 47-49%
**Cost Estimate:** $2,800 (driven by [Gaea's Cradle](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Gaea%27s+Cradle%22), [Cavern of Souls](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Cavern+of+Souls%22))
**First Appeared:** 2008
**Peak Meta Share:** 2012-2014
**Deck Count in Sample:** 3

A creature-based combo deck that uses elf tribal synergies and [Gaea's Cradle](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Gaea%27s+Cradle%22) to generate massive amounts of mana, then wins with [Craterhoof Behemoth](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Craterhoof+Behemoth%22) or [Natural Order](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Natural+Order%22). Once a format staple, now pushed to the fringes by [Orcish Bowmasters](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Orcish+Bowmasters%22) which devastates the small creature strategy.

### Decklist

**Main Deck:**

- 4 [Heritage Druid](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Heritage+Druid%22)
- 4 [Nettle Sentinel](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Nettle+Sentinel%22)
- 3 [Quirion Ranger](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Quirion+Ranger%22)
- 4 [Birchlore Rangers](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Birchlore+Rangers%22)
- 2 [Llanowar Elves](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Llanowar+Elves%22)
- 4 [Elvish Visionary](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Elvish+Visionary%22)
- 3 [Wirewood Symbiote](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Wirewood+Symbiote%22)
- 3 [Dwynen's Elite](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Dwynen%27s+Elite%22)
- 1 [Craterhoof Behemoth](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Craterhoof+Behemoth%22)
- 2 [Endurance](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Endurance%22)
- 1 [Collector Ouphe](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Collector+Ouphe%22)
- 1 [Reclamation Sage](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Reclamation+Sage%22)
- 1 [Dryad Arbor](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Dryad+Arbor%22)
- 4 [Green Sun's Zenith](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Green+Sun%27s+Zenith%22)
- 3 [Natural Order](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Natural+Order%22)
- 4 [Glimpse of Nature](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Glimpse+of+Nature%22)
- 3 [Gaea's Cradle](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Gaea%27s+Cradle%22)
- 4 [Windswept Heath](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Windswept+Heath%22)
- 1 [Verdant Catacombs](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Verdant+Catacombs%22)
- 4 [Forest](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Forest%22)
- 2 [Cavern of Souls](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Cavern+of+Souls%22)
- 1 [Pendelhaven](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Pendelhaven%22)
- 1 [Boseiju, Who Endures](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Boseiju%2C+Who+Endures%22)

**Sideboard:**

- 4 [Thoughtseize](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Thoughtseize%22)
- 3 [Force of Vigor](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Force+of+Vigor%22)
- 2 [Mindbreak Trap](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Mindbreak+Trap%22)
- 2 [Surgical Extraction](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Surgical+Extraction%22)
- 2 [Choke](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Choke%22)
- 2 [Torpor Orb](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Torpor+Orb%22)

### Key Matchups

- **Favorable:** Lands, Red Stompy, Selesnya Depths
- **Unfavorable:** Dimir Tempo, Izzet Delver, [Ocelot Pride](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Ocelot+Pride%22) Midrange
- **Even:** Sneak and Show, The EPIC Storm, Burn

**Similar Decks:** Cradle Control, Maverick
Shares [Gaea's Cradle](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Gaea%27s+Cradle%22) and [Green Sun's Zenith](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Green+Sun%27s+Zenith%22) with Cradle Control but is faster and more all-in on the creature combo. Many Elves players have moved to Cradle Control.

### Key Cards Explained

<img src="https://api.scryfall.com/cards/named?exact=Glimpse+of+Nature&format=image&version=normal&set=chk" alt="Glimpse of Nature" width="217"> <img src="https://api.scryfall.com/cards/named?exact=Heritage+Druid&format=image&version=normal&set=mor" alt="Heritage Druid" width="217"> <img src="https://api.scryfall.com/cards/named?exact=Natural+Order&format=image&version=normal&set=vis" alt="Natural Order" width="217">

- **Glimpse of Nature:** Draws a card for each creature cast in a turn. With [Heritage Druid](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Heritage+Druid%22) mana, chains through the deck to find Craterhoof.
- **Heritage Druid:** Taps three elves for GGG, even ones with summoning sickness. Enables explosive turns with multiple cheap elves.
- **Natural Order:** Sacrifices an elf to put [Craterhoof Behemoth](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Craterhoof+Behemoth%22) directly into play, often winning on the spot.
- **Gaea's Cradle:** With 5+ elves in play, generates enough mana for virtually anything.

### Historical Timeline

**2008** (tier 1, ~5%)
Elves combo deck emerges using [Glimpse of Nature](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Glimpse+of+Nature%22), [Heritage Druid](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Heritage+Druid%22), and [Nettle Sentinel](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Nettle+Sentinel%22) to generate massive mana and cards, finishing with [Craterhoof Behemoth](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Craterhoof+Behemoth%22) or [Natural Order](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Natural+Order%22).
- [Glimpse of Nature](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Glimpse+of+Nature%22) as draw engine
- [Heritage Druid](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Heritage+Druid%22) + [Nettle Sentinel](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Nettle+Sentinel%22) for mana
- [Natural Order](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Natural+Order%22) into [Craterhoof Behemoth](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Craterhoof+Behemoth%22)
- [Green Sun's Zenith](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Green+Sun%27s+Zenith%22) toolbox

**2012** (tier 2, ~3%)
Elves remains competitive but Miracles and [Terminus](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Terminus%22) are devastating — sweeping the board of small creatures repeatedly.
- [Terminus](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Terminus%22) from Miracles is a nightmare
- [Deathrite Shaman](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Deathrite+Shaman%22) added to BG builds

**2017** (tier 2, ~2%)
Top ban weakens Miracles, which is great for creature decks like Elves. Brief resurgence.
- Less [Terminus](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Terminus%22) in the format
- Brief uptick in viability

**2018** (tier 2, ~1.5%)
DRS ban removes a key creature from Elves builds that splashed black. Deck refocuses on mono-green.
- DRS banned from BG Elves
- Returns to mono-green builds

**2023** (fringe, ~0.3%)
[Orcish Bowmasters](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Orcish+Bowmasters%22) is catastrophic for Elves. Kills mana dorks and punishes [Glimpse of Nature](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Glimpse+of+Nature%22) draws. Deck drops to fringe.
- Bowmasters kills every creature in the deck
- Glimpse draws trigger Bowmasters
- Deck nearly unplayable in Bowmasters meta

**2026** (fringe, ~0.2%)
Fringe at 0.2%. Bowmasters has essentially killed the archetype. Elves players have largely migrated to Cradle Control or [Ocelot Pride](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Ocelot+Pride%22) Midrange.
- Nearly extinct due to Bowmasters
- Players migrated to other green decks

### Bans Impact

- **Deathrite Shaman** (2018-07): Lost a key one-drop that provided mana fixing and utility. Significantly weakened the deck.

**Frequency of Change:** low
**Change Notes:** [Orcish Bowmasters](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Orcish+Bowmasters%22) has been devastating for this archetype. A single Bowmasters trigger off [Glimpse of Nature](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Glimpse+of+Nature%22) can wipe the board. The deck persists through dedicated pilots but is far from its former glory.

---

## Maverick

**Also known as:** GW Maverick, Abzan Maverick, Punishing Maverick

**Archetype:** midrange
**Colors:** G, W
**Tier:** fringe
**Meta Share:** 0.2%
**Win Rate Estimate:** 47-49%
**Cost Estimate:** $2,800 (driven by [Gaea's Cradle](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Gaea%27s+Cradle%22), [Savannah](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Savannah%22), [Wasteland](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Wasteland%22), [Kaldra Compleat](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Kaldra+Compleat%22))
**First Appeared:** 2011
**Peak Meta Share:** 2012-2013
**Deck Count in Sample:** 3

A GW creature toolbox deck using [Green Sun's Zenith](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Green+Sun%27s+Zenith%22), [Knight of the Reliquary](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Knight+of+the+Reliquary%22), and mana denial via [Wasteland](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Wasteland%22) and Thalia. Once a premier fair deck, now largely supplanted by [Ocelot Pride](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Ocelot+Pride%22) Midrange and Death and Taxes as the non-blue creature strategy of choice.

### Decklist

**Main Deck:**

- 4 [Green Sun's Zenith](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Green+Sun%27s+Zenith%22)
- 4 [Knight of the Reliquary](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Knight+of+the+Reliquary%22)
- 4 [Thalia, Guardian of Thraben](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Thalia%2C+Guardian+of+Thraben%22)
- 4 [Noble Hierarch](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Noble+Hierarch%22)
- 1 [Dryad Arbor](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Dryad+Arbor%22)
- 4 [Stoneforge Mystic](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Stoneforge+Mystic%22)
- 2 [Endurance](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Endurance%22)
- 1 [Collector Ouphe](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Collector+Ouphe%22)
- 1 [Scavenging Ooze](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Scavenging+Ooze%22)
- 2 [Elvish Reclaimer](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Elvish+Reclaimer%22)
- 4 [Swords to Plowshares](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Swords+to+Plowshares%22)
- 4 [Once Upon a Time](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Once+Upon+a+Time%22)
- 1 [Kaldra Compleat](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Kaldra+Compleat%22)
- 1 [Batterskull](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Batterskull%22)
- 1 [Umezawa's Jitte](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Umezawa%27s+Jitte%22)
- 4 [Wasteland](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Wasteland%22)
- 4 [Windswept Heath](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Windswept+Heath%22)
- 1 [Verdant Catacombs](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Verdant+Catacombs%22)
- 3 [Savannah](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Savannah%22)
- 3 [Forest](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Forest%22)
- 1 [Plains](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Plains%22)
- 1 [Karakas](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Karakas%22)
- 1 [Yavimaya, Cradle of Growth](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Yavimaya%2C+Cradle+of+Growth%22)
- 1 [Boseiju, Who Endures](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Boseiju%2C+Who+Endures%22)
- 1 [Dark Depths](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Dark+Depths%22)
- 1 [Thespian's Stage](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Thespian%27s+Stage%22)
- 1 [Gaea's Cradle](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Gaea%27s+Cradle%22)

**Sideboard:**

- 3 [Force of Vigor](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Force+of+Vigor%22)
- 2 [Mindbreak Trap](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Mindbreak+Trap%22)
- 2 [Choke](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Choke%22)
- 2 [Containment Priest](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Containment+Priest%22)
- 2 [Torpor Orb](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Torpor+Orb%22)
- 2 [Surgical Extraction](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Surgical+Extraction%22)
- 1 [Reclamation Sage](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Reclamation+Sage%22)
- 1 [Pithing Needle](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Pithing+Needle%22)

### Key Matchups

- **Favorable:** Lands, Beanstalk Control, LED Dredge
- **Unfavorable:** Sneak and Show, Dimir Tempo, Oops! All Spells
- **Even:** Death and Taxes, [Ocelot Pride](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Ocelot+Pride%22) Midrange, Izzet Delver

**Similar Decks:** [Ocelot Pride](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Ocelot+Pride%22) Midrange, Selesnya Depths, Death and Taxes
[Ocelot Pride](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Ocelot+Pride%22) Midrange has largely replaced Maverick as the non-blue creature deck of choice. Both use [Green Sun's Zenith](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Green+Sun%27s+Zenith%22) and [Swords to Plowshares](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Swords+to+Plowshares%22) in a GW shell.

### Key Cards Explained

<img src="https://api.scryfall.com/cards/named?exact=Knight+of+the+Reliquary&format=image&version=normal&set=con" alt="Knight of the Reliquary" width="217"> <img src="https://api.scryfall.com/cards/named?exact=Green+Sun%27s+Zenith&format=image&version=normal&set=mbs" alt="Green Sun's Zenith" width="217"> <img src="https://api.scryfall.com/cards/named?exact=Thalia%2C+Guardian+of+Thraben&format=image&version=normal&set=dka" alt="Thalia, Guardian of Thraben" width="217">

- **Knight of the Reliquary:** The deck's signature threat. Grows with each land in the graveyard and tutors key utility lands.
- **Green Sun's Zenith:** Versatile creature tutor that provides the right answer for any situation.
- **Thalia, Guardian of Thraben:** Taxes noncreature spells, slowing down combo and control while you attack with creatures.

### Historical Timeline

**2011** (tier 2, ~4%)
Maverick emerges as a GW(b) creature-based midrange deck using [Knight of the Reliquary](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Knight+of+the+Reliquary%22), [Green Sun's Zenith](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Green+Sun%27s+Zenith%22), and [Stoneforge Mystic](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Stoneforge+Mystic%22). A non-blue fair deck that attacks mana with [Wasteland](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Wasteland%22) and Thalia.
- [Knight of the Reliquary](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Knight+of+the+Reliquary%22) as cornerstone threat
- [Green Sun's Zenith](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Green+Sun%27s+Zenith%22) toolbox
- [Stoneforge Mystic](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Stoneforge+Mystic%22) + equipment
- [Thalia, Guardian of Thraben](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Thalia%2C+Guardian+of+Thraben%22) (2012)

**2013** (tier 2, ~3%)
[Deathrite Shaman](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Deathrite+Shaman%22) gives Abzan/Junk Maverick a powerful mana creature. Deck competes with BUG Delver for the green fair deck slot.
- [Deathrite Shaman](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Deathrite+Shaman%22) in GWB builds
- Competes with BUG Delver

**2018** (tier 2, ~2%)
DRS ban hurts Maverick but less than BUG Delver. [Knight of the Reliquary](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Knight+of+the+Reliquary%22) remains powerful. Deck continues as a solid tier 2 option.
- DRS ban is a mild negative
- Ramunap Excavator for [Wasteland](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Wasteland%22) recursion

**2021** (tier 3, ~1%)
MH2 power creep pushes creature decks down. Ragavan and Murktide outclass Maverick's threats.
- Outclassed by MH2 threats
- [Endurance](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Endurance%22) as green pitch card

**2024** (fringe, ~0.3%)
Many Maverick players migrate to [Ocelot Pride](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Ocelot+Pride%22) Midrange, which uses a similar GSZ + creatures shell but with more powerful energy threats.
- Players migrate to [Ocelot Pride](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Ocelot+Pride%22) Midrange
- Energy creatures outclass old Maverick threats

**2026** (fringe, ~0.2%)
Fringe at 0.2%. Mostly replaced by [Ocelot Pride](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Ocelot+Pride%22) Midrange, which does the GW creature strategy better.
- Functionally replaced by [Ocelot Pride](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Ocelot+Pride%22) Midrange
- Loyal pilots remain

### Bans Impact

- **Deathrite Shaman** (2018-07): Lost the best one-drop in the format that provided mana fixing, life gain, and graveyard hate. Major blow to the archetype.
- **Wrenn and Six** (2019-11 (later unbanned)): [Wrenn and Six](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Wrenn+and+Six%22) initially made the [Punishing Fire](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Punishing+Fire%22) version stronger but was banned due to its impact on the broader format.

**Frequency of Change:** low
**Change Notes:** The archetype has been in decline as newer creature strategies (Energy, Death and Taxes with Yorion) have emerged. Dedicated pilots keep it alive but it lacks a unique edge.

---

## Reanimator

**Also known as:** BR Reanimator, [Reanimate](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Reanimate%22), [Dark Ritual](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Dark+Ritual%22) Reanimator

**Archetype:** combo
**Colors:** B, R
**Tier:** tier 2
**Meta Share:** 2%
**Win Rate Estimate:** 50-52%
**Cost Estimate:** $1,800 (driven by [Badlands](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Badlands%22), [Grief](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Grief%22), [Griselbrand](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Griselbrand%22))
**First Appeared:** 1997
**Peak Meta Share:** 2022-2024
**Deck Count in Sample:** 31

A fast combo deck that puts massive creatures into the graveyard and reanimates them with spells like [Reanimate](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Reanimate%22) and [Animate Dead](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Animate+Dead%22). Post-[Entomb](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Entomb%22) ban in November 2025, the deck has adapted to use [Faithless Looting](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Faithless+Looting%22) and [Grief](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Grief%22) as discard outlets but lost significant consistency. Still capable of turn-one kills via [Dark Ritual](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Dark+Ritual%22) into Reanimate.

### Decklist

**Main Deck:**

- 4 [Reanimate](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Reanimate%22)
- 4 [Animate Dead](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Animate+Dead%22)
- 2 [Exhume](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Exhume%22)
- 4 [Dark Ritual](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Dark+Ritual%22)
- 4 [Faithless Looting](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Faithless+Looting%22)
- 4 [Thoughtseize](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Thoughtseize%22)
- 4 [Grief](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Grief%22)
- 2 [Unmask](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Unmask%22)
- 4 [Archon of Cruelty](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Archon+of+Cruelty%22)
- 2 [Atraxa, Grand Unifier](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Atraxa%2C+Grand+Unifier%22)
- 2 [Griselbrand](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Griselbrand%22)
- 2 [Chancellor of the Annex](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Chancellor+of+the+Annex%22)
- 4 [Lotus Petal](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Lotus+Petal%22)
- 2 [Badlands](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Badlands%22)
- 4 [Bloodstained Mire](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Bloodstained+Mire%22)
- 4 [Polluted Delta](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Polluted+Delta%22)
- 2 [Marsh Flats](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Marsh+Flats%22)
- 2 [Swamp](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Swamp%22)
- 1 [Mountain](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Mountain%22)
- 1 [Undercity Sewers](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Undercity+Sewers%22)
- 2 [Chrome Mox](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Chrome+Mox%22)

**Sideboard:**

- 3 [Show and Tell](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Show+and+Tell%22)
- 1 [Omniscience](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Omniscience%22)
- 1 [Emrakul, the Aeons Torn](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Emrakul%2C+the+Aeons+Torn%22)
- 2 [Serenity](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Serenity%22)
- 2 [Wear // Tear](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Wear+//+Tear%22)
- 2 [Pyroblast](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Pyroblast%22)
- 1 [Chancellor of the Annex](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Chancellor+of+the+Annex%22)
- 1 [Magus of the Moon](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Magus+of+the+Moon%22)
- 2 [Faerie Macabre](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Faerie+Macabre%22)

### Key Matchups

- **Favorable:** Lands, Beanstalk Control, Jeskai Control
- **Unfavorable:** Dimir Tempo, Death and Taxes, [Ocelot Pride](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Ocelot+Pride%22) Midrange
- **Even:** Sneak and Show, The EPIC Storm, Painter

**Similar Decks:** Oops! All Spells, [Doomsday](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Doomsday%22)
Shares the fast combo role with Oops! All Spells but is more resilient and interactive. Both aim to cheat large creatures into play quickly.

### Key Cards Explained

<img src="https://api.scryfall.com/cards/named?exact=Reanimate&format=image&version=normal&set=tmp" alt="Reanimate" width="217"> <img src="https://api.scryfall.com/cards/named?exact=Grief&format=image&version=normal&set=mh2" alt="Grief" width="217"> <img src="https://api.scryfall.com/cards/named?exact=Archon+of+Cruelty&format=image&version=normal&set=mh2" alt="Archon of Cruelty" width="217">

- **Reanimate:** One mana to return any creature from any graveyard to play. The life loss is irrelevant when reanimating [Griselbrand](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Griselbrand%22) or [Archon of Cruelty](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Archon+of+Cruelty%22).
- **Grief:** Free discard outlet that also strips the opponent's hand. Can be reanimated for value or evoked and immediately targeted with [Reanimate](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Reanimate%22).
- **Archon of Cruelty:** The primary reanimation target. Draws a card, forces a discard, removes a permanent, drains 3 life.
- **Dark Ritual:** Enables turn-one [Reanimate](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Reanimate%22) plays by providing BBB for one mana.

### Historical Timeline

**1997** (tier 2, ~2%)
Early reanimator strategies appear using [Reanimate](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Reanimate%22) and Buried Alive.
- [Reanimate](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Reanimate%22) as core card
- Buried Alive for setup

**2009** (tier 2, ~3%)
Modern Legacy format. Reanimator uses [Entomb](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Entomb%22) and [Careful Study](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Careful+Study%22) for consistent fast kills.
- [Entomb](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Entomb%22) as primary enabler
- [Careful Study](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Careful+Study%22) for discard

**2019** (tier 2, ~3%)
[Archon of Cruelty](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Archon+of+Cruelty%22) and later printings improve the reanimation targets.
- Improved targets
- [Unmask](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Unmask%22) for protection

**2023** (tier 1, ~5%)
[Grief](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Grief%22) from MH2 becomes key. Grief + [Reanimate](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Reanimate%22) is a powerful turn-one play.
- [Grief](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Grief%22) + [Reanimate](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Reanimate%22) package
- Atraxa as premium target

**2025** (tier 2, ~2%)
[Entomb](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Entomb%22) banned November 2025. Deck drops from tier 1 to tier 2. Adapts with [Faithless Looting](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Faithless+Looting%22).
- [Entomb](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Entomb%22) banned
- [Faithless Looting](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Faithless+Looting%22) as replacement
- [Show and Tell](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Show+and+Tell%22) sideboard plan

**2026** (tier 2, ~2%)
Stabilized at 2% meta share post-ban. Still capable of explosive starts but less consistent.
- Post-ban optimization
- [Faithless Looting](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Faithless+Looting%22) builds refined

### Bans Impact

- **Entomb** (2025-11): Removed the deck's primary enabler. [Entomb](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Entomb%22) was a one-mana instant-speed tutor to graveyard, enabling consistent turn-one kills. Deck dropped from tier 1 to tier 2.

**Frequency of Change:** high
**Change Notes:** The [Entomb](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Entomb%22) ban in November 2025 was devastating, removing the deck's best enabler. Lists have shifted to [Faithless Looting](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Faithless+Looting%22) and increased [Grief](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Grief%22) counts. The [Show and Tell](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Show+and+Tell%22) sideboard plan has become more important.

---

## Stoneblade

**Also known as:** UW Stoneblade, Esper Stoneblade, UWx Blade

**Archetype:** midrange
**Colors:** U, W
**Tier:** tier 3
**Meta Share:** 2%
**Win Rate Estimate:** 49-51%
**Cost Estimate:** $3,200 (driven by [Tundra](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Tundra%22), [Force of Will](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Force+of+Will%22), [Flooded Strand](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Flooded+Strand%22), [Wasteland](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Wasteland%22))
**First Appeared:** 2010
**Peak Meta Share:** 2011-2013
**Deck Count in Sample:** 31

A fair blue-white midrange deck built around [Stoneforge Mystic](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Stoneforge+Mystic%22) fetching [Batterskull](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Batterskull%22) and [Kaldra Compleat](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Kaldra+Compleat%22). Combines blue card selection and countermagic with efficient white threats and equipment.

### Decklist

**Main Deck:**

- 4 [Brainstorm](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Brainstorm%22)
- 4 [Ponder](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Ponder%22)
- 4 [Force of Will](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Force+of+Will%22)
- 4 [Swords to Plowshares](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Swords+to+Plowshares%22)
- 4 [Stoneforge Mystic](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Stoneforge+Mystic%22)
- 1 [Batterskull](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Batterskull%22)
- 1 [Kaldra Compleat](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Kaldra+Compleat%22)
- 3 [Teferi, Time Raveler](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Teferi%2C+Time+Raveler%22)
- 2 [Shark Typhoon](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Shark+Typhoon%22)
- 2 [Spell Pierce](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Spell+Pierce%22)
- 2 [Counterspell](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Counterspell%22)

- 1 [Phlage, Titan of Fire's Fury](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Phlage%2C+Titan+of+Fire%27s+Fury%22)

- 2 [Polluted Delta](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Polluted+Delta%22)
- 2 [Misty Rainforest](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Misty+Rainforest%22)
- 4 [Tundra](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Tundra%22)
- 1 [Mystic Gate](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Mystic+Gate%22)
- 2 [Island](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Island%22)
- 1 [Plains](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Plains%22)
