- 1 [Karakas](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Karakas%22)
- 1 [Otawara, Soaring City](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Otawara%2C+Soaring+City%22)
- 1 [Eiganjo, Seat of the Empire](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Eiganjo%2C+Seat+of+the+Empire%22)
- 1 [Castle Vantress](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Castle+Vantress%22)

**Sideboard:**

- 2 [Flusterstorm](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Flusterstorm%22)
- 2 [Surgical Extraction](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Surgical+Extraction%22)
- 2 [Hydroblast](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Hydroblast%22)
- 2 [Containment Priest](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Containment+Priest%22)
- 1 [Dress Down](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Dress+Down%22)
- 2 [Terminus](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Terminus%22)
- 1 [Force of Negation](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Force+of+Negation%22)
- 1 [Meddling Mage](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Meddling+Mage%22)
- 1 [Disenchant](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Disenchant%22)
- 1 [Hullbreacher](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Hullbreacher%22)

### Key Matchups

- **Favorable:** Burn, Elves, LED Dredge
- **Unfavorable:** Dimir Tempo, Sneak and Show, Lands
- **Even:** Death and Taxes, Izzet Delver, Painter

**Similar Decks:** Beanstalk Control, Jeskai Control, Esper Vial
Shares the blue-white shell with Jeskai Control but is more proactive with the [Stoneforge Mystic](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Stoneforge+Mystic%22) package.

### Key Cards Explained

<img src="https://api.scryfall.com/cards/named?exact=Stoneforge+Mystic&format=image&version=normal&set=wwk" alt="Stoneforge Mystic" width="217"> <img src="https://api.scryfall.com/cards/named?exact=Batterskull&format=image&version=normal&set=nph" alt="Batterskull" width="217"> <img src="https://api.scryfall.com/cards/named?exact=Kaldra+Compleat&format=image&version=normal&set=mh2" alt="Kaldra Compleat" width="217">

- **Stoneforge Mystic:** Tutors for any equipment on ETB and can cheat it into play for 1W.
- **Batterskull:** Living weapon with vigilance and lifelink. Nearly unbeatable for aggro decks when cheated in on turn 3.
- **Kaldra Compleat:** Indestructible living weapon with first strike and trample.
- **Teferi, Time Raveler:** Shuts down opposing instants, bounces problematic permanents, and draws cards.

### Historical Timeline

**2010** (tier 1, ~8%)
[Stoneforge Mystic](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Stoneforge+Mystic%22) printed in Worldwake. UW Stoneblade emerges as a premier fair deck.
- [Stoneforge Mystic](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Stoneforge+Mystic%22) + [Batterskull](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Batterskull%22) core
- [Umezawa's Jitte](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Umezawa%27s+Jitte%22) as equipment option

**2013** (tier 1, ~7%)
[True-Name Nemesis](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22True-Name+Nemesis%22) from Commander 2013 makes Stoneblade even better.
- [True-Name Nemesis](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22True-Name+Nemesis%22) added
- Dominant fair deck

**2018** (tier 2, ~3%)
DRS ban reshuffles the fair deck hierarchy.
- DRS ban impacts mana bases
- More variety in fair decks

**2023** (tier 3, ~1.5%)
Bowmasters and new printings push Stoneblade down.
- Bowmasters kills SFM
- Dimir Tempo supplants fair midrange role

**2026** (tier 3, ~2%)
Tier 3 at 2%. Loyal pilots keep the deck alive.
- [Kaldra Compleat](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Kaldra+Compleat%22) as primary equipment
- Teferi standard

### Bans Impact

- **Stoneforge Mystic** (2011-06): Banned in Standard but has always been legal in Legacy. The card is the deck's entire identity.

**Frequency of Change:** medium
**Change Notes:** Equipment targets rotate. [Kaldra Compleat](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Kaldra+Compleat%22) replaced [Umezawa's Jitte](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Umezawa%27s+Jitte%22). [Teferi, Time Raveler](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Teferi%2C+Time+Raveler%22) is a recent addition. Splash colors (Esper, Jeskai) are common.

---

## Pox

**Also known as:** Mono Black Pox, [Smallpox](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Smallpox%22), [The Rack](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22The+Rack%22)

**Archetype:** control
**Colors:** B
**Tier:** tier 3
**Meta Share:** 2%
**Win Rate Estimate:** 47-49%
**Cost Estimate:** $1,200 (driven by [Liliana of the Veil](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Liliana+of+the+Veil%22), [Wasteland](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Wasteland%22), [Orcish Bowmasters](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Orcish+Bowmasters%22))
**First Appeared:** 1996
**Peak Meta Share:** 2010-2012
**Deck Count in Sample:** 31

A symmetrical resource denial deck that uses [Smallpox](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Smallpox%22), [Hymn to Tourach](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Hymn+to+Tourach%22), and [Liliana of the Veil](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Liliana+of+the+Veil%22) to strip the opponent of lands, cards, and creatures. Wins by breaking the symmetry through [Mishra's Factory](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Mishra%27s+Factory%22) and planeswalkers.

### Decklist

**Main Deck:**

- 4 [Smallpox](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Smallpox%22)
- 4 [Hymn to Tourach](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Hymn+to+Tourach%22)
- 4 [Thoughtseize](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Thoughtseize%22)
- 3 [Liliana of the Veil](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Liliana+of+the+Veil%22)
- 2 [Liliana, the Last Hope](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Liliana%2C+the+Last+Hope%22)
- 4 [Dark Ritual](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Dark+Ritual%22)
- 2 [Innocent Blood](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Innocent+Blood%22)
- 1 [Toxic Deluge](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Toxic+Deluge%22)
- 2 [Nether Spirit](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Nether+Spirit%22)
- 3 [Bloodghast](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Bloodghast%22)
- 3 [Orcish Bowmasters](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Orcish+Bowmasters%22)
- 2 [Karn, the Great Creator](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Karn%2C+the+Great+Creator%22)
- 3 [Chrome Mox](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Chrome+Mox%22)
- 2 [The Rack](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22The+Rack%22)
- 2 [Urborg, Tomb of Yawgmoth](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Urborg%2C+Tomb+of+Yawgmoth%22)
- 6 [Swamp](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Swamp%22)
- 4 [Wasteland](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Wasteland%22)
- 3 [Mishra's Factory](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Mishra%27s+Factory%22)
- 4 [Bloodstained Mire](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Bloodstained+Mire%22)
- 2 [Marsh Flats](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Marsh+Flats%22)

**Sideboard:**

- 3 [Leyline of the Void](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Leyline+of+the+Void%22)
- 2 [Plague Engineer](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Plague+Engineer%22)
- 2 [Surgical Extraction](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Surgical+Extraction%22)
- 1 [Engineered Plague](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Engineered+Plague%22)
- 1 [Ratchet Bomb](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Ratchet+Bomb%22)
- 2 [Ensnaring Bridge](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Ensnaring+Bridge%22)
- 1 [Pithing Needle](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Pithing+Needle%22)
- 2 [Sphere of Resistance](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Sphere+of+Resistance%22)
- 1 [Trinisphere](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Trinisphere%22)

### Key Matchups

- **Favorable:** Dimir Tempo, Izzet Delver, Stoneblade
- **Unfavorable:** Sneak and Show, Oops! All Spells, Lands
- **Even:** Death and Taxes, Eldrazi, Red Stompy

**Similar Decks:** Mono Black Midrange, Death and Taxes
Shares resource denial with Death and Taxes but uses black disruption instead of white hate bears.

### Key Cards Explained

<img src="https://api.scryfall.com/cards/named?exact=Smallpox&format=image&version=normal&set=tsp" alt="Smallpox" width="217"> <img src="https://api.scryfall.com/cards/named?exact=Hymn+to+Tourach&format=image&version=normal&set=fem" alt="Hymn to Tourach" width="217"> <img src="https://api.scryfall.com/cards/named?exact=Liliana+of+the+Veil&format=image&version=normal&set=isd" alt="Liliana of the Veil" width="217">

- **Smallpox:** Each player discards, sacrifices a creature, sacrifices a land, and loses 1 life. Devastating when you break the symmetry.
- **Hymn to Tourach:** Random discard of two cards for BB. One of the most powerful disruption spells in Magic.
- **Liliana of the Veil:** Repeatable edict and discard. Grinds opponents out over multiple turns.
- **Nether Spirit:** Returns from graveyard during upkeep if it's the only creature there. Perfect symmetry-breaker.

### Historical Timeline

**1996** (tier 3, ~1%)
Pox (the card) printed in Ice Age. Resource denial viable from Magic's earliest days.
- Pox as namesake card
- Sinkhole and [Hymn to Tourach](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Hymn+to+Tourach%22)

**2009** (tier 3, ~1.5%)
[Smallpox](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Smallpox%22) from [Time Spiral](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Time+Spiral%22) provides a more efficient version of the strategy.
- [Smallpox](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Smallpox%22) as four-of
- [Bloodghast](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Bloodghast%22) and [Nether Spirit](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Nether+Spirit%22) for symmetry breaking

**2012** (tier 2, ~2.5%)
[Liliana of the Veil](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Liliana+of+the+Veil%22) from Innistrad is perfect. Deck reaches peak viability.
- [Liliana of the Veil](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Liliana+of+the+Veil%22) as key planeswalker
- Peak competitive viability

**2023** (tier 3, ~1.5%)
Bowmasters gives mono-black a powerful new card.
- [Orcish Bowmasters](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Orcish+Bowmasters%22) added
- Improved creature base

**2026** (tier 3, ~2%)
Tier 3 at 2%. Loyal following and Bowmasters has improved creature matchups.
- Stable with Bowmasters
- Karn wishboard in some builds

**Frequency of Change:** low
**Change Notes:** Very stable core. Bowmasters was a significant addition in 2023. Karn wishboard in some builds.

---

## Mardu Energy

**Also known as:** Mardu Aggro, RBW Energy, Mardu Scam

**Archetype:** aggro
**Colors:** R, B, W
**Tier:** tier 2
**Meta Share:** 3%
**Win Rate Estimate:** 51-53%
**Cost Estimate:** $2,600 (driven by [Badlands](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Badlands%22), [Scrubland](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Scrubland%22), [Plateau](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Plateau%22), [Wasteland](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Wasteland%22))
**First Appeared:** 2024
**Peak Meta Share:** 2025-2026
**Deck Count in Sample:** 47

An aggressive energy-based deck combining [Ocelot Pride](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Ocelot+Pride%22) and [Amped Raptor](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Amped+Raptor%22) with black disruption and [Broadside Bombardiers](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Broadside+Bombardiers%22). Leverages MH3 energy creatures alongside [Thoughtseize](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Thoughtseize%22) and efficient removal.

### Decklist

**Main Deck:**

- 4 [Ocelot Pride](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Ocelot+Pride%22)
- 4 [Amped Raptor](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Amped+Raptor%22)
- 4 [Broadside Bombardiers](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Broadside+Bombardiers%22)
- 4 [Orcish Bowmasters](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Orcish+Bowmasters%22)
- 3 [Guide of Souls](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Guide+of+Souls%22)
- 4 [Thoughtseize](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Thoughtseize%22)
- 4 [Lightning Bolt](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Lightning+Bolt%22)
- 3 [Galvanic Discharge](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Galvanic+Discharge%22)
- 2 [Swords to Plowshares](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Swords+to+Plowshares%22)
- 1 [Grief](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Grief%22)
- 2 [Ajani, Nacatl Pariah](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Ajani%2C+Nacatl+Pariah%22)
- 2 [Fable of the Mirror-Breaker](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Fable+of+the+Mirror-Breaker%22)
- 2 [Badlands](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Badlands%22)
- 1 [Scrubland](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Scrubland%22)
- 2 [Plateau](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Plateau%22)
- 4 [Bloodstained Mire](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Bloodstained+Mire%22)
- 4 [Marsh Flats](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Marsh+Flats%22)
- 2 [Arid Mesa](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Arid+Mesa%22)
- 1 [Swamp](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Swamp%22)
- 1 [Mountain](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Mountain%22)
- 1 [Plains](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Plains%22)
- 3 [Urza's Saga](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Urza%27s+Saga%22)
- 2 [Wasteland](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Wasteland%22)

**Sideboard:**

- 2 [Mindbreak Trap](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Mindbreak+Trap%22)
- 2 [Torpor Orb](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Torpor+Orb%22)
- 2 [Surgical Extraction](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Surgical+Extraction%22)
- 2 [Pyroblast](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Pyroblast%22)
- 2 [Containment Priest](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Containment+Priest%22)
- 2 [Plague Engineer](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Plague+Engineer%22)
- 1 [Wear // Tear](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Wear+//+Tear%22)
- 1 [Pithing Needle](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Pithing+Needle%22)
- 1 [Haywire Mite](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Haywire+Mite%22)

### Key Matchups

- **Favorable:** Dimir Tempo, Beanstalk Control, Jeskai Control
- **Unfavorable:** Sneak and Show, Oops! All Spells, Lands
- **Even:** [Ocelot Pride](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Ocelot+Pride%22) Midrange, Izzet Delver, Painter

**Similar Decks:** [Ocelot Pride](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Ocelot+Pride%22) Midrange, Dimir Tempo
Shares the energy creature core with [Ocelot Pride](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Ocelot+Pride%22) Midrange but adds black for [Thoughtseize](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Thoughtseize%22), Bowmasters, and [Broadside Bombardiers](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Broadside+Bombardiers%22).

### Key Cards Explained

<img src="https://api.scryfall.com/cards/named?exact=Broadside+Bombardiers&format=image&version=normal&set=lci" alt="Broadside Bombardiers" width="217"> <img src="https://api.scryfall.com/cards/named?exact=Ocelot+Pride&format=image&version=normal&set=mh3" alt="Ocelot Pride" width="217"> <img src="https://api.scryfall.com/cards/named?exact=Amped+Raptor&format=image&version=normal&set=mh3" alt="Amped Raptor" width="217">

- **Broadside Bombardiers:** Menace creature that sacrifices on attack to deal 3 damage and give another attacker +1/+0 and trample.
- **Ocelot Pride:** Generates cat tokens when you gain life and deal combat damage.
- **Amped Raptor:** Energy creature with cascade equal to energy spent.
- **Thoughtseize:** Surgical disruption that protects the aggro plan from sweepers and combo.

### Historical Timeline

**2024** (tier 3, ~1%)
MH3 energy cards spark Mardu experimentation. [Broadside Bombardiers](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Broadside+Bombardiers%22) and [Ocelot Pride](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Ocelot+Pride%22) alongside black disruption.
- MH3 energy cards as foundation
- [Broadside Bombardiers](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Broadside+Bombardiers%22) adds reach

**2025** (tier 2, ~2.5%)
Deck solidifies as a real contender. Energy aggro with black disruption proves potent against blue.
- Lists refined
- [Grief](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Grief%22) package explored

**2026** (tier 2, ~3%)
Tier 2 at 3%. Premier aggressive disruption strategy.
- Stable core established
- Flex between aggression and disruption

**Frequency of Change:** high
**Change Notes:** New archetype still evolving rapidly. Some builds lean into the [Grief](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Grief%22) package, others focus on pure energy aggro.

---

## Boros Initiative

**Also known as:** White Stompy Initiative, Mono White Initiative, RW Initiative

**Archetype:** stompy
**Colors:** W, R
**Tier:** tier 2
**Meta Share:** 2%
**Win Rate Estimate:** 50-52%
**Cost Estimate:** $2,400 (driven by [City of Traitors](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22City+of+Traitors%22), [Ancient Tomb](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Ancient+Tomb%22), [Solitude](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Solitude%22), [Chalice of the Void](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Chalice+of+the+Void%22))
**First Appeared:** 2022
**Peak Meta Share:** 2022-2023
**Deck Count in Sample:** 31

A [Chalice of the Void](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Chalice+of+the+Void%22) stompy deck that uses fast mana to deploy initiative creatures like [Caves of Chaos Adventurer](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Caves+of+Chaos+Adventurer%22) and hate bears like [Archon of Emeria](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Archon+of+Emeria%22).

- 4 [Chalice of the Void](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Chalice+of+the+Void%22)

- 3 [Lotus Petal](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Lotus+Petal%22)
- 3 [Swords to Plowshares](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Swords+to+Plowshares%22)
- 2 [Touch the Spirit Realm](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Touch+the+Spirit+Realm%22)
- 4 [Ancient Tomb](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Ancient+Tomb%22)
- 4 [City of Traitors](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22City+of+Traitors%22)
- 1 [Eiganjo, Seat of the Empire](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Eiganjo%2C+Seat+of+the+Empire%22)

- 2 [Plateau](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Plateau%22)
- 2 [Inspiring Vantage](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Inspiring+Vantage%22)

**Sideboard:**

- 2 [Containment Priest](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Containment+Priest%22)
- 2 [Ethersworn Canonist](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Ethersworn+Canonist%22)
- 3 [Leyline of the Void](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Leyline+of+the+Void%22)
- 2 [Pyroblast](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Pyroblast%22)
- 2 [Mindbreak Trap](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Mindbreak+Trap%22)
- 2 [Faerie Macabre](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Faerie+Macabre%22)
- 1 [Pithing Needle](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Pithing+Needle%22)
- 1 [Unlicensed Hearse](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Unlicensed+Hearse%22)

### Key Matchups

- **Favorable:** Dimir Tempo, Izzet Delver, [Doomsday](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Doomsday%22)
- **Unfavorable:** Painter, [Ocelot Pride](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Ocelot+Pride%22) Midrange, Lands
- **Even:** Sneak and Show, Eldrazi, Death and Taxes

**Similar Decks:** Red Stompy, Death and Taxes, Eldrazi
Shares the Chalice + fast mana shell with Red Stompy and Eldrazi. Initiative provides a unique card advantage engine.

### Key Cards Explained

<img src="https://api.scryfall.com/cards/named?exact=Caves+of+Chaos+Adventurer&format=image&version=normal&set=clb" alt="Caves of Chaos Adventurer" width="217"> <img src="https://api.scryfall.com/cards/named?exact=Chalice+of+the+Void&format=image&version=normal&set=mrd" alt="Chalice of the Void" width="217"> <img src="https://api.scryfall.com/cards/named?exact=Archon+of+Emeria&format=image&version=normal&set=znr" alt="Archon of Emeria" width="217">

- **Caves of Chaos Adventurer:** 4/4 with initiative for 3W. The Undercity dungeon provides treasure, card selection, damage, and a game-winning effect.
- **Chalice of the Void:** On one, shuts down [Brainstorm](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Brainstorm%22), [Ponder](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Ponder%22), [Swords to Plowshares](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Swords+to+Plowshares%22).
- **Archon of Emeria:** Restricts opponents to one spell per turn and nonbasic lands enter tapped.
- **Solitude:** Free removal via pitch casting.

### Historical Timeline

**2022** (tier 1, ~7%)
Initiative mechanic from Baldur's Gate arrives. Mono White Stompy immediately adopts the enormously powerful initiative creatures.
- White Plume Adventurer at 3 mana
- Chalice + fast mana shell

**2023** (tier 2, ~4%)
White Plume Adventurer banned March. Deck adapts to 4-mana initiative creatures.
- White Plume banned
- Caves of Chaos at 4 mana

**2025** (tier 2, ~2.5%)
Competes with other stompy decks. Boros splash provides [Pyroblast](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Pyroblast%22) access.
- Boros splash
- Competes with Eldrazi and Red Stompy

**2026** (tier 2, ~2%)
Tier 2 at 2%. Initiative remains powerful but faces stiff competition.
- Stable shell
- Competes for stompy slot

### Bans Impact

- **White Plume Adventurer** (2023-03): Banned for being too efficient at 3 mana. Deck adapted with [Caves of Chaos Adventurer](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Caves+of+Chaos+Adventurer%22) and [Seasoned Dungeoneer](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Seasoned+Dungeoneer%22).

**Frequency of Change:** medium
**Change Notes:** Initiative creatures are the core. Some builds splash red for [Pyroblast](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Pyroblast%22) and [Fable of the Mirror-Breaker](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Fable+of+the+Mirror-Breaker%22).

---

## Cloudpost Ramp

**Also known as:** 12-Post, [Cloudpost](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Cloudpost%22), Post

**Archetype:** ramp
**Colors:** C
**Tier:** tier 3
**Meta Share:** 1%
**Win Rate Estimate:** 48-50%
**Cost Estimate:** $3,500 (driven by [Candelabra of Tawnos](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Candelabra+of+Tawnos%22), [Karn Liberated](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Karn+Liberated%22), [Ugin, the Spirit Dragon](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Ugin%2C+the+Spirit+Dragon%22))
**First Appeared:** 2003
**Peak Meta Share:** 2011-2012
**Deck Count in Sample:** 16

A big mana deck using [Cloudpost](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Cloudpost%22) and [Glimmerpost](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Glimmerpost%22) to generate enormous colorless mana, deploying massive threats like Ugin and [Karn Liberated](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Karn+Liberated%22).

### Decklist

**Main Deck:**

- 4 [Cloudpost](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Cloudpost%22)
- 4 [Glimmerpost](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Glimmerpost%22)
- 2 [Vesuva](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Vesuva%22)
- 2 [Thespian's Stage](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Thespian%27s+Stage%22)
- 4 [Expedition Map](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Expedition+Map%22)
- 4 [Crop Rotation](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Crop+Rotation%22)
- 2 [Candelabra of Tawnos](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Candelabra+of+Tawnos%22)
- 2 [Pithing Needle](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Pithing+Needle%22)
- 2 [Ugin, the Spirit Dragon](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Ugin%2C+the+Spirit+Dragon%22)
- 2 [Karn Liberated](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Karn+Liberated%22)
- 3 [Karn, the Great Creator](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Karn%2C+the+Great+Creator%22)
- 1 [Ulamog, the Ceaseless Hunger](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Ulamog%2C+the+Ceaseless+Hunger%22)
- 1 [Kozilek, Butcher of Truth](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Kozilek%2C+Butcher+of+Truth%22)
- 2 [All Is Dust](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22All+Is+Dust%22)
- 3 [Warping Wail](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Warping+Wail%22)
- 4 [Once Upon a Time](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Once+Upon+a+Time%22)
- 4 [Ancient Stirrings](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Ancient+Stirrings%22)
- 4 [Elvish Rejuvenator](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Elvish+Rejuvenator%22)
- 6 [Forest](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Forest%22)
- 1 [Bojuka Bog](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Bojuka+Bog%22)
- 1 [Eye of Ugin](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Eye+of+Ugin%22)
- 1 [Karakas](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Karakas%22)
- 1 [Blast Zone](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Blast+Zone%22)

**Sideboard:**

- 2 [Trinisphere](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Trinisphere%22)
- 2 [Chalice of the Void](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Chalice+of+the+Void%22)
- 1 [Ensnaring Bridge](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Ensnaring+Bridge%22)
- 2 [Tormod's Crypt](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Tormod%27s+Crypt%22)
- 3 [Force of Vigor](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Force+of+Vigor%22)
- 2 [Endurance](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Endurance%22)
- 1 [Walking Ballista](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Walking+Ballista%22)
- 1 [Liquimetal Coating](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Liquimetal+Coating%22)
- 1 [Mycosynth Lattice](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Mycosynth+Lattice%22)

### Key Matchups

- **Favorable:** Death and Taxes, Burn, Elves
- **Unfavorable:** Dimir Tempo, Izzet Delver, Oops! All Spells
- **Even:** Lands, Eldrazi, Beanstalk Control

**Similar Decks:** Lands, Eldrazi
Like Lands, uses nonbasic lands as the engine but goes bigger. Eldrazi shares colorless threats but different mana base.

### Key Cards Explained

<img src="https://api.scryfall.com/cards/named?exact=Cloudpost&format=image&version=normal&set=mrd" alt="Cloudpost" width="217"> <img src="https://api.scryfall.com/cards/named?exact=Glimmerpost&format=image&version=normal&set=som" alt="Glimmerpost" width="217"> <img src="https://api.scryfall.com/cards/named?exact=Karn%2C+the+Great+Creator&format=image&version=normal&set=war" alt="Karn, the Great Creator" width="217">

- **Cloudpost:** Taps for 1 mana for each Locus in play. With four Loci, each taps for 4.
- **Glimmerpost:** Second Locus that gains life on ETB.
- **Karn, the Great Creator:** Provides wishboard and shuts off opposing artifacts.
- **Ugin, the Spirit Dragon:** 8 mana wrath that also exiles. Easy to cast with multiple Cloudposts.

### Historical Timeline

**2003** (tier 3, ~1%)
[Cloudpost](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Cloudpost%22) printed in Mirrodin. Locus ramp becomes viable.
- [Cloudpost](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Cloudpost%22) + [Glimmerpost](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Glimmerpost%22) engine

**2011** (tier 2, ~3%)
Peak popularity with Eldrazi finishers.
- Eldrazi titans as finishers
- [Primeval Titan](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Primeval+Titan%22) for land tutoring

**2019** (tier 3, ~1.5%)
[Karn, the Great Creator](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Karn%2C+the+Great+Creator%22) adds wishboard dimension.
- Karn wishboard
- [Mycosynth Lattice](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Mycosynth+Lattice%22) combo

**2026** (tier 3, ~1%)
Tier 3 at 1%. Niche but powerful when assembling multiple Loci.
- Stable list
- Niche metagame player

**Frequency of Change:** low
**Change Notes:** Very stable core. Karn wishboard is the main recent innovation.

---

## Hogaak

**Also known as:** BG Hogaak, Hogaak Depths, Hogaak Combo

**Archetype:** combo
**Colors:** B, G
**Tier:** tier 3
**Meta Share:** 0.7%
**Win Rate Estimate:** 48-50%
**Cost Estimate:** $1,500 (driven by [Bayou](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Bayou%22), [Verdant Catacombs](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Verdant+Catacombs%22), [Hogaak, Arisen Necropolis](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Hogaak%2C+Arisen+Necropolis%22))
**First Appeared:** 2019
**Peak Meta Share:** 2019-2020
**Deck Count in Sample:** 11

A graveyard-based combo deck using [Hogaak, Arisen Necropolis](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Hogaak%2C+Arisen+Necropolis%22) as a free 8/8 trampler, combined with [Vengevine](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Vengevine%22) and [Altar of Dementia](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Altar+of+Dementia%22) for a self-mill win condition.

### Decklist

**Main Deck:**

- 4 [Hogaak, Arisen Necropolis](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Hogaak%2C+Arisen+Necropolis%22)
- 4 [Vengevine](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Vengevine%22)
- 4 [Stitcher's Supplier](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Stitcher%27s+Supplier%22)
- 4 [Satyr Wayfinder](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Satyr+Wayfinder%22)
- 4 [Gravecrawler](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Gravecrawler%22)
- 4 [Carrion Feeder](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Carrion+Feeder%22)
- 4 [Bloodghast](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Bloodghast%22)
- 3 [Altar of Dementia](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Altar+of+Dementia%22)
- 4 [Cabal Therapy](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Cabal+Therapy%22)
- 4 [Once Upon a Time](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Once+Upon+a+Time%22)
- 4 [Verdant Catacombs](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Verdant+Catacombs%22)
- 4 [Polluted Delta](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Polluted+Delta%22)
- 2 [Bayou](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Bayou%22)
- 1 [Overgrown Tomb](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Overgrown+Tomb%22)
- 1 [Swamp](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Swamp%22)
- 1 [Forest](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Forest%22)
- 2 [Nurturing Peatland](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Nurturing+Peatland%22)
- 3 [Undiscovered Paradise](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Undiscovered+Paradise%22)
- 3 [Wasteland](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Wasteland%22)

**Sideboard:**

- 3 [Force of Vigor](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Force+of+Vigor%22)
- 3 [Thoughtseize](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Thoughtseize%22)
- 2 [Endurance](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Endurance%22)
- 2 [Surgical Extraction](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Surgical+Extraction%22)
- 2 [Collector Ouphe](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Collector+Ouphe%22)
- 1 [Pithing Needle](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Pithing+Needle%22)
- 1 [Boseiju, Who Endures](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Boseiju%2C+Who+Endures%22)
- 1 [Reclamation Sage](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Reclamation+Sage%22)

### Key Matchups

- **Favorable:** Jeskai Control, Beanstalk Control, Burn
- **Unfavorable:** Dimir Tempo, Izzet Delver, Death and Taxes
- **Even:** Lands, LED Dredge, [Ocelot Pride](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Ocelot+Pride%22) Midrange

**Similar Decks:** LED Dredge, Reanimator
Shares the graveyard-centric plan with LED Dredge but is creature-based. Both fold to graveyard hate.

### Key Cards Explained

<img src="https://api.scryfall.com/cards/named?exact=Hogaak%2C+Arisen+Necropolis&format=image&version=normal&set=mh1" alt="Hogaak, Arisen Necropolis" width="217"> <img src="https://api.scryfall.com/cards/named?exact=Vengevine&format=image&version=normal&set=roe" alt="Vengevine" width="217"> <img src="https://api.scryfall.com/cards/named?exact=Altar+of+Dementia&format=image&version=normal&set=tmp" alt="Altar of Dementia" width="217">

- **Hogaak, Arisen Necropolis:** Free 8/8 trampler cast by convoking and delving. Recurs from graveyard.
- **Vengevine:** Returns from graveyard when you cast two creatures in a turn.
- **Altar of Dementia:** Sacrifice outlet that mills. Enables infinite mill with recurring creatures.
- **Stitcher's Supplier:** Mills three on ETB and death. Fuels graveyard synergies.

### Historical Timeline

**2019** (tier 2, ~2%)
Hogaak from MH1 warps Modern. In Legacy, creates a powerful but fair graveyard deck.
- Hogaak as free 8/8
- [Vengevine](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Vengevine%22) synergies

**2021** (tier 3, ~1%)
Settles into a niche role. Powerful against fair decks but weak to graveyard hate.
- [Altar of Dementia](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Altar+of+Dementia%22) as win condition

**2026** (tier 3, ~0.7%)
Tier 3 at 0.7%. Niche graveyard strategy.
- Stable niche deck

### Bans Impact

- **Hogaak, Arisen Necropolis** (2019-08): Banned in Modern but legal in Legacy where [Force of Will](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Force+of+Will%22) keeps it in check.

**Frequency of Change:** low
**Change Notes:** Core is very stable. [Once Upon a Time](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Once+Upon+a+Time%22) was a big addition.

---

## Coveted Jewel Combo

**Also known as:** Jewel Combo, Flicker Jewel, [Coveted Jewel](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Coveted+Jewel%22)

**Archetype:** combo
**Colors:** U, W
**Tier:** tier 3
**Meta Share:** 0.7%
**Win Rate Estimate:** 48-50%
**Cost Estimate:** $2,100 (driven by [City of Traitors](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22City+of+Traitors%22), [Ancient Tomb](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Ancient+Tomb%22), [Solitude](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Solitude%22), [Tundra](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Tundra%22))
**First Appeared:** 2023
**Peak Meta Share:** 2024-2025
**Deck Count in Sample:** 11

A combo deck using [Coveted Jewel](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Coveted+Jewel%22) with flicker effects like [Flickerwisp](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Flickerwisp%22) and [Ephemerate](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Ephemerate%22) to generate enormous mana and card advantage. The Jewel draws three and adds three on ETB.

### Decklist

**Main Deck:**

- 3 [Coveted Jewel](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Coveted+Jewel%22)
- 4 [Flickerwisp](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Flickerwisp%22)

- 1 [Eiganjo, Seat of the Empire](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Eiganjo%2C+Seat+of+the+Empire%22)
- 2 [Cavern of Souls](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Cavern+of+Souls%22)
- 3 [Rishadan Port](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Rishadan+Port%22)

**Sideboard:**

- 2 [Containment Priest](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Containment+Priest%22)

- 2 [Surgical Extraction](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Surgical+Extraction%22)
- 1 [Pithing Needle](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Pithing+Needle%22)

### Key Matchups

- **Favorable:** Dimir Tempo, Izzet Delver, Burn
- **Unfavorable:** Sneak and Show, Oops! All Spells, Painter
- **Even:** [Ocelot Pride](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Ocelot+Pride%22) Midrange, Death and Taxes, Eldrazi

**Similar Decks:** Death and Taxes, Esper Vial
Evolved from Death and Taxes, adding [Coveted Jewel](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Coveted+Jewel%22) combo as a powerful mana engine.

### Key Cards Explained

<img src="https://api.scryfall.com/cards/named?exact=Coveted+Jewel&format=image&version=normal&set=c18" alt="Coveted Jewel" width="217"> <img src="https://api.scryfall.com/cards/named?exact=Ephemerate&format=image&version=normal&set=mh1" alt="Ephemerate" width="217"> <img src="https://api.scryfall.com/cards/named?exact=Flickerwisp&format=image&version=normal&set=eve" alt="Flickerwisp" width="217">

- **Coveted Jewel:** Six mana artifact that draws three and adds three on ETB. Flickering resets both.
- **Ephemerate:** One mana instant flicker with rebound. Flickers Jewel twice for six cards.
- **Flickerwisp:** 3/1 flyer that exiles something until end of turn. Resets Jewel.
- **Recruiter of the Guard:** Tutors for any creature with toughness 2 or less. Finds [Flickerwisp](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Flickerwisp%22).

### Historical Timeline

**2023** (fringe, ~0.3%)
[Coveted Jewel](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Coveted+Jewel%22) + flicker interaction discovered. Early builds from DnT shells.
- Combo discovered
- DnT shell

**2024** (tier 3, ~0.8%)
Deck refined, puts up tournament results.
- Refined lists
- Tournament results

**2026** (tier 3, ~0.7%)
Tier 3 at 0.7%. Niche combo-creature hybrid.
- Stable hybrid strategy

**Frequency of Change:** medium
**Change Notes:** Still being optimized. Balance between combo pieces and fair creatures is the key tension.

---

## Ruby Storm

**Also known as:** Mono Red Storm, Birgi Storm, [Ruby Medallion](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Ruby+Medallion%22) Storm

**Archetype:** combo
**Colors:** R
**Tier:** tier 3
**Meta Share:** 0.4%
**Win Rate Estimate:** 47-49%
**Cost Estimate:** $600 (driven by [City of Traitors](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22City+of+Traitors%22), [Fiery Islet](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Fiery+Islet%22))
**First Appeared:** 2021
**Peak Meta Share:** 2022-2023
**Deck Count in Sample:** 6

A mono-red storm combo deck using [Birgi, God of Storytelling](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Birgi%2C+God+of+Storytelling%22) and [Ruby Medallion](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Ruby+Medallion%22) to reduce costs, chaining rituals until casting lethal [Grapeshot](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Grapeshot%22) or [Empty the Warrens](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Empty+the+Warrens%22).

### Decklist

**Main Deck:**

- 4 [Birgi, God of Storytelling](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Birgi%2C+God+of+Storytelling%22)
- 4 [Ruby Medallion](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Ruby+Medallion%22)
- 2 [Bonus Round](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Bonus+Round%22)
- 4 [Burning Wish](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Burning+Wish%22)
- 1 [Grapeshot](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Grapeshot%22)
- 1 [Empty the Warrens](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Empty+the+Warrens%22)
- 4 [Rite of Flame](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Rite+of+Flame%22)
- 4 [Desperate Ritual](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Desperate+Ritual%22)
- 4 [Pyretic Ritual](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Pyretic+Ritual%22)
- 4 [Seething Song](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Seething+Song%22)
- 4 [Manamorphose](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Manamorphose%22)
- 2 [Reforge the Soul](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Reforge+the+Soul%22)
- 4 [Faithless Looting](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Faithless+Looting%22)
- 2 [Gut Shot](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Gut+Shot%22)
- 6 [Mountain](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Mountain%22)
- 2 [Dwarven Mine](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Dwarven+Mine%22)
- 4 [Fiery Islet](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Fiery+Islet%22)
- 4 [City of Traitors](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22City+of+Traitors%22)

**Sideboard:**

- 1 [Grapeshot](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Grapeshot%22)
- 1 [Empty the Warrens](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Empty+the+Warrens%22)
- 1 [Shattering Spree](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Shattering+Spree%22)
- 1 [Pulverize](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Pulverize%22)
- 1 [Reforge the Soul](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Reforge+the+Soul%22)
- 1 [Past in Flames](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Past+in+Flames%22)
- 1 [Fury](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Fury%22)
- 3 [Defense Grid](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Defense+Grid%22)
- 2 [Pyroblast](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Pyroblast%22)
- 2 [Chalice of the Void](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Chalice+of+the+Void%22)
- 1 [Trinisphere](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Trinisphere%22)

### Key Matchups

- **Favorable:** Lands, Death and Taxes, Elves
- **Unfavorable:** Dimir Tempo, [Ocelot Pride](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Ocelot+Pride%22) Midrange, Red Stompy
- **Even:** Izzet Delver, The EPIC Storm, Burn

**Similar Decks:** The EPIC Storm, Oops! All Spells
Shares the storm goal with TES but uses red rituals and Birgi instead of black tutors and [Ad Nauseam](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Ad+Nauseam%22).

### Key Cards Explained

<img src="https://api.scryfall.com/cards/named?exact=Birgi%2C+God+of+Storytelling&format=image&version=normal&set=khm" alt="Birgi, God of Storytelling" width="217"> <img src="https://api.scryfall.com/cards/named?exact=Ruby+Medallion&format=image&version=normal&set=tmp" alt="Ruby Medallion" width="217"> <img src="https://api.scryfall.com/cards/named?exact=Bonus+Round&format=image&version=normal&set=bbd" alt="Bonus Round" width="217">

- **Birgi, God of Storytelling:** Adds R whenever you cast a spell. With [Ruby Medallion](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Ruby+Medallion%22), every ritual nets extra mana.
- **Ruby Medallion:** Reduces red spells by 1.
- **Bonus Round:** Copies every instant and sorcery for the rest of the turn.
- **Burning Wish:** Tutors from sideboard for the right finisher.

### Historical Timeline

**2021** (tier 3, ~0.5%)
Birgi from Kaldheim enables mono-red storm.
- Birgi as enabler
- [Ruby Medallion](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Ruby+Medallion%22) synergy

**2022** (tier 3, ~0.7%)
Refined with [Bonus Round](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Bonus+Round%22). Occasional tournament results.
- [Bonus Round](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Bonus+Round%22) added
- [Burning Wish](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Burning+Wish%22) toolbox

**2026** (tier 3, ~0.4%)
Tier 3 at 0.4%. Budget storm option, less consistent than TES.
- Budget storm option
- Stable but niche

**Frequency of Change:** low
**Change Notes:** Stable core around Birgi and [Ruby Medallion](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Ruby+Medallion%22). [Bonus Round](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Bonus+Round%22) was a key addition.

## Cephalid Breakfast

**Also known as:** Breakfast Combo, Cephalid Combo, Nomads Combo

**Archetype:** combo
**Colors:** U, W
**Tier:** tier 3
**Meta Share:** 0.4%
**Win Rate Estimate:** 48-50%
**Cost Estimate:** $2,800 (driven by [Tundra](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Tundra%22), [Force of Will](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Force+of+Will%22), [Flooded Strand](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Flooded+Strand%22))
**First Appeared:** 2003
**Peak Meta Share:** 2005-2007
**Deck Count in Sample:** 6

A creature-based combo deck using [Cephalid Illusionist](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Cephalid+Illusionist%22) with [Nomads en-Kor](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Nomads+en-Kor%22) to mill the entire library, winning with [Narcomoeba](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Narcomoeba%22) and [Dread Return](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Dread+Return%22) into [Thassa's Oracle](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Thassa%27s+Oracle%22).

### Decklist

**Main Deck:**

- 4 [Cephalid Illusionist](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Cephalid+Illusionist%22)
- 4 [Nomads en-Kor](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Nomads+en-Kor%22)
- 1 [Thassa's Oracle](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Thassa%27s+Oracle%22)
- 3 [Narcomoeba](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Narcomoeba%22)
- 4 [Stoneforge Mystic](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Stoneforge+Mystic%22)
- 1 [Batterskull](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Batterskull%22)
- 3 [Recruiter of the Guard](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Recruiter+of+the+Guard%22)
- 1 [Dread Return](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Dread+Return%22)
- 4 [Force of Will](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Force+of+Will%22)
- 4 [Brainstorm](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Brainstorm%22)
- 4 [Ponder](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Ponder%22)
- 3 [Swords to Plowshares](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Swords+to+Plowshares%22)
- 4 [Aether Vial](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Aether+Vial%22)
- 4 [Flooded Strand](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Flooded+Strand%22)
- 2 [Polluted Delta](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Polluted+Delta%22)
- 2 [Misty Rainforest](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Misty+Rainforest%22)
- 3 [Tundra](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Tundra%22)
- 2 [Island](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Island%22)
- 1 [Plains](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Plains%22)
- 1 [Karakas](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Karakas%22)
- 2 [Cavern of Souls](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Cavern+of+Souls%22)
- 1 [Otawara, Soaring City](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Otawara%2C+Soaring+City%22)
- 1 [Eiganjo, Seat of the Empire](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Eiganjo%2C+Seat+of+the+Empire%22)
- 1 [Wasteland](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Wasteland%22)

**Sideboard:**

- 2 [Surgical Extraction](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Surgical+Extraction%22)
- 2 [Flusterstorm](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Flusterstorm%22)
- 2 [Containment Priest](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Containment+Priest%22)
- 2 [Meddling Mage](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Meddling+Mage%22)
- 2 [Rest in Peace](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Rest+in+Peace%22)
- 2 [Leyline of the Void](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Leyline+of+the+Void%22)
- 1 [Dress Down](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Dress+Down%22)
- 1 [Force of Negation](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Force+of+Negation%22)
- 1 [Kaldra Compleat](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Kaldra+Compleat%22)

### Key Matchups

- **Favorable:** Lands, Burn, [Cloudpost](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Cloudpost%22) Ramp
- **Unfavorable:** Dimir Tempo, Izzet Delver, [Ocelot Pride](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Ocelot+Pride%22) Midrange
- **Even:** Death and Taxes, Painter, Sneak and Show

**Similar Decks:** Oops! All Spells, [Doomsday](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Doomsday%22)
Like Oops, wins by milling the entire library. Uses a creature combo and can also play a fair [Stoneforge Mystic](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Stoneforge+Mystic%22) game.

### Key Cards Explained

<img src="https://api.scryfall.com/cards/named?exact=Cephalid+Illusionist&format=image&version=normal&set=tor" alt="Cephalid Illusionist" width="217"> <img src="https://api.scryfall.com/cards/named?exact=Nomads+en-Kor&format=image&version=normal&set=sth" alt="Nomads en-Kor" width="217"> <img src="https://api.scryfall.com/cards/named?exact=Thassa%27s+Oracle&format=image&version=normal&set=thb" alt="Thassa's Oracle" width="217">

- **Cephalid Illusionist:** Mills three whenever it becomes the target of a spell or ability.
- **Nomads en-Kor:** 0-cost activated ability targets Illusionist unlimited times.
- **Thassa's Oracle:** Wins on ETB when library is empty.
- **Aether Vial:** Cheats creatures in at instant speed, dodging countermagic.

### Historical Timeline

**2003** (tier 3, ~1%)
[Cephalid Illusionist](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Cephalid+Illusionist%22) + [Nomads en-Kor](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Nomads+en-Kor%22) combo discovered.
- Core combo established

**2007** (tier 3, ~1.5%)
Known quantity. [Aether Vial](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Aether+Vial%22) builds provide fair backup.
- [Aether Vial](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Aether+Vial%22) builds
- Stoneforge backup plan

**2020** (tier 3, ~0.5%)
[Thassa's Oracle](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Thassa%27s+Oracle%22) from Theros Beyond Death is a massive upgrade.
- [Thassa's Oracle](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Thassa%27s+Oracle%22) as win condition

**2026** (tier 3, ~0.4%)
Tier 3 at 0.4%. Niche combo with fair backup plan.
- Recruiter as tutor
- Stable niche deck

**Frequency of Change:** low
**Change Notes:** [Thassa's Oracle](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Thassa%27s+Oracle%22) replaced Laboratory Maniac. Core combo unchanged since 2003.

## Goblins

**Also known as:** Goblin Tribal, Mono Red Goblins, Vial Goblins

**Archetype:** aggro
**Colors:** R
**Tier:** fringe
**Meta Share:** 0.4%
**Win Rate Estimate:** 46-48%
**Cost Estimate:** $1,100 (driven by [Cavern of Souls](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Cavern+of+Souls%22), [Wasteland](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Wasteland%22), [Rishadan Port](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Rishadan+Port%22))
**First Appeared:** 2003
**Peak Meta Share:** 2003-2005
**Deck Count in Sample:** 6

A tribal aggro deck using [Goblin Lackey](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Goblin+Lackey%22) and [Aether Vial](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Aether+Vial%22) to cheat goblins into play. [Muxus, Goblin Grandee](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Muxus%2C+Goblin+Grandee%22) is the ultimate top-end.

### Decklist

**Main Deck:**

- 4 [Goblin Lackey](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Goblin+Lackey%22)
- 4 [Goblin Matron](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Goblin+Matron%22)
- 4 [Goblin Ringleader](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Goblin+Ringleader%22)
- 2 [Muxus, Goblin Grandee](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Muxus%2C+Goblin+Grandee%22)
- 3 [Goblin Warchief](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Goblin+Warchief%22)
- 3 [Munitions Expert](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Munitions+Expert%22)
- 2 [Sling-Gang Lieutenant](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Sling-Gang+Lieutenant%22)
- 1 [Goblin Trashmaster](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Goblin+Trashmaster%22)
- 2 [Goblin Cratermaker](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Goblin+Cratermaker%22)
- 3 [Goblin Piledriver](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Goblin+Piledriver%22)
- 4 [Aether Vial](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Aether+Vial%22)
- 4 [Cavern of Souls](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Cavern+of+Souls%22)
- 4 [Mountain](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Mountain%22)
- 4 [Wasteland](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Wasteland%22)
- 4 [Rishadan Port](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Rishadan+Port%22)
- 4 [Bloodstained Mire](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Bloodstained+Mire%22)
- 2 [Arid Mesa](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Arid+Mesa%22)
- 1 [Badlands](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Badlands%22)
- 3 [Fiery Islet](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Fiery+Islet%22)
- 1 [Castle Embereth](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Castle+Embereth%22)
- 1 [Den of the Bugbear](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Den+of+the+Bugbear%22)

**Sideboard:**

- 3 [Pyroblast](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Pyroblast%22)
- 2 [Chalice of the Void](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Chalice+of+the+Void%22)
- 2 [Surgical Extraction](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Surgical+Extraction%22)
- 2 [Mindbreak Trap](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Mindbreak+Trap%22)
- 2 [Torpor Orb](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Torpor+Orb%22)
- 2 [Grafdigger's Cage](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Grafdigger%27s+Cage%22)
- 1 [Pithing Needle](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Pithing+Needle%22)
- 1 [Goblin Trashmaster](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Goblin+Trashmaster%22)

### Key Matchups

- **Favorable:** Lands, Jeskai Control, Burn
- **Unfavorable:** Dimir Tempo, [Ocelot Pride](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Ocelot+Pride%22) Midrange, Izzet Delver
- **Even:** Death and Taxes, Eldrazi, Painter

**Similar Decks:** Elves, Merfolk
Shares the [Aether Vial](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Aether+Vial%22) tribal approach with Merfolk. Like Elves, a once-dominant creature deck hurt by Bowmasters.

### Key Cards Explained

<img src="https://api.scryfall.com/cards/named?exact=Goblin+Lackey&format=image&version=normal&set=usg" alt="Goblin Lackey" width="217"> <img src="https://api.scryfall.com/cards/named?exact=Muxus%2C+Goblin+Grandee&format=image&version=normal&set=jmp" alt="Muxus, Goblin Grandee" width="217"> <img src="https://api.scryfall.com/cards/named?exact=Goblin+Ringleader&format=image&version=normal&set=apc" alt="Goblin Ringleader" width="217">

- **Goblin Lackey:** Deals combat damage to put any goblin from hand into play free.
- **Muxus, Goblin Grandee:** Reveals top 6 and puts all goblins MV 5 or less into play.
- **Goblin Ringleader:** Reveals top 4 and puts all goblins into hand.
- **Goblin Matron:** Tutors for any goblin.

### Historical Timeline

**2003** (tier 1, ~8%)
Goblins is tier 1. Lackey and Warchief enable incredibly fast starts.
- [Goblin Lackey](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Goblin+Lackey%22) as enabler
- Ringleader for card advantage

**2010** (tier 2, ~3%)
Still competitive but losing ground to blue tempo.
- Format evolution hurts linear aggro

**2020** (tier 3, ~1%)
Muxus from Jumpstart is a massive addition.
- Muxus as top-end

**2023** (fringe, ~0.5%)
Bowmasters kills most goblins and devastates the strategy.
- Bowmasters devastating

**2026** (fringe, ~0.4%)
Fringe at 0.4%. Loyal pilots only.
- Outclassed by modern threats

**Frequency of Change:** low
**Change Notes:** Muxus from Jumpstart was the last major addition. Struggles against Bowmasters.

## Nic Fit

**Also known as:** BG Nic Fit, Junk Nic Fit, [Veteran Explorer](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Veteran+Explorer%22)

**Archetype:** midrange
**Colors:** B, G
**Tier:** fringe
**Meta Share:** 0.2%
**Win Rate Estimate:** 45-48%
**Cost Estimate:** $1,500 (driven by [Bayou](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Bayou%22), [Savannah](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Savannah%22), [Verdant Catacombs](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Verdant+Catacombs%22))
**First Appeared:** 2011
**Peak Meta Share:** 2013-2015
**Deck Count in Sample:** 3

A ramp midrange deck using [Veteran Explorer](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Veteran+Explorer%22) sacrificed to [Cabal Therapy](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Cabal+Therapy%22) to ramp, then plays expensive threats opponents can't match.

### Decklist

**Main Deck:**

- 4 [Veteran Explorer](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Veteran+Explorer%22)
- 4 [Cabal Therapy](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Cabal+Therapy%22)
- 4 [Green Sun's Zenith](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Green+Sun%27s+Zenith%22)
- 2 [Primeval Titan](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Primeval+Titan%22)
- 2 [Siege Rhino](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Siege+Rhino%22)
- 2 [Thragtusk](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Thragtusk%22)
- 2 [Tireless Tracker](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Tireless+Tracker%22)
- 1 [Collector Ouphe](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Collector+Ouphe%22)

- 2 [Thoughtseize](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Thoughtseize%22)
- 3 [Pernicious Deed](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Pernicious+Deed%22)
- 2 [Abrupt Decay](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Abrupt+Decay%22)
- 1 [Toxic Deluge](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Toxic+Deluge%22)
- 2 [Phyrexian Tower](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Phyrexian+Tower%22)
- 2 [Bayou](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Bayou%22)
- 1 [Savannah](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Savannah%22)
- 1 [Scrubland](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Scrubland%22)
- 4 [Verdant Catacombs](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Verdant+Catacombs%22)
- 4 [Windswept Heath](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Windswept+Heath%22)
- 5 [Forest](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Forest%22)
- 4 [Swamp](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Swamp%22)
- 1 [Plains](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Plains%22)
- 1 [Boseiju, Who Endures](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Boseiju%2C+Who+Endures%22)
- 1 [Field of the Dead](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Field+of+the+Dead%22)
- 1 [Nurturing Peatland](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Nurturing+Peatland%22)

**Sideboard:**

- 2 [Surgical Extraction](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Surgical+Extraction%22)
- 2 [Force of Vigor](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Force+of+Vigor%22)
- 3 [Leyline of the Void](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Leyline+of+the+Void%22)
- 2 [Plague Engineer](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Plague+Engineer%22)
- 2 [Choke](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Choke%22)
- 1 [Massacre](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Massacre%22)
- 1 [Reclamation Sage](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Reclamation+Sage%22)
- 2 [Carpet of Flowers](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Carpet+of+Flowers%22)

### Key Matchups

- **Favorable:** Burn, Izzet Delver, Dimir Tempo
- **Unfavorable:** Sneak and Show, Oops! All Spells, [Doomsday](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Doomsday%22)
- **Even:** Lands, Death and Taxes, [Ocelot Pride](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Ocelot+Pride%22) Midrange

**Similar Decks:** Maverick, Jund
Shares BG midrange core with Maverick but goes much bigger with [Veteran Explorer](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Veteran+Explorer%22) ramp.

### Key Cards Explained

<img src="https://api.scryfall.com/cards/named?exact=Veteran+Explorer&format=image&version=normal&set=wth" alt="Veteran Explorer" width="217"> <img src="https://api.scryfall.com/cards/named?exact=Cabal+Therapy&format=image&version=normal&set=jud" alt="Cabal Therapy" width="217"> <img src="https://api.scryfall.com/cards/named?exact=Pernicious+Deed&format=image&version=normal&set=apc" alt="Pernicious Deed" width="217">

- **Veteran Explorer:** When it dies, each player searches for two basic lands. Most Legacy decks play 0-2 basics.
- **Cabal Therapy:** Names a card to strip from opponent's hand. Sac Explorer to flashback.
- **Pernicious Deed:** Destroys all nonland permanents CMC X or less.
- **Phyrexian Tower:** Sacs creatures for BB. Sacs Explorer at instant speed.

### Historical Timeline

**2011** (tier 3, ~1%)
Nic Fit emerges exploiting Legacy's low basic land counts.
- [Veteran Explorer](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Veteran+Explorer%22) + [Cabal Therapy](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Cabal+Therapy%22) engine

**2014** (tier 3, ~1.5%)
Peak popularity. [Siege Rhino](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Siege+Rhino%22) makes Abzan preferred.
- [Siege Rhino](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Siege+Rhino%22) added
- Abzan builds popular

**2023** (fringe, ~0.3%)
Bowmasters and power creep push to fringes.
- Power creep outpaces the strategy

**2026** (fringe, ~0.2%)
Fringe at 0.2%. Beloved pet deck.
- Loyal pilots only

**Frequency of Change:** low
**Change Notes:** [Veteran Explorer](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Veteran+Explorer%22) + [Cabal Therapy](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Cabal+Therapy%22) is the unchanging core. Splash colors vary.

## Food Chain

**Also known as:** [Food Chain](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Food+Chain%22) Combo, [Eternal Scourge](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Eternal+Scourge%22) Combo, FC Griffin

**Archetype:** combo
**Colors:** U, G
**Tier:** fringe
**Meta Share:** 0.2%
**Win Rate Estimate:** 47-49%
**Cost Estimate:** $2,800 (driven by [Tropical Island](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Tropical+Island%22), [Underground Sea](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Underground+Sea%22), [Force of Will](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Force+of+Will%22))
**First Appeared:** 2015
**Peak Meta Share:** 2017-2019
**Deck Count in Sample:** 3

A combo deck using [Food Chain](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Food+Chain%22) with [Misthollow Griffin](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Misthollow+Griffin%22) or [Eternal Scourge](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Eternal+Scourge%22) to generate infinite creature mana for [Walking Ballista](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Walking+Ballista%22).

### Decklist

**Main Deck:**

- 4 [Food Chain](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Food+Chain%22)
- 3 [Misthollow Griffin](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Misthollow+Griffin%22)
- 2 [Eternal Scourge](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Eternal+Scourge%22)
- 1 [Walking Ballista](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Walking+Ballista%22)
- 3 [Orcish Bowmasters](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Orcish+Bowmasters%22)
- 4 [Force of Will](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Force+of+Will%22)
- 4 [Brainstorm](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Brainstorm%22)
- 4 [Ponder](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Ponder%22)
- 2 [Force of Negation](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Force+of+Negation%22)
- 2 [Thoughtseize](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Thoughtseize%22)
- 2 [Abrupt Decay](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Abrupt+Decay%22)
- 3 [Manipulate Fate](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Manipulate+Fate%22)
- 3 [Once Upon a Time](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Once+Upon+a+Time%22)
- 2 [Tropical Island](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Tropical+Island%22)
- 2 [Underground Sea](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Underground+Sea%22)
- 1 [Bayou](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Bayou%22)
- 4 [Misty Rainforest](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Misty+Rainforest%22)
- 4 [Polluted Delta](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Polluted+Delta%22)
- 2 [Verdant Catacombs](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Verdant+Catacombs%22)
- 1 [Island](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Island%22)
- 1 [Forest](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Forest%22)
- 1 [Swamp](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Swamp%22)
- 3 [Wasteland](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Wasteland%22)
- 1 [Boseiju, Who Endures](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Boseiju%2C+Who+Endures%22)
- 1 [Otawara, Soaring City](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Otawara%2C+Soaring+City%22)

**Sideboard:**

- 2 [Flusterstorm](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Flusterstorm%22)
- 2 [Surgical Extraction](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Surgical+Extraction%22)
- 2 [Hydroblast](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Hydroblast%22)
- 2 [Endurance](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Endurance%22)
- 2 [Carpet of Flowers](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Carpet+of+Flowers%22)
- 1 [Collector Ouphe](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Collector+Ouphe%22)
- 2 [Plague Engineer](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Plague+Engineer%22)
- 2 [Veil of Summer](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Veil+of+Summer%22)

### Key Matchups

- **Favorable:** Lands, Death and Taxes, Burn
- **Unfavorable:** Dimir Tempo, Oops! All Spells, Izzet Delver
- **Even:** Sneak and Show, Painter, Beanstalk Control

**Similar Decks:** [Aluren](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Aluren%22), Sneak and Show
Like [Aluren](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Aluren%22), wins with an enchantment-based creature combo. Aluren is more competitive currently.

### Key Cards Explained

<img src="https://api.scryfall.com/cards/named?exact=Food+Chain&format=image&version=normal&set=mmq" alt="Food Chain" width="217"> <img src="https://api.scryfall.com/cards/named?exact=Misthollow+Griffin&format=image&version=normal&set=avr" alt="Misthollow Griffin" width="217"> <img src="https://api.scryfall.com/cards/named?exact=Manipulate+Fate&format=image&version=normal&set=inv" alt="Manipulate Fate" width="217">

- **Food Chain:** Exile a creature for CMC+1 mana, creature spells only. Infinite with exile-cast creatures.
- **Misthollow Griffin:** Cast from exile. Nets 1 mana each loop with [Food Chain](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Food+Chain%22).
- **Manipulate Fate:** Exiles 3 cards from library, draws a card. Sets up exile-cast creatures.
- **Walking Ballista:** Infinite mana outlet. Cast for X=infinite.

### Historical Timeline

**2015** (tier 3, ~1%)
[Food Chain](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Food+Chain%22) + [Misthollow Griffin](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Misthollow+Griffin%22) combo refined for Legacy.
- Core combo
- [Eternal Scourge](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Eternal+Scourge%22) as backup

**2018** (tier 2, ~2%)
Peak popularity. [Walking Ballista](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Walking+Ballista%22) as clean win condition.
- [Walking Ballista](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Walking+Ballista%22) added

**2023** (fringe, ~0.3%)
Power creep pushes deck down. Combo too slow.
- Outpaced by faster combos

**2026** (fringe, ~0.2%)
Fringe at 0.2%. Pet deck for combo enthusiasts.
- Unique but underpowered

**Frequency of Change:** low
**Change Notes:** Core combo is fixed. [Manipulate Fate](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Manipulate+Fate%22) exiles Griffins/Scourges for the combo.

---

## Enchantress

**Also known as:** GW Enchantress, Enchantress Prison, Enchantress Control

**Archetype:** prison
**Colors:** G, W
**Tier:** fringe
**Meta Share:** 0.2%
**Win Rate Estimate:** 46-48%
**Cost Estimate:** $1,400 (driven by [Serra's Sanctum](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Serra%27s+Sanctum%22), [Savannah](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Savannah%22), [Windswept Heath](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Windswept+Heath%22))
**First Appeared:** 1998
**Peak Meta Share:** 2009-2012
**Deck Count in Sample:** 3

A prison deck using [Argothian Enchantress](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Argothian+Enchantress%22) and [Enchantress's Presence](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Enchantress%27s+Presence%22) to draw cards off enchantments, locking opponents out with [Solitary Confinement](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Solitary+Confinement%22) and [Elephant Grass](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Elephant+Grass%22).

### Decklist

**Main Deck:**

- 4 [Argothian Enchantress](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Argothian+Enchantress%22)
- 4 [Enchantress's Presence](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Enchantress%27s+Presence%22)
- 4 [Sythis, Harvest's Hand](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Sythis%2C+Harvest%27s+Hand%22)
- 2 [Solitary Confinement](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Solitary+Confinement%22)
- 2 [Elephant Grass](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Elephant+Grass%22)
- 4 [Sterling Grove](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Sterling+Grove%22)
- 4 [Wild Growth](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Wild+Growth%22)
- 4 [Utopia Sprawl](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Utopia+Sprawl%22)
- 2 [Destiny Spinner](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Destiny+Spinner%22)
- 1 [Sigil of the Empty Throne](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Sigil+of+the+Empty+Throne%22)
- 2 [Rest in Peace](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Rest+in+Peace%22)
- 2 [Mirri's Guile](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Mirri%27s+Guile%22)
- 3 [Carpet of Flowers](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Carpet+of+Flowers%22)
- 3 [Banishing Light](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Banishing+Light%22)
- 1 [Serra's Sanctum](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Serra%27s+Sanctum%22)
- 4 [Windswept Heath](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Windswept+Heath%22)
- 2 [Savannah](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Savannah%22)
- 7 [Forest](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Forest%22)
- 2 [Plains](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Plains%22)
- 1 [Dryad Arbor](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Dryad+Arbor%22)
- 1 [Hall of Heliod's Generosity](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Hall+of+Heliod%27s+Generosity%22)
- 1 [Boseiju, Who Endures](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Boseiju%2C+Who+Endures%22)

**Sideboard:**

- 3 [Force of Vigor](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Force+of+Vigor%22)
- 2 [Choke](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Choke%22)
- 1 [Sphere of Safety](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Sphere+of+Safety%22)
- 3 [Leyline of Sanctity](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Leyline+of+Sanctity%22)
- 2 [Endurance](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Endurance%22)
- 2 [Containment Priest](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Containment+Priest%22)
- 1 [Energy Flux](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Energy+Flux%22)
- 1 [Aura of Silence](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Aura+of+Silence%22)

### Key Matchups

- **Favorable:** Dimir Tempo, Izzet Delver, Burn
- **Unfavorable:** Sneak and Show, Oops! All Spells, Painter
- **Even:** Lands, Death and Taxes, [Ocelot Pride](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Ocelot+Pride%22) Midrange

**Similar Decks:** Lands, [Cloudpost](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Cloudpost%22) Ramp
Like Lands, a non-blue prison deck aiming to lock the opponent out.

### Key Cards Explained

<img src="https://api.scryfall.com/cards/named?exact=Argothian+Enchantress&format=image&version=normal&set=usg" alt="Argothian Enchantress" width="217"> <img src="https://api.scryfall.com/cards/named?exact=Solitary+Confinement&format=image&version=normal&set=jud" alt="Solitary Confinement" width="217"> <img src="https://api.scryfall.com/cards/named?exact=Sterling+Grove&format=image&version=normal&set=inv" alt="Sterling Grove" width="217">

- **Argothian Enchantress:** Draws a card for each enchantment cast.
- **Solitary Confinement:** Can't be targeted and take no damage. Enchantress draws fuel the upkeep discard.
- **Sterling Grove:** Gives enchantments shroud and sacs to tutor.
- **Elephant Grass:** Opponents must pay mana to attack.

### Historical Timeline

**1998** (tier 3, ~1%)
[Argothian Enchantress](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Argothian+Enchantress%22) from [Urza's Saga](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Urza%27s+Saga%22) enables enchantment strategies.
- Enchantress as engine

**2009** (tier 3, ~1.5%)
Viable Legacy deck with [Solitary Confinement](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Solitary+Confinement%22) lock.
- [Enchantress's Presence](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Enchantress%27s+Presence%22)
- [Solitary Confinement](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Solitary+Confinement%22) lock

**2021** (tier 3, ~0.5%)
Sythis from MH2 adds a third efficient enchantress.
- Sythis added

**2026** (fringe, ~0.2%)
Fringe at 0.2%. Niche prison deck beloved by loyal pilots.
- Niche prison role

**Frequency of Change:** low
**Change Notes:** Sythis from MH2 was a huge upgrade. Otherwise very stable.

## High Tide

**Also known as:** Mono Blue Tide, Spiral Tide, [Time Spiral](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Time+Spiral%22) Tide

**Archetype:** combo
**Colors:** U
**Tier:** historic
**Meta Share:** 0%
**Win Rate Estimate:** N/A (historic)
**Cost Estimate:** $4,000 (driven by [Candelabra of Tawnos](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Candelabra+of+Tawnos%22), [Time Spiral](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Time+Spiral%22), [Force of Will](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Force+of+Will%22))
**First Appeared:** 1995
**Peak Meta Share:** 2005-2010
**Deck Count in Sample:** 0

A mono-blue combo deck using [High Tide](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22High+Tide%22) to double [Island](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Island%22) mana, then untapping with [Time Spiral](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Time+Spiral%22) and [Turnabout](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Turnabout%22) to generate massive mana and win with [Blue Sun's Zenith](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Blue+Sun%27s+Zenith%22) or [Brain Freeze](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Brain+Freeze%22).

### Decklist

**Main Deck:**

- 4 [High Tide](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22High+Tide%22)
- 4 [Time Spiral](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Time+Spiral%22)
- 3 [Turnabout](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Turnabout%22)
- 2 [Candelabra of Tawnos](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Candelabra+of+Tawnos%22)
- 1 [Blue Sun's Zenith](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Blue+Sun%27s+Zenith%22)
- 1 [Brain Freeze](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Brain+Freeze%22)
- 4 [Brainstorm](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Brainstorm%22)
- 4 [Ponder](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Ponder%22)

- 3 [Merchant Scroll](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Merchant+Scroll%22)
- 3 [Cunning Wish](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Cunning+Wish%22)
- 4 [Force of Will](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Force+of+Will%22)
- 2 [Flusterstorm](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Flusterstorm%22)
- 2 [Snap](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Snap%22)
- 12 [Island](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Island%22)
- 2 [Flooded Strand](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Flooded+Strand%22)
- 2 [Polluted Delta](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Polluted+Delta%22)
- 2 [Misty Rainforest](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Misty+Rainforest%22)
- 1 [Mystic Sanctuary](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Mystic+Sanctuary%22)

**Sideboard:**

- 1 [Brain Freeze](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Brain+Freeze%22)
- 1 [Blue Sun's Zenith](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Blue+Sun%27s+Zenith%22)
- 1 [Surgical Extraction](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Surgical+Extraction%22)
- 1 [Flusterstorm](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Flusterstorm%22)
- 2 [Hydroblast](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Hydroblast%22)
- 2 [Pact of Negation](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Pact+of+Negation%22)
- 1 [Echoing Truth](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Echoing+Truth%22)
- 1 [Rebuild](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Rebuild%22)
- 1 [Turnabout](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Turnabout%22)
