- 1 [Snap](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Snap%22)
- 1 [Wipe Away](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Wipe+Away%22)
- 1 [Blue Elemental Blast](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Blue+Elemental+Blast%22)

### Key Matchups

- **Favorable:** Lands, Death and Taxes, Elves
- **Unfavorable:** Dimir Tempo, Izzet Delver, Red Stompy
- **Even:** Sneak and Show, The EPIC Storm, [Doomsday](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Doomsday%22)

**Similar Decks:** [Doomsday](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Doomsday%22), Omni-Tell
Fellow blue combo deck aiming to win in one turn. Requires careful sequencing.

### Key Cards Explained

<img src="https://api.scryfall.com/cards/named?exact=High+Tide&format=image&version=normal&set=fem" alt="High Tide" width="217"> <img src="https://api.scryfall.com/cards/named?exact=Time+Spiral&format=image&version=normal&set=usg" alt="Time Spiral" width="217"> <img src="https://api.scryfall.com/cards/named?exact=Candelabra+of+Tawnos&format=image&version=normal&set=atq" alt="Candelabra of Tawnos" width="217">

- **High Tide:** Islands produce an additional U until end of turn.
- **Time Spiral:** Untaps up to six lands, each player draws seven. Nets massive mana with [High Tide](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22High+Tide%22).
- **Candelabra of Tawnos:** Taps for X to untap X lands. Doubles mana with [High Tide](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22High+Tide%22).
- **Cunning Wish:** Instant-speed tutor from sideboard.

### Historical Timeline

**1995** (tier 2, ~2%)
[High Tide](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22High+Tide%22) from Fallen Empires combined with untap effects creates early combo.
- [High Tide](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22High+Tide%22) as mana engine

**2005** (tier 2, ~3%)
Peak viability. Specialists like Feline Longmore put up results.
- [Time Spiral](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Time+Spiral%22) as combo piece
- Candelabra for mana multiplication

**2015** (tier 3, ~0.5%)
Format too fast. [High Tide](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22High+Tide%22) too slow and fragile.
- Format too fast

**2023** (historic, ~0%)
Effectively unplayable in Bowmasters era.
- No longer viable

### Bans Impact

- **Frantic Search** (2003-06): Banned early in Legacy. Would have been another untap effect.

**Frequency of Change:** N/A
**Change Notes:** Historic deck. Last competitively relevant around 2015. Format too hostile for slow mono-blue combo.

---

## Belcher

**Also known as:** [Goblin Charbelcher](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Goblin+Charbelcher%22), All-In Belcher, Land-Light Belcher

**Archetype:** combo
**Colors:** R, G
**Tier:** fringe
**Meta Share:** 0.1%
**Win Rate Estimate:** 45-48%
**Cost Estimate:** $800 (driven by [Lion's Eye Diamond](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Lion%27s+Eye+Diamond%22), [Chrome Mox](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Chrome+Mox%22))
**First Appeared:** 2004
**Peak Meta Share:** 2008-2010
**Deck Count in Sample:** 2

An all-in combo deck playing zero or one lands, using fast mana to activate [Goblin Charbelcher](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Goblin+Charbelcher%22) for lethal damage when no lands remain in library.

### Decklist

**Main Deck:**

- 4 [Goblin Charbelcher](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Goblin+Charbelcher%22)
- 4 [Lion's Eye Diamond](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Lion%27s+Eye+Diamond%22)
- 4 [Lotus Petal](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Lotus+Petal%22)
- 4 [Chrome Mox](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Chrome+Mox%22)
- 4 [Elvish Spirit Guide](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Elvish+Spirit+Guide%22)
- 4 [Simian Spirit Guide](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Simian+Spirit+Guide%22)
- 4 [Land Grant](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Land+Grant%22)
- 4 [Rite of Flame](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Rite+of+Flame%22)
- 4 [Desperate Ritual](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Desperate+Ritual%22)
- 4 [Pyretic Ritual](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Pyretic+Ritual%22)
- 4 [Burning Wish](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Burning+Wish%22)
- 2 [Empty the Warrens](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Empty+the+Warrens%22)
- 4 [Seething Song](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Seething+Song%22)
- 1 [Taiga](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Taiga%22)
- 4 [Chancellor of the Tangle](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Chancellor+of+the+Tangle%22)
- 4 [Manamorphose](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Manamorphose%22)
- 1 [Irencrag Feat](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Irencrag+Feat%22)

**Sideboard:**

- 2 [Empty the Warrens](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Empty+the+Warrens%22)
- 1 [Grapeshot](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Grapeshot%22)
- 1 [Shattering Spree](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Shattering+Spree%22)
- 1 [Pulverize](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Pulverize%22)
- 1 [Reverent Silence](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Reverent+Silence%22)
- 3 [Defense Grid](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Defense+Grid%22)
- 2 [Xantid Swarm](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Xantid+Swarm%22)
- 2 [Pyroblast](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Pyroblast%22)
- 2 [Veil of Summer](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Veil+of+Summer%22)

### Key Matchups

- **Favorable:** Lands, Death and Taxes, Elves
- **Unfavorable:** Dimir Tempo, Izzet Delver, The EPIC Storm
- **Even:** Red Stompy, Burn, Eldrazi

**Similar Decks:** Oops! All Spells, The EPIC Storm, Ruby Storm
Like Oops, wins with almost no lands. Both fold to [Force of Will](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Force+of+Will%22) but are blazing fast.

### Key Cards Explained

<img src="https://api.scryfall.com/cards/named?exact=Goblin+Charbelcher&format=image&version=normal&set=mrd" alt="Goblin Charbelcher" width="217"> <img src="https://api.scryfall.com/cards/named?exact=Lion%27s+Eye+Diamond&format=image&version=normal&set=mir" alt="Lion's Eye Diamond" width="217"> <img src="https://api.scryfall.com/cards/named?exact=Empty+the+Warrens&format=image&version=normal&set=tsp" alt="Empty the Warrens" width="217">

- **Goblin Charbelcher:** Activate for 3 to reveal until a land, dealing that much damage. With 0-1 lands, lethal.
- **Lion's Eye Diamond:** Discard hand for 3 mana. With [Burning Wish](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Burning+Wish%22), cast Wish first then crack LED.
- **Empty the Warrens:** Backup plan creating goblin tokens.
- **Land Grant:** Reveals hand to search for a [Forest](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Forest%22) ([Taiga](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Taiga%22)). Free spell.

### Historical Timeline

**2004** (tier 3, ~1%)
Charbelcher combo discovered for Legacy.
- Charbelcher as win condition
- Zero-land mana base

**2009** (tier 3, ~1%)
Consistent fringe combo. Folds to [Force of Will](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Force+of+Will%22).
- Budget-friendly combo

**2020** (fringe, ~0.3%)
[Chancellor of the Tangle](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Chancellor+of+the+Tangle%22) provides free mana.
- Chancellor added

**2026** (fringe, ~0.1%)
Fringe at 0.1%. Ultra-budget combo.
- Not competitively viable

**Frequency of Change:** low
**Change Notes:** Very stable. [Chancellor of the Tangle](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Chancellor+of+the+Tangle%22) and [Irencrag Feat](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Irencrag+Feat%22) were recent additions.

---

## Stiflenought

**Also known as:** UB Stiflenought, [Stifle](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Stifle%22) Dreadnought, Phyrexian Nought

**Archetype:** tempo
**Colors:** U, B
**Tier:** fringe
**Meta Share:** 0.1%
**Win Rate Estimate:** 46-48%
**Cost Estimate:** $2,800 (driven by [Underground Sea](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Underground+Sea%22), [Force of Will](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Force+of+Will%22), [Wasteland](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Wasteland%22))
**First Appeared:** 2006
**Peak Meta Share:** 2008-2010
**Deck Count in Sample:** 2

A tempo deck using [Stifle](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Stifle%22) to counter [Phyrexian Dreadnought](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Phyrexian+Dreadnought%22)'s sacrifice trigger, creating a 12/12 trampler for two mana total.

### Decklist

**Main Deck:**

- 4 [Phyrexian Dreadnought](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Phyrexian+Dreadnought%22)
- 4 [Stifle](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Stifle%22)
- 3 [Dress Down](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Dress+Down%22)
- 4 [Brainstorm](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Brainstorm%22)
- 4 [Ponder](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Ponder%22)
- 4 [Force of Will](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Force+of+Will%22)
- 4 [Daze](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Daze%22)
- 2 [Spell Pierce](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Spell+Pierce%22)
- 3 [Thoughtseize](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Thoughtseize%22)
- 3 [Orcish Bowmasters](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Orcish+Bowmasters%22)
- 3 [Murktide Regent](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Murktide+Regent%22)
- 2 [Fatal Push](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Fatal+Push%22)
- 4 [Polluted Delta](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Polluted+Delta%22)
- 3 [Misty Rainforest](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Misty+Rainforest%22)
- 3 [Underground Sea](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Underground+Sea%22)
- 1 [Watery Grave](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Watery+Grave%22)
- 2 [Island](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Island%22)
- 1 [Swamp](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Swamp%22)
- 4 [Wasteland](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Wasteland%22)
- 1 [Otawara, Soaring City](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Otawara%2C+Soaring+City%22)
- 1 [Snuff Out](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Snuff+Out%22)

**Sideboard:**

- 2 [Surgical Extraction](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Surgical+Extraction%22)
- 2 [Hydroblast](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Hydroblast%22)
- 2 [Flusterstorm](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Flusterstorm%22)
- 2 [Plague Engineer](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Plague+Engineer%22)
- 1 [Nihil Spellbomb](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Nihil+Spellbomb%22)
- 1 [Force of Negation](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Force+of+Negation%22)
- 1 [Dismember](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Dismember%22)
- 1 [Subtlety](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Subtlety%22)
- 1 [Stern Scolding](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Stern+Scolding%22)
- 1 [Sheoldred's Edict](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Sheoldred%27s+Edict%22)
- 1 [Massacre](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Massacre%22)

### Key Matchups

- **Favorable:** Lands, Beanstalk Control, Burn
- **Unfavorable:** [Ocelot Pride](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Ocelot+Pride%22) Midrange, Death and Taxes, Painter
- **Even:** Dimir Tempo, Izzet Delver, Sneak and Show

**Similar Decks:** Dimir Tempo, [Death's Shadow](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Death%27s+Shadow%22)
Essentially Dimir Tempo with [Stifle](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Stifle%22)/Dreadnought instead of Tamiyo and [Barrowgoyf](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Barrowgoyf%22). Trades consistency for explosive potential.

### Key Cards Explained

<img src="https://api.scryfall.com/cards/named?exact=Phyrexian+Dreadnought&format=image&version=normal&set=mir" alt="Phyrexian Dreadnought" width="217"> <img src="https://api.scryfall.com/cards/named?exact=Stifle&format=image&version=normal&set=scg" alt="Stifle" width="217"> <img src="https://api.scryfall.com/cards/named?exact=Dress+Down&format=image&version=normal&set=mh2" alt="Dress Down" width="217">

- **Phyrexian Dreadnought:** 12/12 trampler for 1 with sacrifice trigger. [Stifle](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Stifle%22) negates it.
- **Stifle:** Counters triggered ability for U. Also hits fetchlands.
- **Dress Down:** Removes all abilities. Dreadnought enters as vanilla 12/12.
- **Wasteland:** Compounds the mana denial angle with [Stifle](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Stifle%22) on fetchlands.

### Historical Timeline

**2006** (tier 2, ~2%)
[Stifle](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Stifle%22) + Dreadnought becomes a Legacy staple interaction.
- Combo discovered
- Tempo shell

**2010** (tier 2, ~2%)
Peak popularity in various tempo shells.
- Multiple shell variants

**2021** (tier 3, ~0.5%)
[Dress Down](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Dress+Down%22) from MH2 as backup enabler. Brief renewed interest.
- [Dress Down](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Dress+Down%22) added

**2026** (fringe, ~0.1%)
Fringe at 0.1%. Dimir Tempo is strictly better.
- Outclassed by Dimir Tempo

**Frequency of Change:** low
**Change Notes:** [Dress Down](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Dress+Down%22) from MH2 provides an additional way to negate the trigger.

---

## Merfolk

**Also known as:** Fish, Mono Blue Merfolk, UW Merfolk

**Archetype:** aggro
**Colors:** U
**Tier:** fringe
**Meta Share:** 0.2%
**Win Rate Estimate:** 46-48%
**Cost Estimate:** $1,400 (driven by [Force of Will](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Force+of+Will%22), [Cavern of Souls](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Cavern+of+Souls%22), [True-Name Nemesis](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22True-Name+Nemesis%22))
**First Appeared:** 2008
**Peak Meta Share:** 2010-2013
**Deck Count in Sample:** 3

A tribal aggro deck using lord effects for unblockable islandwalk damage. Combines [Aether Vial](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Aether+Vial%22) with [Force of Will](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Force+of+Will%22) for aggro-control.

### Decklist

**Main Deck:**

- 4 [Lord of Atlantis](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Lord+of+Atlantis%22)
- 4 [Master of the Pearl Trident](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Master+of+the+Pearl+Trident%22)
- 4 [True-Name Nemesis](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22True-Name+Nemesis%22)
- 4 [Silvergill Adept](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Silvergill+Adept%22)
- 4 [Vodalian Hexcatcher](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Vodalian+Hexcatcher%22)
- 2 [Svyelun of Sea and Sky](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Svyelun+of+Sea+and+Sky%22)
- 2 [Harbinger of the Tides](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Harbinger+of+the+Tides%22)
- 2 [Tide Shaper](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Tide+Shaper%22)
- 4 [Aether Vial](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Aether+Vial%22)
- 4 [Force of Will](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Force+of+Will%22)
- 2 [Force of Negation](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Force+of+Negation%22)
- 2 [Chalice of the Void](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Chalice+of+the+Void%22)
- 4 [Mutavault](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Mutavault%22)
- 4 [Cavern of Souls](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Cavern+of+Souls%22)
- 6 [Island](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Island%22)
- 4 [Wasteland](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Wasteland%22)
- 2 [Rishadan Port](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Rishadan+Port%22)
- 1 [Otawara, Soaring City](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Otawara%2C+Soaring+City%22)
- 1 [Minamo, School at Water's Edge](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Minamo%2C+School+at+Water%27s+Edge%22)

**Sideboard:**

- 2 [Hydroblast](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Hydroblast%22)
- 2 [Flusterstorm](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Flusterstorm%22)
- 2 [Subtlety](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Subtlety%22)
- 1 [Dismember](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Dismember%22)
- 2 [Surgical Extraction](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Surgical+Extraction%22)
- 2 [Grafdigger's Cage](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Grafdigger%27s+Cage%22)
- 2 [Torpor Orb](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Torpor+Orb%22)
- 2 [Mindbreak Trap](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Mindbreak+Trap%22)

### Key Matchups

- **Favorable:** Jeskai Control, Beanstalk Control, Burn
- **Unfavorable:** [Ocelot Pride](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Ocelot+Pride%22) Midrange, Eldrazi, Painter
- **Even:** Dimir Tempo, Izzet Delver, Death and Taxes

**Similar Decks:** Goblins, Death and Taxes
Tribal [Aether Vial](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Aether+Vial%22) deck like Goblins. Uniquely has [Force of Will](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Force+of+Will%22) access among tribal decks.

### Key Cards Explained

<img src="https://api.scryfall.com/cards/named?exact=Lord+of+Atlantis&format=image&version=normal&set=lea" alt="Lord of Atlantis" width="217"> <img src="https://api.scryfall.com/cards/named?exact=True-Name+Nemesis&format=image&version=normal&set=c13" alt="True-Name Nemesis" width="217"> <img src="https://api.scryfall.com/cards/named?exact=Vodalian+Hexcatcher&format=image&version=normal&set=dmu" alt="Vodalian Hexcatcher" width="217">

- **Lord of Atlantis:** All merfolk get +1/+1 and islandwalk. Unblockable vs blue decks.
- **True-Name Nemesis:** Protection from a chosen player. Untargetable, unblockable.
- **Vodalian Hexcatcher:** Lord with flash that sacs merfolk to counter noncreature spells.
- **Aether Vial:** Cheats merfolk in at instant speed.

### Historical Timeline

**2008** (tier 2, ~3%)
Merfolk tribal becomes competitive with critical mass of lords.
- Lord tribal core
- [Aether Vial](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Aether+Vial%22) for tempo

**2013** (tier 2, ~3%)
[True-Name Nemesis](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22True-Name+Nemesis%22) is a massive upgrade.
- [True-Name Nemesis](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22True-Name+Nemesis%22) added

**2022** (tier 3, ~0.5%)
[Vodalian Hexcatcher](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Vodalian+Hexcatcher%22) adds a counterspell lord.
- Hexcatcher added

**2023** (fringe, ~0.3%)
Bowmasters rough for small creatures.
- Bowmasters hurts small creatures

**2026** (fringe, ~0.2%)
Fringe at 0.2%. Loyal tribe with FoW edge.
- [Force of Will](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Force+of+Will%22) gives unique edge

**Frequency of Change:** low
**Change Notes:** [Vodalian Hexcatcher](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Vodalian+Hexcatcher%22) from Dominaria United was a major addition. Svyelun from MH2 added card advantage.

## MUD

**Also known as:** Colorless Stompy, [Metalworker](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Metalworker%22) Stompy, Steel Stompy

**Archetype:** stompy
**Colors:** C
**Tier:** tier 3
**Meta Share:** 0.5%
**Win Rate Estimate:** 48-50%
**Cost Estimate:** $2,000 (driven by [City of Traitors](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22City+of+Traitors%22), [Ancient Tomb](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Ancient+Tomb%22), [Metalworker](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Metalworker%22), [Grim Monolith](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Grim+Monolith%22))
**First Appeared:** 2009
**Peak Meta Share:** 2015-2017
**Deck Count in Sample:** 8

A colorless artifact stompy deck using [Metalworker](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Metalworker%22) and [Ancient Tomb](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Ancient+Tomb%22) to power out threats, backed by Chalice and [Trinisphere](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Trinisphere%22).

### Decklist

**Main Deck:**

- 4 [Metalworker](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Metalworker%22)
- 4 [Karn, the Great Creator](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Karn%2C+the+Great+Creator%22)
- 2 [Karn, Scion of Urza](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Karn%2C+Scion+of+Urza%22)
- 3 [Wurmcoil Engine](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Wurmcoil+Engine%22)
- 3 [Walking Ballista](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Walking+Ballista%22)
- 1 [Steel Hellkite](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Steel+Hellkite%22)
- 3 [Lodestone Golem](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Lodestone+Golem%22)
- 4 [Chalice of the Void](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Chalice+of+the+Void%22)
- 3 [Trinisphere](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Trinisphere%22)
- 4 [Grim Monolith](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Grim+Monolith%22)
- 3 [Voltaic Key](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Voltaic+Key%22)
- 1 [Staff of Domination](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Staff+of+Domination%22)
- 4 [Ancient Tomb](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Ancient+Tomb%22)
- 4 [City of Traitors](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22City+of+Traitors%22)
- 4 [Wasteland](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Wasteland%22)
- 4 [Mishra's Factory](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Mishra%27s+Factory%22)
- 4 [Urza's Saga](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Urza%27s+Saga%22)
- 1 [Inventors' Fair](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Inventors%27+Fair%22)
- 1 [Blast Zone](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Blast+Zone%22)
- 1 [Eye of Ugin](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Eye+of+Ugin%22)
- 2 [Mystic Forge](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Mystic+Forge%22)

**Sideboard:**

- 1 [Ensnaring Bridge](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Ensnaring+Bridge%22)
- 1 [Tormod's Crypt](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Tormod%27s+Crypt%22)
- 1 [Pithing Needle](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Pithing+Needle%22)
- 1 [Liquimetal Coating](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Liquimetal+Coating%22)
- 1 [Mycosynth Lattice](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Mycosynth+Lattice%22)
- 1 [Ratchet Bomb](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Ratchet+Bomb%22)
- 1 [Crucible of Worlds](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Crucible+of+Worlds%22)
- 1 [Grafdigger's Cage](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Grafdigger%27s+Cage%22)
- 1 [Trinisphere](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Trinisphere%22)
- 1 [Spine of Ish Sah](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Spine+of+Ish+Sah%22)
- 1 [Wurmcoil Engine](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Wurmcoil+Engine%22)
- 2 [Defense Grid](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Defense+Grid%22)
- 2 [Mindbreak Trap](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Mindbreak+Trap%22)

### Key Matchups

- **Favorable:** Dimir Tempo, Izzet Delver, [Doomsday](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Doomsday%22)
- **Unfavorable:** [Ocelot Pride](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Ocelot+Pride%22) Midrange, Lands, Painter
- **Even:** Sneak and Show, Eldrazi, Red Stompy

**Similar Decks:** Eldrazi, Red Stompy, [Mystic Forge](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Mystic+Forge%22) Combo
Shares Chalice + fast mana shell with Eldrazi and Red Stompy. More artifact-focused with [Metalworker](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Metalworker%22).

### Key Cards Explained

<img src="https://api.scryfall.com/cards/named?exact=Metalworker&format=image&version=normal&set=usg" alt="Metalworker" width="217"> <img src="https://api.scryfall.com/cards/named?exact=Chalice+of+the+Void&format=image&version=normal&set=mrd" alt="Chalice of the Void" width="217"> <img src="https://api.scryfall.com/cards/named?exact=Karn%2C+the+Great+Creator&format=image&version=normal&set=war" alt="Karn, the Great Creator" width="217">

- **Metalworker:** Taps to reveal artifacts from hand, adding 2 colorless each.
- **Chalice of the Void:** On one, counters most of Legacy's best spells.
- **Karn, the Great Creator:** Shuts off artifacts and wishes for silver bullets.
- **Trinisphere:** All spells cost at least 3. Devastating against cantrip decks.

### Historical Timeline

**2009** (tier 3, ~1%)
MUD emerges using [Metalworker](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Metalworker%22) and artifact mana.
- [Metalworker](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Metalworker%22) as mana engine
- Chalice + [Trinisphere](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Trinisphere%22) lock

**2016** (tier 2, ~2%)
Peak popularity. [Walking Ballista](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Walking+Ballista%22) as great mana sink.
- [Walking Ballista](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Walking+Ballista%22) added

**2019** (tier 3, ~1%)
Karn wishboard transforms the deck.
- Karn wishboard
- [Mystic Forge](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Mystic+Forge%22) added

**2026** (tier 3, ~0.5%)
Tier 3 at 0.5%. Competes with other stompy variants.
- Unique [Metalworker](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Metalworker%22) angle

**Frequency of Change:** low
**Change Notes:** Karn wishboard and [Urza's Saga](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Urza%27s+Saga%22) are the main recent innovations.

---

## Ninjas

**Also known as:** UB Ninjas, Ninja Tempo, Yuriko Ninjas

**Archetype:** tempo
**Colors:** U, B
**Tier:** fringe
**Meta Share:** 0.2%
**Win Rate Estimate:** 46-48%
**Cost Estimate:** $2,400 (driven by [Underground Sea](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Underground+Sea%22), [Force of Will](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Force+of+Will%22), [Wasteland](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Wasteland%22))
**First Appeared:** 2018
**Peak Meta Share:** 2019-2020
**Deck Count in Sample:** 3

A tempo deck using evasive creatures to enable ninjutsu, primarily Yuriko. Yuriko's trigger drains based on revealed card's mana value.

### Decklist

**Main Deck:**

- 4 [Yuriko, the Tiger's Shadow](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Yuriko%2C+the+Tiger%27s+Shadow%22)
- 4 [Changeling Outcast](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Changeling+Outcast%22)
- 4 [Ornithopter](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Ornithopter%22)
- 4 [Ingenious Infiltrator](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Ingenious+Infiltrator%22)
- 3 [Moon-Circuit Hacker](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Moon-Circuit+Hacker%22)
- 4 [Brainstorm](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Brainstorm%22)
- 4 [Ponder](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Ponder%22)
- 4 [Force of Will](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Force+of+Will%22)
- 3 [Daze](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Daze%22)
- 3 [Fatal Push](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Fatal+Push%22)
- 1 [Snuff Out](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Snuff+Out%22)
- 2 [Retrofitter Foundry](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Retrofitter+Foundry%22)
- 4 [Polluted Delta](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Polluted+Delta%22)
- 3 [Misty Rainforest](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Misty+Rainforest%22)
- 3 [Underground Sea](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Underground+Sea%22)
- 1 [Watery Grave](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Watery+Grave%22)
- 2 [Island](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Island%22)
- 1 [Swamp](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Swamp%22)
- 3 [Wasteland](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Wasteland%22)
- 1 [Otawara, Soaring City](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Otawara%2C+Soaring+City%22)
- 2 [Urza's Saga](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Urza%27s+Saga%22)

**Sideboard:**

- 2 [Surgical Extraction](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Surgical+Extraction%22)
- 2 [Hydroblast](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Hydroblast%22)
- 1 [Force of Negation](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Force+of+Negation%22)
- 2 [Plague Engineer](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Plague+Engineer%22)
- 2 [Flusterstorm](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Flusterstorm%22)
- 1 [Nihil Spellbomb](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Nihil+Spellbomb%22)
- 1 [Dismember](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Dismember%22)
- 1 [Subtlety](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Subtlety%22)
- 1 [Sheoldred's Edict](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Sheoldred%27s+Edict%22)
- 1 [Pithing Needle](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Pithing+Needle%22)
- 1 [Stern Scolding](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Stern+Scolding%22)

### Key Matchups

- **Favorable:** Jeskai Control, Beanstalk Control, Burn
- **Unfavorable:** [Ocelot Pride](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Ocelot+Pride%22) Midrange, Eldrazi, Red Stompy
- **Even:** Dimir Tempo, Izzet Delver, Painter

**Similar Decks:** Dimir Tempo, Stiflenought
Shares UB tempo shell with Dimir Tempo but replaces threats with ninja package.

### Key Cards Explained

<img src="https://api.scryfall.com/cards/named?exact=Yuriko%2C+the+Tiger%27s+Shadow&format=image&version=normal&set=c18" alt="Yuriko, the Tiger's Shadow" width="217"> <img src="https://api.scryfall.com/cards/named?exact=Changeling+Outcast&format=image&version=normal&set=mh1" alt="Changeling Outcast" width="217"> <img src="https://api.scryfall.com/cards/named?exact=Ingenious+Infiltrator&format=image&version=normal&set=mh1" alt="Ingenious Infiltrator" width="217">

- **Yuriko, the Tiger's Shadow:** Commander ninjutsu for UB bypasses command tax. Drains on combat damage.
- **Changeling Outcast:** Unblockable 1/1 for B. Perfect ninjutsu enabler.
- **Ingenious Infiltrator:** Draws a card whenever any ninja deals combat damage.
- **Brainstorm:** Puts high-MV cards on top for Yuriko to reveal.

### Historical Timeline

**2018** (tier 3, ~1%)
Yuriko from Commander 2018 creates a new archetype.
- Yuriko as build-around

**2020** (tier 3, ~1.5%)
Peak popularity with [Ingenious Infiltrator](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Ingenious+Infiltrator%22).
- Infiltrator added

**2023** (fringe, ~0.3%)
Bowmasters kills enabler creatures.
- Bowmasters hurts enablers

**2026** (fringe, ~0.2%)
Fringe at 0.2%. Fun alternative to Dimir Tempo.
- Pet deck for ninja fans

**Frequency of Change:** low
**Change Notes:** [Moon-Circuit Hacker](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Moon-Circuit+Hacker%22) from Kamigawa was a solid addition. Core ninja package stable.

---

## Esper Vial

**Also known as:** Esper Blade, WUB Vial, Esper Recruiter

**Archetype:** midrange
**Colors:** W, U, B
**Tier:** fringe
**Meta Share:** 0.2%
**Win Rate Estimate:** 46-48%
**Cost Estimate:** $3,000 (driven by [Tundra](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Tundra%22), [Underground Sea](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Underground+Sea%22), [Scrubland](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Scrubland%22), [Force of Will](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Force+of+Will%22))
**First Appeared:** 2015
**Peak Meta Share:** 2018-2019
**Deck Count in Sample:** 3

A creature toolbox deck using [Aether Vial](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Aether+Vial%22), [Stoneforge Mystic](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Stoneforge+Mystic%22), and [Recruiter of the Guard](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Recruiter+of+the+Guard%22) to assemble the right creatures for each matchup.

### Decklist

**Main Deck:**

- 4 [Aether Vial](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Aether+Vial%22)
- 4 [Stoneforge Mystic](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Stoneforge+Mystic%22)

- 2 [Thalia, Guardian of Thraben](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Thalia%2C+Guardian+of+Thraben%22)

- 1 [Kaldra Compleat](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Kaldra+Compleat%22)
- 4 [Swords to Plowshares](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Swords+to+Plowshares%22)
- 2 [Thoughtseize](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Thoughtseize%22)
- 2 [Force of Will](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Force+of+Will%22)
- 2 [Tundra](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Tundra%22)
- 1 [Scrubland](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Scrubland%22)
- 1 [Underground Sea](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Underground+Sea%22)
- 4 [Flooded Strand](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Flooded+Strand%22)
- 2 [Polluted Delta](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Polluted+Delta%22)
- 2 [Marsh Flats](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Marsh+Flats%22)
- 2 [Plains](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Plains%22)
- 1 [Island](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Island%22)
- 1 [Karakas](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Karakas%22)
- 2 [Cavern of Souls](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Cavern+of+Souls%22)
- 3 [Wasteland](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Wasteland%22)
- 2 [Rishadan Port](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Rishadan+Port%22)
- 1 [Eiganjo, Seat of the Empire](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Eiganjo%2C+Seat+of+the+Empire%22)

**Sideboard:**

- 2 [Surgical Extraction](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Surgical+Extraction%22)
- 2 [Containment Priest](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Containment+Priest%22)
- 2 [Meddling Mage](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Meddling+Mage%22)
- 1 [Ethersworn Canonist](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Ethersworn+Canonist%22)
- 2 [Hydroblast](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Hydroblast%22)
- 2 [Flusterstorm](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Flusterstorm%22)
- 1 [Council's Judgment](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Council%27s+Judgment%22)
- 1 [Dress Down](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Dress+Down%22)
- 2 [Leyline of the Void](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Leyline+of+the+Void%22)

### Key Matchups

- **Favorable:** Burn, LED Dredge, Jeskai Control
- **Unfavorable:** Sneak and Show, Oops! All Spells, Lands
- **Even:** Dimir Tempo, Death and Taxes, [Ocelot Pride](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Ocelot+Pride%22) Midrange

**Similar Decks:** Death and Taxes, Stoneblade, [Coveted Jewel](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Coveted+Jewel%22) Combo
A DnT variant adding blue and black for more interaction. Stoneblade is the spell-oriented version.

### Key Cards Explained

<img src="https://api.scryfall.com/cards/named?exact=Aether+Vial&format=image&version=normal&set=dst" alt="Aether Vial" width="217"> <img src="https://api.scryfall.com/cards/named?exact=Recruiter+of+the+Guard&format=image&version=normal&set=cn2" alt="Recruiter of the Guard" width="217"> <img src="https://api.scryfall.com/cards/named?exact=Stoneforge+Mystic&format=image&version=normal&set=wwk" alt="Stoneforge Mystic" width="217">

- **Aether Vial:** Cheats creatures in at instant speed for free.
- **Recruiter of the Guard:** Tutors for any creature with toughness 2 or less.
- **Stoneforge Mystic:** Tutors equipment and cheats it into play.
- **Solitude:** Free removal via pitch casting.

### Historical Timeline

**2015** (tier 3, ~0.5%)
[Recruiter of the Guard](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Recruiter+of+the+Guard%22) from Conspiracy 2 enables Esper toolbox.
- Recruiter as engine

**2019** (tier 3, ~1%)
Peak popularity with diverse toolbox.
- Peak results

**2023** (fringe, ~0.3%)
Bowmasters joins but also punishes small creatures.
- Bowmasters mixed blessing

**2026** (fringe, ~0.2%)
Fringe at 0.2%. DnT generally preferred.
- Niche toolbox option

**Frequency of Change:** medium
**Change Notes:** Bowmasters was a huge addition. Recruiter chains for specific answers.

## Jund

**Also known as:** BRG Midrange, Jund Midrange, RGB Good Stuff

**Archetype:** midrange
**Colors:** B, R, G
**Tier:** fringe
**Meta Share:** 0.2%
**Win Rate Estimate:** 46-48%
**Cost Estimate:** $2,200 (driven by [Badlands](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Badlands%22), [Bayou](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Bayou%22), [Ragavan, Nimble Pilferer](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Ragavan%2C+Nimble+Pilferer%22), [Liliana of the Veil](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Liliana+of+the+Veil%22))
**First Appeared:** 2009
**Peak Meta Share:** 2013-2015
**Deck Count in Sample:** 3

A three-color midrange deck combining the best discard, removal, and threats in BRG. [Barrowgoyf](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Barrowgoyf%22), [Thoughtseize](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Thoughtseize%22), [Lightning Bolt](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Lightning+Bolt%22) alongside green utility.

### Decklist

**Main Deck:**

- 4 [Barrowgoyf](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Barrowgoyf%22)
- 4 [Orcish Bowmasters](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Orcish+Bowmasters%22)
- 3 [Ragavan, Nimble Pilferer](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Ragavan%2C+Nimble+Pilferer%22)
- 2 [Endurance](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Endurance%22)
- 2 [Bloodbraid Elf](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Bloodbraid+Elf%22)
- 4 [Thoughtseize](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Thoughtseize%22)
- 4 [Lightning Bolt](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Lightning+Bolt%22)
- 3 [Abrupt Decay](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Abrupt+Decay%22)
- 2 [Fatal Push](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Fatal+Push%22)
- 3 [Hymn to Tourach](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Hymn+to+Tourach%22)
- 2 [Liliana of the Veil](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Liliana+of+the+Veil%22)
- 3 [Sylvan Library](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Sylvan+Library%22)
- 2 [Badlands](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Badlands%22)
- 2 [Bayou](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Bayou%22)
- 1 [Taiga](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Taiga%22)
- 4 [Bloodstained Mire](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Bloodstained+Mire%22)
- 4 [Verdant Catacombs](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Verdant+Catacombs%22)
- 2 [Wooded Foothills](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Wooded+Foothills%22)
- 1 [Swamp](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Swamp%22)
- 1 [Mountain](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Mountain%22)
- 1 [Forest](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Forest%22)
- 4 [Wasteland](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Wasteland%22)
- 2 [Nurturing Peatland](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Nurturing+Peatland%22)

**Sideboard:**

- 2 [Surgical Extraction](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Surgical+Extraction%22)
- 3 [Pyroblast](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Pyroblast%22)
- 2 [Force of Vigor](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Force+of+Vigor%22)
- 2 [Plague Engineer](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Plague+Engineer%22)
- 1 [Collector Ouphe](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Collector+Ouphe%22)
- 2 [Choke](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Choke%22)
- 2 [Torpor Orb](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Torpor+Orb%22)
- 1 [Pithing Needle](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Pithing+Needle%22)

### Key Matchups

- **Favorable:** Dimir Tempo, Izzet Delver, Burn
- **Unfavorable:** Sneak and Show, Oops! All Spells, Lands
- **Even:** [Ocelot Pride](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Ocelot+Pride%22) Midrange, Death and Taxes, Painter

**Similar Decks:** Nic Fit, Mardu Energy
Shares BG disruption with Nic Fit but without ramp. Mardu Energy is the preferred non-blue disruption aggro deck.

### Key Cards Explained

<img src="https://api.scryfall.com/cards/named?exact=Barrowgoyf&format=image&version=normal&set=mh3" alt="Barrowgoyf" width="217"> <img src="https://api.scryfall.com/cards/named?exact=Thoughtseize&format=image&version=normal&set=lrw" alt="Thoughtseize" width="217"> <img src="https://api.scryfall.com/cards/named?exact=Lightning+Bolt&format=image&version=normal&set=lea" alt="Lightning Bolt" width="217">

- **Barrowgoyf:** MH3 [Tarmogoyf](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Tarmogoyf%22) upgrade. Efficient threat with diverse graveyard types.
- **Thoughtseize:** Best discard spell in Magic.
- **Lightning Bolt:** Efficient removal that also goes to face.
- **Abrupt Decay:** Uncounterable removal for CMC 3 or less.

### Historical Timeline

**2009** (tier 3, ~1%)
Jund midrange appears in Legacy.
- Three-color midrange shell

**2013** (tier 2, ~2%)
DRS makes three-color mana consistent.
- [Deathrite Shaman](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Deathrite+Shaman%22) as fixer

**2018** (tier 3, ~0.5%)
DRS ban devastates the mana base.
- DRS banned
- Mana struggles

**2024** (fringe, ~0.3%)
[Barrowgoyf](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Barrowgoyf%22) from MH3 and Bowmasters bring some interest.
- [Barrowgoyf](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Barrowgoyf%22) replaces [Tarmogoyf](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Tarmogoyf%22)

**2026** (fringe, ~0.2%)
Fringe at 0.2%. Outclassed by blue decks.
- Mardu Energy preferred

### Bans Impact

- **Deathrite Shaman** (2018-07): Lost its best one-drop mana fixer. DRS held three-color bases together.

**Frequency of Change:** low
**Change Notes:** [Barrowgoyf](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Barrowgoyf%22) from MH3 replaced [Tarmogoyf](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Tarmogoyf%22). Without [Brainstorm](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Brainstorm%22), lacks card selection.

## Bomberman

**Also known as:** [Auriok Salvagers](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Auriok+Salvagers%22) Combo, LED Salvagers, Salvager Combo

**Archetype:** combo
**Colors:** W
**Tier:** historic
**Meta Share:** 0%
**Win Rate Estimate:** N/A (historic)
**Cost Estimate:** $3,500 (driven by [Lion's Eye Diamond](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Lion%27s+Eye+Diamond%22), [Tundra](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Tundra%22), [Force of Will](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Force+of+Will%22), [Mox Opal](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Mox+Opal%22))
**First Appeared:** 2005
**Peak Meta Share:** 2006-2008
**Deck Count in Sample:** 0

A combo deck using [Auriok Salvagers](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Auriok+Salvagers%22) with [Lion's Eye Diamond](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Lion%27s+Eye+Diamond%22) to generate infinite mana, fueling lethal [Pyrite Spellbomb](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Pyrite+Spellbomb%22) or [Walking Ballista](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Walking+Ballista%22).

**Sideboard:**

- 2 [Flusterstorm](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Flusterstorm%22)
- 2 [Containment Priest](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Containment+Priest%22)

- 1 [Dress Down](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Dress+Down%22)

- 1 [Force of Negation](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Force+of+Negation%22)

### Key Matchups

- **Favorable:** Lands, Death and Taxes, Burn
- **Unfavorable:** Dimir Tempo, Izzet Delver, Red Stompy
- **Even:** Sneak and Show, Painter, Beanstalk Control

**Similar Decks:** Painter, [Mystic Forge](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Mystic+Forge%22) Combo
Like Painter, an artifact combo in a fair shell. [Mystic Forge](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Mystic+Forge%22) uses similar artifact mana.

### Key Cards Explained

<img src="https://api.scryfall.com/cards/named?exact=Auriok+Salvagers&format=image&version=normal&set=5dn" alt="Auriok Salvagers" width="217"> <img src="https://api.scryfall.com/cards/named?exact=Lion%27s+Eye+Diamond&format=image&version=normal&set=mir" alt="Lion's Eye Diamond" width="217"> <img src="https://api.scryfall.com/cards/named?exact=Pyrite+Spellbomb&format=image&version=normal&set=mrd" alt="Pyrite Spellbomb" width="217">

- **Auriok Salvagers:** Returns artifact MV 1 or less from graveyard for 1W. Infinite loop with LED.
- **Lion's Eye Diamond:** Discard hand for 3 mana. With Salvagers, discard is irrelevant.
- **Pyrite Spellbomb:** 2 damage for R + sac. Recur infinitely for lethal.
- **Enlightened Tutor:** Finds LED or the kill condition.

### Historical Timeline

**2005** (tier 3, ~1%)
Salvagers + LED combo discovered.
- Infinite mana combo
- [Pyrite Spellbomb](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Pyrite+Spellbomb%22) kill

**2007** (tier 2, ~2%)
Peak viability with Stoneforge fair backup.
- Stoneforge backup
- [Enlightened Tutor](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Enlightened+Tutor%22) toolbox

**2015** (fringe, ~0.2%)
Power creep makes combo too slow.
- Four-mana combo creature too slow

**2020** (historic, ~0%)
Effectively historic. Painter is better in every way.
- Replaced by Painter

**Frequency of Change:** N/A
**Change Notes:** Historic deck last seen competitively around 2015. Combo too slow for modern Legacy.

---

## Hive Mind

**Also known as:** [Hive Mind](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Hive+Mind%22) Pacts, Show and Hive, Pact Combo

**Archetype:** combo
**Colors:** U, R
**Tier:** historic
**Meta Share:** 0%
**Win Rate Estimate:** N/A (historic)
**Cost Estimate:** $2,600 (driven by [Volcanic Island](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Volcanic+Island%22), [Force of Will](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Force+of+Will%22), [City of Traitors](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22City+of+Traitors%22), [Ancient Tomb](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Ancient+Tomb%22))
**First Appeared:** 2010
**Peak Meta Share:** 2011-2013
**Deck Count in Sample:** 0

A combo deck using [Show and Tell](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Show+and+Tell%22) for [Hive Mind](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Hive+Mind%22), then casting Pacts that the opponent copies but cannot pay for on their upkeep.

### Decklist

**Main Deck:**

- 4 [Hive Mind](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Hive+Mind%22)
- 4 [Show and Tell](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Show+and+Tell%22)

**Sideboard:**

- 2 [Flusterstorm](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Flusterstorm%22)

- 2 [Through the Breach](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Through+the+Breach%22)
- 1 [Emrakul, the Aeons Torn](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Emrakul%2C+the+Aeons+Torn%22)
- 1 [Omniscience](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Omniscience%22)
- 2 [Surgical Extraction](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Surgical+Extraction%22)
- 1 [Defense Grid](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Defense+Grid%22)

### Key Matchups

- **Favorable:** Lands, Death and Taxes, Burn
- **Unfavorable:** Dimir Tempo, Izzet Delver, Red Stompy
- **Even:** Sneak and Show, [Doomsday](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Doomsday%22), The EPIC Storm

**Similar Decks:** Sneak and Show, Omni-Tell
Shares [Show and Tell](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Show+and+Tell%22) shell with Sneak and Show but uses [Hive Mind](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Hive+Mind%22) + Pacts instead of creatures.

### Key Cards Explained

<img src="https://api.scryfall.com/cards/named?exact=Hive+Mind&format=image&version=normal&set=m10" alt="Hive Mind" width="217"> <img src="https://api.scryfall.com/cards/named?exact=Summoner%27s+Pact&format=image&version=normal&set=fut" alt="Summoner's Pact" width="217"> <img src="https://api.scryfall.com/cards/named?exact=Show+and+Tell&format=image&version=normal&set=usg" alt="Show and Tell" width="217">

- **Hive Mind:** Copies every instant/sorcery for all players. Pacts force unplayable upkeep costs.
- **Summoner's Pact:** Free spell. Opponent's copy requires 2GG next upkeep or lose.
- **Show and Tell:** Each player puts a permanent into play. You put [Hive Mind](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Hive+Mind%22).
- **Pact of Negation:** Free counter with 3UU upkeep. Opponent can't pay.

### Historical Timeline

**2010** (tier 2, ~2%)
[Hive Mind](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Hive+Mind%22) combo discovered using [Show and Tell](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Show+and+Tell%22) and Pacts.
- [Hive Mind](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Hive+Mind%22) + Pacts combo

**2012** (tier 2, ~2.5%)
Peak popularity as alternative to Sneak and Show.
- Wins through creature hosers

**2016** (tier 3, ~0.5%)
Sneak and Show proves more resilient. [Hive Mind](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Hive+Mind%22) fades.
- SnS preferred

**2020** (historic, ~0%)
Effectively historic. Omni-Tell is better.
- Replaced by Omni-Tell

**Frequency of Change:** N/A
**Change Notes:** Historic deck. Alternative to Sneak and Show that won through creature-hosing effects. Format outgrew it.

---

## UW Miracles

**Also known as:** Miracles, Post-Top Miracles, UW Control

**Archetype:** control
**Colors:** U, W
**Tier:** tier 3
**Meta Share:** 0.5%
**Win Rate Estimate:** 48-50%
**Cost Estimate:** $3,200 (driven by [Tundra](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Tundra%22), [Jace, the Mind Sculptor](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Jace%2C+the+Mind+Sculptor%22), [Force of Will](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Force+of+Will%22), [Flooded Strand](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Flooded+Strand%22))
**First Appeared:** 2017
**Peak Meta Share:** 2018-2019
**Deck Count in Sample:** 8

The post-[Sensei's Divining Top](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Sensei%27s+Divining+Top%22) version of Miracles. Uses [Terminus](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Terminus%22) and [Entreat the Angels](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Entreat+the+Angels%22) set up with [Brainstorm](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Brainstorm%22) and Jace rather than the banned Top.

### Decklist

**Main Deck:**

- 4 [Terminus](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Terminus%22)
- 2 [Entreat the Angels](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Entreat+the+Angels%22)
- 3 [Jace, the Mind Sculptor](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Jace%2C+the+Mind+Sculptor%22)
- 3 [Counterbalance](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Counterbalance%22)
- 4 [Force of Will](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Force+of+Will%22)
- 4 [Brainstorm](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Brainstorm%22)
- 4 [Ponder](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Ponder%22)
- 4 [Swords to Plowshares](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Swords+to+Plowshares%22)
- 3 [Counterspell](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Counterspell%22)
- 1 [Spell Pierce](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Spell+Pierce%22)
- 2 [Predict](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Predict%22)
- 2 [Accumulated Knowledge](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Accumulated+Knowledge%22)
- 2 [Snapcaster Mage](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Snapcaster+Mage%22)
- 1 [Shark Typhoon](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Shark+Typhoon%22)
- 4 [Flooded Strand](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Flooded+Strand%22)
- 2 [Polluted Delta](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Polluted+Delta%22)
- 2 [Misty Rainforest](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Misty+Rainforest%22)
- 4 [Tundra](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Tundra%22)
- 3 [Island](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Island%22)
- 2 [Plains](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Plains%22)
- 1 [Mystic Sanctuary](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Mystic+Sanctuary%22)
- 1 [Castle Vantress](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Castle+Vantress%22)
- 1 [Otawara, Soaring City](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Otawara%2C+Soaring+City%22)
- 1 [Karakas](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Karakas%22)

**Sideboard:**

- 2 [Flusterstorm](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Flusterstorm%22)
- 2 [Hydroblast](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Hydroblast%22)
- 2 [Surgical Extraction](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Surgical+Extraction%22)
- 2 [Containment Priest](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Containment+Priest%22)
- 1 [Dress Down](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Dress+Down%22)
- 1 [Force of Negation](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Force+of+Negation%22)
- 1 [Meddling Mage](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Meddling+Mage%22)
- 2 [Rest in Peace](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Rest+in+Peace%22)
- 1 [Disenchant](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Disenchant%22)
- 1 [Monastery Mentor](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Monastery+Mentor%22)

### Key Matchups

- **Favorable:** Eldrazi, Goblins, Elves
- **Unfavorable:** Dimir Tempo, Sneak and Show, Oops! All Spells
- **Even:** [Ocelot Pride](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Ocelot+Pride%22) Midrange, Death and Taxes, Lands

**Similar Decks:** Jeskai Control, Beanstalk Control, Stoneblade
Predecessor to Jeskai Control. Jeskai adds red for [Pyroblast](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Pyroblast%22) and Phlage. Beanstalk is more popular currently.

### Key Cards Explained

<img src="https://api.scryfall.com/cards/named?exact=Terminus&format=image&version=normal&set=avr" alt="Terminus" width="217"> <img src="https://api.scryfall.com/cards/named?exact=Counterbalance&format=image&version=normal&set=csp" alt="Counterbalance" width="217"> <img src="https://api.scryfall.com/cards/named?exact=Jace%2C+the+Mind+Sculptor&format=image&version=normal&set=wwk" alt="Jace, the Mind Sculptor" width="217">

- **Terminus:** One-mana miracle that tucks all creatures. Set up with [Brainstorm](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Brainstorm%22).
- **Counterbalance:** Reveals top card to counter matching MV spells. Without Top, relies on cantrips.
- **Jace, the Mind Sculptor:** Brainstorms every turn, bounces, threatens ultimate.
- **Entreat the Angels:** Miracle creates X 4/4 flying angels.

### Historical Timeline

**2012** (tier 1, ~15%)
Original Miracles with Top dominates. [Counterbalance](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Counterbalance%22) + Top is near-unbreakable.
- [Counterbalance](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Counterbalance%22) + Top lock
- [Terminus](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Terminus%22) as sweeper

**2017** (tier 2, ~4%)
Top banned April 2017. Players rebuild with [Brainstorm](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Brainstorm%22) as miracle enabler.
- Top banned
- Rebuilt with [Brainstorm](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Brainstorm%22)

**2019** (tier 2, ~3%)
Post-Top Miracles competitive but not dominant. Narset and planeswalkers strengthen shell.
- Narset added
- Planeswalker-heavy

**2023** (tier 3, ~0.5%)
Bowmasters weakens Jace and [Brainstorm](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Brainstorm%22) setup. Jeskai Control preferred.
- Bowmasters punishes [Brainstorm](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Brainstorm%22)/Jace

**2026** (tier 3, ~0.5%)
Tier 3 at 0.5%. Nostalgic but outclassed by Jeskai and Beanstalk Control.
- Outclassed by newer control decks

### Bans Impact

- **Sensei's Divining Top** (2017-04): Original Miracles with Top was the best deck for years. Top ban forced complete rebuild.

**Frequency of Change:** medium
**Change Notes:** After Top ban in 2017, rebuilt around [Brainstorm](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Brainstorm%22). [Counterbalance](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Counterbalance%22) without Top is less consistent. [Predict](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Predict%22) helps set up miracles.

---

## Variant Index

This section maps every known Legacy archetype name (~420 variants across 65 parent categories) to its parent archetype. Used by the AI to recognize deck names and understand relationships between variants.

### Delver / Tempo
**Description**: Cheap threats backed by free countermagic ([Force of Will](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Force+of+Will%22), [Daze](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Daze%22)) and mana denial ([Wasteland](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Wasteland%22)). The defining Legacy tempo shell.

| Variant | Colors | Status | Meta % | Notes |
|---------|--------|--------|--------|-------|
| Dimir Tempo | UB | tier_1 | 14.6% | Current dominant build. Bowmasters + Tamiyo + [Thoughtseize](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Thoughtseize%22). The deck to beat. |
| Izzet Delver | UR | tier_2 | 4.3% | Classic [Delver of Secrets](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Delver+of+Secrets%22) + [Lightning Bolt](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Lightning+Bolt%22) + [Murktide Regent](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Murktide+Regent%22). Was tier 1 in 2021-2022. |
| UR Tempo | UR | tier_2 | 4.3% | Same as Izzet Delver. MTGTop8 naming convention. |
| Sultai Tempo | UBG | tier_3 | 0.5% | BUG Delver variant with [Tarmogoyf](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Tarmogoyf%22)/[Barrowgoyf](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Barrowgoyf%22) + [Abrupt Decay](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Abrupt+Decay%22). Less popular post-DRS ban. |
| Sultai Delver | UBG | tier_3 | 0.5% | Same as Sultai Tempo. |
| BUG | UBG | tier_3 | 0.5% | Older name for Sultai Tempo/Delver. |
| BUG Midrange | UBG | tier_3 | 0.5% | Grindier BUG build with more planeswalkers and fewer Dazes. |
| Grixis Tempo | UBR | fringe | 0.2% | UBR shell combining Bowmasters + [Lightning Bolt](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Lightning+Bolt%22). Less focused than Dimir or Izzet. |
| Grixis Aggro | UBR | fringe | 0.1% | More aggressive Grixis variant. |
| Temur Tempo | URG | fringe | 0.1% | RUG Delver successor. [Tarmogoyf](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Tarmogoyf%22) + Bolt + cantrips. Was tier 1 pre-W6 ban. |
| Canadian Threshold | URG | historic | 0.0% | Original name for RUG Delver. Nimble Mongoose + [Lightning Bolt](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Lightning+Bolt%22) + [Stifle](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Stifle%22). |

| Esper Tempo | UWB | fringe | 0.1% | Rare UWB Delver build. Swords + [Thoughtseize](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Thoughtseize%22) + Force. |
| Dimir Aggro | UB | tier_2 | 1.0% | More aggressive Dimir build without Murktide, lower curve. |
| Dimir Flash | UB | fringe | 0.1% | Flash-speed threats, all instants. Brazen Borrower + Bowmasters. |
| Dimir Rogues | UB | fringe | 0.1% | Rogues tribal with mill synergies. |
| Mono Blue Tempo | U | fringe | 0.1% | Delver + all-blue for maximum [Force of Will](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Force+of+Will%22) consistency. |
| Simic Tempo | UG | fringe | 0.1% | [Tarmogoyf](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Tarmogoyf%22)/[Barrowgoyf](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Barrowgoyf%22) + green sideboard cards. |
| 4 Color Tempo | UBRG | fringe | 0.1% | Greedy 4-color Delver. Rare post-Astrolabe ban. |
| Delver (Other) | varies | fringe | 0.1% | Catch-all for unusual Delver builds. |

### Control
**Description**: Permission-based strategies that win through card advantage and inevitability. Heavy on counterspells, removal, and planeswalkers.

| Variant | Colors | Status | Meta % | Notes |
|---------|--------|--------|--------|-------|
| Beanstalk Control | UWRG | tier_2 | 2.3% | [Up the Beanstalk](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Up+the+Beanstalk%22) draws cards off 5+ MV spells ([Force of Will](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Force+of+Will%22), [Solitude](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Solitude%22), [Fury](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Fury%22)). Non-Yorion 60-card build. |
| Beanstalk Control (Yorion) | UWRG | tier_3 | 0.4% | 80-card Yorion companion version. More redundancy, less consistency. |
| Jeskai Control | UWR | tier_3 | 0.9% | Classic UWR control. Swords + Bolt + Force + planeswalkers. |
| UWx Control | UW+ | tier_3 | 1.0% | Broad category for UW-based control decks. MTGTop8 umbrella. |
| UW Miracles | UW | tier_3 | 0.5% | Post-Top ban Miracles. [Terminus](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Terminus%22) + [Counterbalance](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Counterbalance%22) without [Sensei's Divining Top](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Sensei%27s+Divining+Top%22). |

### Stoneblade
**Description**: [Stoneforge Mystic](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Stoneforge+Mystic%22) decks that tutor equipment ([Batterskull](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Batterskull%22), [Kaldra Compleat](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Kaldra+Compleat%22)) in a fair blue shell.

| Variant | Colors | Status | Meta % | Notes |
|---------|--------|--------|--------|-------|
| Stoneblade | UW+ | tier_3 | 2.0% | Generic Stoneblade. UW base with [Stoneforge Mystic](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Stoneforge+Mystic%22) + equipment. |
| UWx Stoneblade | UW+ | tier_3 | 1.0% | Same as Stoneblade, broader naming. |
| Jeskai Stoneblade | UWR | fringe | 0.3% | Adds [Lightning Bolt](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Lightning+Bolt%22) and [Pyroblast](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Pyroblast%22) from red. |
| Esper Stoneblade | UWB | fringe | 0.2% | Adds [Thoughtseize](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Thoughtseize%22), Bowmasters, and Vindicate from black. |
| Bant Stoneblade | UWG | fringe | 0.1% | Adds Uro, [Endurance](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Endurance%22), [Green Sun's Zenith](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Green+Sun%27s+Zenith%22) from green. |
| 4 Color Stoneblade | 4c | fringe | 0.1% | Greedy 4-color Stoneforge build. |
| Abzan Stoneblade | WBG | fringe | 0.1% | Non-blue Stoneforge with [Thoughtseize](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Thoughtseize%22) + green creatures. |
| Boros Stoneblade | WR | fringe | 0.1% | Stoneforge in RW shell. [Imperial Recruiter](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Imperial+Recruiter%22) + equipment. |
| Orzhov Stoneblade | WB | fringe | 0.1% | BW Stoneforge. [Thoughtseize](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Thoughtseize%22) + Vindicate + equipment. |
| Mono White Stoneblade | W | fringe | 0.1% | Mono-white Stoneforge. Maximum equipment focus. |

### Death and Taxes

### Food Chain
**Description**: [Food Chain](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Food+Chain%22) + [Misthollow Griffin](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Misthollow+Griffin%22) or [Eternal Scourge](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Eternal+Scourge%22) = infinite mana (creatures only). Win with [Walking Ballista](https://scryfall.com/search?q=!%22Walking+Ballista%22) or cast from exile creatures.

### Enchantress

| 4 Color Estrid | 4c | fringe | 0.0% | Estrid planeswalker in multi-color enchantress. |

### Jund
